dem don add 6 NIPP plant dem , 22 new substation for di power grid wey dey 6 years report .
Generation companies ( GenCos ) and 22 power substation wey dem build and dey operate between 2015 and now , don make improvement dey for di national eletcricity grid to di 5 , 800 megourtt wey be di highest peak energy wey dem record for March 2021 .
Dis dey according to di latest NIPP report on top power project execution since 2015 , wey Daily trust obtained from di Niger Delta power holding company ( NDPHC ) .
Di NIPP na di intervention vehicle warehouse wey di federal , state and local goment own for NDPHC .
For 2015 , di power grid don dey between 4 , 500 megourtts ( MW ) wey don bikom useful by di commissioning and utilisation of Geregu , Omotosho , Olorunshogo , Alaoji , calabar , Ihovbor NIPP GesCos
Dat one add nearly 1 , 000MW
Howeva , di grid continue to dey rise wit all - time peak electricity wey don reach 5 , 801 . 60MW as of March 2021 , according to di statistics wey we get from independent system operation ( ISO ) arm of di Transmission company of Nigeria .
( TCN )
NDPHC don start di NIPP intervention wit di first phase wey dey power generation .
E don begin dey build 10 power GenCos wey dem dey call ' The Big Ten' around gas - producing state dem wey include Ondo , Ogun , and Kogi states .
Howeva , work still dey go on dem till 2015
Dem lunch the second phase for 2015 to include intervention project , wey go focus on transmission , distribution , and energy wey dem don renew towards meeting NDPHC mandate for lighting di nation .
currently , dem bin dey six power GenCos wey dey produce about 3 , 400MW electricity for di national grid while di four oda GenCos dey ongoing .
Even among di four , some of im turbines don dey commission and dey operational since 2015 .
Explanation of di report show say di NIPP intervention for di transmission section wey dey di power sector value di chain , NDPHC don complete 22 substations wey bin dey compromise 10 units of 330 / 132 kilovolts ( KV ) level and 12 units of 132 / 33KV substations .
E don also complete 2 , 194 kilometres wey dey 330KV power transmission line and 887km wey dey 132KV transmission lines .
Dis infracstructure since 2015 , don add 5 , 590MVA energy supply capacity wey dey 330KV level and 3 , 793MVA wey dey 132KV level .
To promote energy wey dey clean and improve , di NIPP for di second phase don turn to major driver of di federal goment energy mix by 2030 wey dem dey call vision 30 - 30 - 30 wich seek energy wey go improve to at least 30 percent of di energy grid by 2030 .
While e don install 20 , 000 solar home systems for some northen states , di NIPP don dey deliver a huge part of the ongoing five million SHS to domot nationwide under di Economic Sustainability plan ( ESP ) .
Dia bin dey intervention for di gas sector wey go solve major challenge of di power plant wich be di availability of gas - to - power .
According to di oga patapata for NDPHC , Mr Chiedu Ugbo , for interview wey im get with Daily Trust , di company dey achieve dis tru di fuel and gas or public private partnership model .
E don create a department for dis to spearhead im gas pipeline and feed stock wey dey connect all di 10 NIPP GenCon .
wen dem tok power distribution , di report tok say di NIPP intervention bin don see di completion of ovr 360 NIPP injection substations wit a combined capacity wey reach 3 , 540 MW .
To complement dis substations , NDPHC don build about 2 , 600KM of 11KV power distribution lines and 4600KM of 33KM distribution lines wey dey supply electricity directly to transformer
Dia bin dey 296 appointed project wey dem don distribute , wich injection substations dey inside , 1924 of 33kv lines , 4600km of 11kv lines wit dem oda infastruction
NDPHC sef don increase im distribution capacity wit di installation of 25 , 900 completely self - protected ( CSP ) transformer wey dey across obodo , nah Mr Ugbo add dis one .
On top all dis achivement wey don help to improve di operation of national grid , di report highlight threat to di infastructure especially for di one wey dey di power distribution level .
Some of di wahala wey NDPHC dey see for dis distribution be say dem dey tif dia equipment and infrastructure , vandalism , and lack of cooperation from Distribution companies ( DisCos
Di oda nah community wahala wey dey regard land and Right of way ( ROIs ) , motor accident wey don damage some power infrastructure and rising insecurity wey dey facility areas , e start

Im howeva tok say despite dis , di sector neva reach dat kin viability , so di goment need to deepen di interventions tru NIPP .
On top all di tremendous milestone wey NIPP / NDPHC don achieve , dia bin major area of impediment wey dey full realizeation of di lofty idea wey di management of NDPHC championed .
Mr Olubiyo tok say di wahala dem dey face include delay in taking over projects by di DisCos wich dem suppose capture for dia capital Expenditure ( CAPEX )
Im continue im tok say nah di Nigerian Electricity Regulatory Commission ( NERC ) bin di inderance for di delay in di implementaion of di regulations of eligeable consumer
wit di kin huge power assets wey NIPP don provide , di Manufacturers Association of Nigeria ( MAN ) and oda dedicated power users fit decide to connect to di NIPP plants and facilities directly and dey enjoy uninterrupted power supply , but dis bin dey delay .
Anoda wahala wey NDPHC dey get nah funding , wich im think say di equity stakeholders suppose raise for more power sector projects .
Di leadearship of di power sector go need to address di low tariff wey dey NIPP plants and di low load ( Energy ) dispatch wey dey available units from TCN
Consumer dem dey look for more electricity , why energy from NIPP GenCos con dey restricted ?

unlike oda places , Ramadan season for Nigeria don unfortunately turn into a season wey dey get unnecessary controversy
Di controvercy don start from di arrival of di Ramadan crescent wey dey usher in di new month and di moon go waka commot to show e end .
di Ramadan peroid dey equally witness controversy ova ideological , jurisprudential or political stances wey some Ulama expressed for di course of dia Quranic trfseer sessions
ova many many years , dia bin don dey unnecessary controversy ova say wich charitable work better pass between make dem dey suponsor broadcast Quranic tafseer abi make dem dey do charitable mass feeding of di needy for Ramadan .
As e dey go for oda Muslim societies , Ramadan dey always inspire a phenomenal risefor individual and for societal spirituality for Nigeria wer plenty wealthy pipo dey sponsorlive or recorded broadcast for Quranic tafseer by different Ulama
Many oda pipo dey spend more on top charitable feeding of di poor .
Howeva , while almost , if no be all , who dey sponsor di broadcast tafseerb dey spend for di charitable feeding too , no be all wey dey spend for charitable feeding dey suponsor di broadcast of tafseer .
Ramadan period for northern Nigeria , television and radio stations dey make profit wit di sale of airtime for tafseer and oda religious lectures wey individual , firms and groups sponsor
from di kin number of sponsor broadcast of tafseer an dem oda religious lecture wey dey for like 10 radio stations for Kano , for example , one fit begin dey wonda weda dem dey do oda programme for Ramadam period .
E good say dem dey sponsor tafseer broadcast , especially for Ramadan , di amount wey dem dey spend for dis regard be like say im dey imbalance if we consider di kin hunger wey dey wire di needy
afta all , if dem get chance to choose , dem go certainly choose food hangout ova dat kin sponsored broadcast , as e don be say public tafseer session dey evriwia for Ramadan wey persin fit choose wich to attend .
Besides , di kin underlying dynamics and politics wey dey for sponsoring Ramadan tafseer broadcast , persin no fit rule out Riyaa , sectarian and even political interest wey be di main motives for di sponsor of tafseer and dem oda religious lectures .
Wetin dey interesting be say , while some sponsor dey compete for who go sponsor di broadcast of tafseer wey some prominent Ulama dey anchor , some of di Ulama dey sponsor dia own broadcast tafseer even if dem no see persin wey wan sponsor ; odas even dey beg for sponsor wey go sponsor dia programme .
Also , di content wey some tafseer and oda religious lectures dey feature get some serious flaws , to dey sponsor dis kin broadcast nah big misplacement of priority
anoda thing wey dey interesting be say , some dey sponsor di broadcast of Adhan ( Kiran sallah ) for inside city like Kano .
wia , thank you to sheer wey dey increase for Mosques , regular Adhan don dey reach evri corner
Anyway , Ikhlas bin di ogbonge yardstick way dey determine if weda charitable feeding and di sponsoring of Ramadan tafseer broadcast dey worthy or not , striking appropriate balance between di two go give better outkom .
Even though say Ramadan be di month of di Quran wey be say Muslims suppose dey commited in terms of reading , learning wetin im mean and to dey live dia lives accordingly
Di month nah di month of generous charity wey be say Muslims , particularly di ones wey dey wealthy suppose dey do charity work , especially mass feeding .
Howeva , while dat one com be di bottom line , wich explain why di controversy no dey necessary , di Liberal Musilims don over do am
capitalizing on top public frustration wey dey inside di hunger wey dey wire di society , dem dey kwesion weda di sponsoring of di broadcast Ramadan tafseer dey worthy or relevance for under dis kin condition wey we dey find ourselves .
As dem don pretend show empathy and concern , dey tok say di two charity work be di same and make pipo choose between dem .
Under di hard condition wey pipo dey , e no surprise to dey see many pipo , including di ones wey fit discern , fall for di propaganda wey dem no know e context , nah im be di raging face - off wey dey between di Liberal Muslims , for anoda side , dem bin wan undermine Islamic and moral values for di society by force , togada with di
Also , contrary to wetin dem claim , di Liberal Muslims no dey disturb by di kin wahala wey dey for di vulnerable , dis don explain why dem neva urge those wey dey spend huge resources on top oda things , no mater how worthless im be , make dem divert di resources to charitable course .
Dem neva urge dat di kin massive amounts of resources dia elite role spend on top say dey wan maintain dia big lifestyles suppose dey diverted for di feeding of di poor or to take give dem shelter
Instead , dia conscience go kom alive wen resources dey for only , say , Hajj , Umrah , Daourh

Di memories of Nigeria colo wey dey for black and white ( iii )
sometimes afta dat , and afta I don get like two popular strip wey dey for di now default news paper wey dem dey call The Democrat , I get my first four letters wey reject me from Mavel Comics , I gada myself remain a young man wey still get hope .
with di kin ups and downs wey dey for Nigeria , im still allow me get dream , to be artist wey dey work for a ogbonge culture company wey for anoda kontiri , anoda continent
Fast - forward to 20002 , one day as I dey sit down for di post office wey dey di centre of di city to drop off my latest art sample to Marvel Submission Editor , I no fit get bus
Plenty pipo dey use leg take waka , some gada for group , dem dey worry .
I dey weird out , waka go home , only to hear say raiot don start .
again , many pipo die for di riot , farmilies and friends tear apart as Christian dey beingn move to Kaduna South and Muslims begin move from Kaduna South to di North
My Kaduna , my Nigeria , don dey fall apart .
Di small consolation wey I get be some Christian friend wey stay for certain areas , like me , dem feel safe and no go anywia
So , as di violence dey intense for oda parts , I go dey play soccer for my street , dey exchange VHS tapes and bootlegs VCDs
Di idea to dey hate persin bikos of im religion or ethnic dey incredible for us .
But one teen , wey just move to our domot some years , nah im make me get encounter with intolerance .
if to say we be Muslims , playing soccer , dis new guy call us make we go attack di infidel wey dey live down di road .
we com look each oda jokingly , we dey confuse , afta wich we burst to laughter , we com tell say make im get out .
As if dat one no bad reach , my heartbreak for don worse as I see di apprearance of labels and slur from both of dem .
My perfect Kaduna don dey fall apart , and families and friends don dey part ways , no be say dem no love each oda but bikos say dat na di safest thing to do .
afta di wahala don end , I begin face university with cautious optimism .
literally , many old friend dey there , as Zaria no too far from Kaduna .
Many pipo dey get new friend , some dey till today , some don dey stronger
The best part be say , all dis friend dem weda new or old , no dey base on religion or ethnicity
Some of us wey notice know say , di Kaduna wey we know , love and don lose , neva really destroy .
E no fit go bikos say nah for our heart im reside , so e go hard to kil patapata
Afta all di almost 29 years wey I don spend as a journalist , show me things wey plenty pipo no fit experience for dia life .
I get front row seat to fight for , gbege attack , concerts by superstars dem , movies premieres and all kin generation - defining moments
I also get to dey interview for some big big newsmaker wey dey Nigeria , during moment wey dem get most chutzpah , or nothin at all .
Nah di Nigeria wey no get worrior wey no fit fight for social justice , virtue - signalers , outrage - peddlers , or cancel culture - purveyor .
Nah di Nigeria wey dey flawed , still dey remind me of my old Kaduna , even though di image different to each oda .
But bodi no fit take all of dem for too long .
On top of bed , I con look around my old room again , evrithin just dey as I leave am before im coronavirus lockdown .
I com smile to myself , nah from dat moment I begin to dey decide on di kin steps wey I go take .
I com twist di rubber band round di sack of fotos two times , com put am back for inside longbox .
Maybe one day I go look oda ones , di colour foto , wey carry more recent memories .
Maybe I no go do am .
One thing dey clear say : nah my mother , and father , and di kin relationship wey dem get or wey dem no get wit me , nah im make me di kin child wey I be .
Wetin I be to oda kids wey know me , also di kin man wey I be , to pipo wey know me .
But I find am as wahahla , and e dey relieve more for my sack of black and white fotos , I don realize say while my head guide di kin persin wey I be , nah my heart don dey keep me Nigerian all dis years .
42 Niger communities wey dey under Boko Haram dey control Senator Musa .
Di Senator wey dey represent Niger East for di National Assembly , Senator Mohammed Sani Musa , im tok say about 42 communities wey dey Niger State don fall under Boko Haram control .
Dem don showcase 5 , 000 villagers for di last three days .
Dis dey kom after Niger state governor , Sani Bello , don raise alarm say di insurgents don hoist dia flag for some communities .
Speaking on di ground of senate on Tuesday while dem dey move on a motion on di kilins wey dey apun for Shiroro , Muya and Rafi local goment areas for Niger state , Senator Musa tok say bandit and terrorist don kil ova 475 persins for Niger East between 2020 till date .
Di lawmakers don express im worry dat almost seven years now Niger East Senatorial Districts wey dey Niger Delta don dey under eviriday and dey sustain plenty deadly attack by heartless , venomous , hydraheaded Boko Haram terrorist .
Di result don dey total collapse wey dey di local economies of di affected victims , total collapse of educational system for di affected areas , famine don dey bikos of di collapse of agricultural activities , displacement wey be as a result of distortion of crisis prone areas , depopulation as a result of wanton death , wey dey among odas .
Im tok say di attack are taking places for di absence of di slightest hindrances , resistance of confrotation from authorities .
Dem don kidnap many and don seize dem wives from dem com forcefully attached dem to Boko Haram members .
Three military camps wey dey Allour , Bassa and Zagzaga for di two local goment area don get sack , di insurgents don kil some security personnel in di last one month of di renewed attack
I fit confirm am authoritatively say Boko Haram terrorist don mount dia flags for many places wey dem don capture like Kure , Alour and Magani
Dey don abandoned pipo wey dey dis wat - torn part of di states and leave dem make dem face dia wahala , make dem dey in agony wey no get end and dey deep inside poverty .
futhermore , for dis moment primary schools for Gwada , Kuta , Pandogari and Minna dem don carry dem do IDP camp as dem dey follow di sacking of almost 5600 villagers from dia ancestral homes in Shiroro , Rafi and Munya local goment area for di last few weeks by di armed rubber wey don raid di town and villages .
Wetin dis mean be say if dey fit attack without hindrance for Niger East Senatorial districts .
I no know how we wan take bikom safe for Abujan again .
Im tok say March 2021 to date some jaguda don kil more 25 gallant soldier dem , policemen and oda security personnel while 16 civillians die , and dem no fit account for many odas .
If dem no address dis threat drastically , di attack go continue and di danger wey day dat one be say e fit bikom wetin we no fit handle further to oda communities .
Wey bin farming communities and dem bin farmers , dem fit comot dia farm dis season and dis fit negatively affect food surficiency and economic diversification policy of di Federal Goment , im added .
My visit go Adamour state
Working wit di goment for any level don offer innovators like me di chance to dey bring more beta and transformation wey we ordinarily no fit do for our field
I strongly believe say di goment , as institution , be di greatest vehicle for systemic change and positive transformation wey persin no fit find anywia .
For dat , weneva I kom across opportunities to work wit dem goment bodi , weda local or nah for outside country , I dey always dey hapi bikos say e represent a great opportunity for me learn from and fit contribute to di civil service wey dey fields dat are exciting and dey transformative for pipo beyond wetin my
One of my recent visit of such nature nah to Adamour state , wey dey fascinating for me bikos of im diversity , resilience and outstanding potencial .
I begin dey work actively for Adamour state some years ago , wit di international organisation , OXFAM , on top a project wey dey in line wit European Union's support to food security and resilience for Nothen Nigeria were we deployed a mobile solution to integrating di agricultural value chain .
We don work wit field officers wey dey represent Fufore , Guyuk , Mubi South and Song local goment areas wey dey Adamour state to enhance agriculture and Agricbusiness practices wit tecnology .
Howeva , my return to Adamour state last year dey towards a grannder and dey get more exciting task .
E don involve a preposition to take work wit di state goment to transform di ministry of Entrepreneurship and Development and poverty Alliviation togeda wit di wealth creation Agency ( PAWECA ) wit di general aim of how to dey reduce poverty and dey sustainably dey improve prosperity for di teeming young pipo wey dey di state .
For some context , I dey very delighted to learn dat di state goment don establish di ministry of entrepreneurship and Development wey go help lay focus on entrepreneurship and to acquire technical skil .
E no exist untill di goment of Ahmadu Umar Fintiri administration com establish am , di ministry don bikom di key pillar of di administration strategies wey dey towards economic development of di state .
Di role of dis institution dey sailent as im supporse be for Adamour state , wit im fair share of youth unemployment , security and oda challenges .
Im dey , howeva , very very evident dat the Adamour state ministry of Entrepreneurship and development , togeda wit Poverty Alleviation and Wealth Creation Agency ( PAWECA ) , e fit dey adequately utilised for trasforming di local economy , boosting youth entrepreneurship and to dey reduce unemployment drastically for di state .
But as im be for most goment institutions , dis dey require discipline and dedicated effort to fit achieve dem
Typically , for wia dey exist , complex international organisational challenges don shackle di growth and efficiency of dis kin institutions .
For persin to understand dis conundrum , I tok to Adamour state's secretary to di state goment , Malam Bashiru Ahmed , who no dey only passionate about di issue but dey remarkably informed about local and global effort wey dey around am and as such uniquely position to help chat oury solving am
Im repeat Governor Fintiri commitment to take solve youth wey no get job and enhance di local economy by boosting entrepreneurship .
Malam Bashiru don express im idea and understanding wey dey around reforming and improving di capacity of ministries and agencies of goment , arguing dat di desire transformation only fit be possible if dem enhance di culture of innovation , embrace di use of technology , and if dem improve internal processeces and procedures so dat
Nah bikos of di challege wey most public and private institution dey seek to solve continue to dey generate demands wey only technologically savvy , innovation - driven , forward thinking , and efficient institution fit do .
In di course of di weeks to follow afta dis encounter , I also meet di Commissioner of di Ministry of Entrepreneurship and Youth Development , Ilya James and di head of Poverty Alliviation and Wealth Creation ( PAWECA ) Hajiya Aisha Bello , make dem examine wetin dem have and dia lay grounds for developing initiatives base on
we wan establish organisational culture wey dey efficient and fit give result and go equip di ministry and agency to bikom innovation - driven through di use of technology .
In a way wey dey demostrable and fit give result we go initiate human - centre design thinking among staff and optimaize internal processes to ensure quality service delivery
last last , we go offer tools wey go dey for di monioring and measuring of organaisational performance of di ministry agency .
Dis go go hand in hand for di already existing togada wit newly - hatched programs and campaings of di two institutions
Governor fintiri administration , by im sheer resolve and commitment wey dey towards capacity development ey dey in partnership wit various global and indeed local partner like di United Nation and Development Programme ( UNDP ) and di Nigerian Content Development Board ( NCDB ) , upgrading vocational and fabrication centres like di vocational
I dey quite inspired by di kin obsession wey Governor Fintiri get for local content participation policies wey dey all project and programme , wey dey evident for di goment derive for local content participation in di NEDC rapid response projects togeda wit bin di key galvaniser and pivot wey dey di North East Governor's forum .
As I land for Yola dis week , di state capital of Adamour , amidst all dis aspirations for di great Fombina , as dem dey call di religion historically , I dey beset wit a renewed melanchonly for di loss of one of di greatest sons of Adamour , and Nigeria ogbonge public servant and academic Dr . Mahmud Tukur , who for im life time don
We pray make Allah grant im great rewards , and make us fulfill im dream and aspiration for Nigeria as a whole .

Nigerians don vex as Governors don mull N408 per litre for fuel price .
Nigerians dem don express dia anger ova di proposal of di Nigeria goment Forum ( NGF ) committees on top fuel subsidy , to push for deregulation of di downstream .
for a virtual meeting wey apun for Wednesday , di committee wey di state governor of Kaduna Nasir El - Rufai chaired inside a report , recommended a Premium Motor Spirit ( PMS ) wey dem dey also call petrol price wey between N408 . 5 per litre and N380 per litre while dem dey call for immediate removal of fuel subsidy
El - Rufai tok say dem no fit sustain di current subsidy regime , and only smugglers dem and dem illegal markets dey benefit from am .
Im also tok say Nigeria no fit benefit from di recent production wey Petroleum Exporting Countries ( OPEC ) , which dem suppose keep di fuel price high , bikos of subsidies .
Nah between N70 billion and 210 bn dem estimate to be dey spend evri month for di price of gasoline to remain 165 per litre , dis dey below di cost price and di moni wey den give to di federation account go shrink to less dan 50bn per month or even zero if threats persist , im tok .
Di committee don recommend PMS pump price increment from di current N162per litre to N408 . 5 per litre
Reacting to dis on Thursday , Nigerians across di states don show dia anger on di governors .
ForAnambra state , a civil servant , Mr . Uzoma Okeke tok say di proposal dey unthinkable if we dey look di state of economy of the nation .
A driver wey im name be , Michael Okafor tok say im don dey struggle to buy petrol for N170 / litre inside di state .
Inside Jos for Plateau State , Malam Nura Alhassan wey be tailor , don express im disappointment on top di development .
If di proposal don turn reality , di poor inside dis kontiri go suffer plenty bikos say whateva figure dem don increase , nah ordinary Nigerian go feel am .
More pipo dem don react to dis inside Kaduna , Port Harcourt , Abeokuta , Jos and Kano .
For instance , inside Kano , Buhari Abba Rano , 36 , tok say Wit dis kin level of insecurity wey dey around Nigerian governors dem dey busy dey start fake projects dem and loitering around Abuja and overnight agitating for complete deregulation .
Dis don show say our crude oil don dey useless and dem no care about di dem lives of di common man .
Fatima Baba Kura tok im believe say dis price wey dem propose go kos set back for di kontiri to a worse state than wetin im don be .
Inside Lagos , many Nigerians dem don express shock ova di don already propose fuel price increment from di governors dem who suppose to dey defend dia pipo .
A student , Miss Onyekachi Emeka tok say di price increase go fit trigger increase inside transportation fare .
For inside Akwa Ibom , Abia and Edo states , di residents dem don corroborated di view of oda Nigerians dem as dem dey described di proposal as unfair to di Nigerian pipo dem who don already have enough of di inflation rate , high cost of food and fuel and di security situation wey don dey spoil .
Experts dem don tell FG say make im don discard proposal
Experts wey react to dis development don bin urge di federal goment make dem discard di governors dem proposal for di best interest of dem Nigerian .
Di pesin wey dey for in charge petrol industry , Siraju Oyewale tok say arbitrary fixing of fuel price dey diffirent to di principle of deregulation .
I get problem wit pipo wey dey sit down dey sit down dey fix prices for petrol .
Dat one no dey deregulation
Dat one still be price regulation .
Politicians dem , or even dem goment agencies wey dey fix prices dey different to di principle of deregulation .
Even though say im support deregulation , Oyewale tok say di price go rise above di current price but e no go reach N380 .
Oyewale also tok say Nigeria must to refine im crude oil for locally level to tackle di petrol import cost wey dey rise by NNPC .
An economic expert wey dey stay for Abuja , Samson Simon Galadima tok say selling petrol for price wey dey twice di current price go further exacerbate inflationary pressure , hence , impoverishing Nigerians dem even more as purchasing power don reduce .
Galadima tok say lasting solution to Nigeria's fuel price wey no stable go dey deeply diversified energy - mix bikos our overdependence on petrol no dey healthy .
President of di Independent Marketers Association of Nigeria ( IPMAN ) , Chinedu Okoronkwo tok say e dey wrong for di NGF to dey fix fuel price .
Im tok say full deregulation go encourage more local and foreign investors dem to invest inside di sector and grow di economy but dat di governor's proposal should not be honoured .
NNPC tok say nah only FG fit tell us how much to dey sell fuel
Di Nigerian National Petroleum Corporation ( NNPC ) don tok say e no go go wit di proposal by NGF dat make dem sell a litre of petrol for N380 .
Persin wey dey speak for NNPC Dr Kennie Obateru wey torchlight dis to Daily Trust on Thursday tok say as di fuel price be now , e don dbikom policy issue and nah only di federal goment fit direct di corporation to sell for a specific price .
We still dey wait for di conclusion of di meeting wey dey go on between di organised labour and the Federal Goment .
nah afta di outkom of di meeting we fit announce di price
NNPC don tok say di NGF only made a proposal wey fit be accepted or discarded by di federal goment .

Mohammed Buba Marwa ( Retd ) tok for Wednesday inside Abuja wen im host di acting Inspector General of Police , Alkali Baba Usman .
dis dey as im urge di police to hand over drugs wey dey no dey legal and make dem arrest suspects wey dey in connection wit drug trafficking to di NDLEA for prosecution as e no fall under Police jurisdiction .

within three months , we don seize ova 2 million kilogrammes of assorted drugs .

Di virtue of open grazing for inside Nigeria
as dem dey tok am for inside one popular adage , if you dey inside tunnel , na light wey you need , no be sound
light for end of turnnel on palava wey dey on top cattle husbandary don tay
Na true say population don increase ova di years , and plenty land don dey use for farming and infracstructure , but wetin analysis show be say for 20 million cattle dem and 200 million Nigerians , land go dtill dey plenty
To take start , Kano State wey be one of di place wey pipo plenty pass get about one million cattle and tranquility dey .
na 92 . 3m landmass Nigeria get , wit 70 . 8 ha wey dem dey use do agriculture but na only 34 million to 35 million dem don use since last year
bikos say we dey tok , make we look maize production
data wey dey available show say inside 2020 , na only 12m tonnes dem produce
research don touchlight say 86 % of cereal biomass na em be say na material wey human no dey consume dem take do am .
According to wetin FAO tok , 33 % of land wey dey dis world na em dem dey use for animal feeds while 30 % of di earth surface dey permanently under pature to dey support global intensive livestock producton
Ethiopia get 100 million hectares landmass wit 60 million cattle , e plenty three times pass Nigeria own wey dey under open grazing
Ethiopia be one of di economy for Africa wey dey grow fast fast wit livestock production wey cover 40 % of Agricultural output and e dey contribute 13 - 16 % to di total GDP
Cattle production dey face myraid of challenge dem wey dey associated wit husbandry , di misconduct of herder dem , climate change and local politics
For today world , technology be weapon of first choice wey fit help overkom plenty challenge dem wey dey face livestock production
Na about N10 trillion ( PAN ) di industry worth and na em big pass for Africa
Commercial and free - range rural poultry dey for al state wey dey give commercial poultry di all - important Federal character .
Di poultry revolution no just apun laidat , na goment policy make am apun , public - private sector partnership and di entrepreneurship spirit wey Nigerian get .
Na di same technology fit transform di cattle industry wey evribodi go benefit .

opposition wey dey kom from di herders , though na from di Fulani pipo e plenti pass , e kom still dey among di farmers wey no want make pastolist dem enjoy di benefit of di plan sef , dey spoil di reform effort
Distrust don plenti for Middle belt , place wey be say fight between farmers and herders too plenti bikos of land , even though peacemakin and effort wey di military dey take since 2018 don reduce di blood shed
Shortage don dey federal and state goment budget , small part na bikos of di economy wey spoil bikos of di pandemic , and bikos di kontri no get technical experts wey know how dem take dey manage ranch and grazin reserve
For many states , especially for North - West , di way wey criminal gang and group dem wey get arm dey grow dey spoil access to grazin reserves and e dey make pipo wey wan invest before no do am again
unless dey do somethin about am , dis kasala and oda ones fit delay or make e spoil di plan , wey go make di kontri dey helpless wen di fight between farmers and herders dey serious pass before own , wey fit kom turn fight between ethnic group , region and religion
To tackle dis kasala , e go dey important make Federal and State authority join hand make effort , wit donors and investors help .
First , make Abuja and oda states wey dey support am provide political leadership wey strong pass before , make dey kom increase dia communication wit public , so dem go fit spoil pipo doubt and wrong understanding of di plan
Dis one dey common pass for pastoralists dia side , wey go ask dem make dem change dia nomadic lifestlye wey dey wit dia pipo for centuries , wey still get serious doubt say di plan promise about pasture na lie .
But many farmers dey fear say dem go lose dia land give pipo wey dey produce livestock .
Many pipo for di middle Belt and oda states for di South still dey suspect di plan long - term goals , wey dem dey see as opportunity for herders and di Fulani people particularly
Wit di support from Abuja and oda partners , state goments go need find pipo wey go be expert , wey go know technical aspect of thins , especially pipo wey go dey manage di ranch and grazin reserve , dairy production and meat processin
Make Federal and State goment sef increase dia budget for di plan , release di fund quick and make dey kom create financial transparency to make sure say evrithin dey accounted for , to dey work wit donors and investors wey necessary
E dey important sef to dey deal wit insecurities wey dey rural area , to dey curb impunity and to dey kom rehabilitate communities wey di fight affect seriously for di states wey dey participate .
Authorities go need consider weather change mata join , make dem decide if herders from oda kontris sometimes go benefit from di plan sef
As some of dis step go take time , make di pipo wey dey plan am focus on how dem go fit bring result wey strong , wey pipo go fit see for small time
less dan two years from now , di kontri go hold general election
if di plan go survive di change of goment wey go follow , Politians go need bring proof wey clear say e get benefit ( Change dey certain , as president Buhari and many state governor dem no go fit compete again as dey don serve two term )
By di time wey champaign for election don dey hot for 2022 endin , di pipo wey dey back di plan suppose fit show some of di ranch wey dem build or di reserve wey dem repair , strong donor wey dem get and dia investors commitment and di first group of pipo wey dey don train to be professional for Livestock mamagement
Nothin for dis thin dey easy but di plan worth di effort
No be say e perfect , but e bring chance wey dey important , chance to change Nigeria livestock system wit strategy wey go address wetin both herders and small - scale farmers need .
About 70 percent pipo wey dey work for Nigeria dey get moni from Agriculture
To modernise di Livestock sector go boost di kontri prosperity and for di same time , na one big way to solve one of Nigeria kasala wey dangerous
As time dey reach for di 2023 election , both federal and state authority go need do quick so pipo go see wetin dem dey do , or else all dia work to create dis kind moment of opportunity go spoil .

5 years afta : why Nigeria no still see beans export
Nigeria hope to dey export dry cowpea ( beans ) to kontri dem wey dey European Union don spoil
Dis na bikos of di extension of di ban wey dey ground before on top di kontri dry beans by European Union wey go end by 2022
Di EU food safety authority don ban Nigeria beans for 2015 bikos he get like 0 . 3mg per kg to 4 . 6mg per kg Dichlorvos , one pesticide , wey be say di type wey suppose remain no suppose pass na 0 . 01mg per kg
Dey consider say Dichlorvos get poison wey fit kos diffuculty for breathin , diarrhoea , vomitin , convulsion , dizziness and oda sickness sef
experts tok say like many organophosphate ( OP ) insecticide , e get enzyme cholinesterase sef wey dey kos disruption of di nervous system and muscular system
some expert sef claim say some farmers and middlemen dey use Sniper , anoda chemical wey dey deadly use preserve dia beans
Independent investigation wey dis paper conduct last year show say most of di beans for di kontri dey perserved wit chemical wey dey dangerous to human health
One food scientist , Idowu Amusa , list di consequences wey dey di consumption of food wey dem use sniper and oda harmful chemical preserve wey include gastro - intestinal issues , brain and oda internal damage , blood poisonin , food poisonin and e fit kos death
Di EU don extend di ban from 2018 on importation of dry beans from Nigeria until June 2019 bikos of di pesticide wey dey always dey der
Nigeria Agricultural Quarantine Service ( NAQS ) , di kontri produce regulator , don assure di farmers and oda stakeholders before say di kontri dey work hard to ensure say dem lift di ban for 2021
One recent document from EU don announce extension of di ban , he tok say Nigeria no implement di Union food safety plan wey dem submit for 2018
wit di extension , beans wey dem produce for Nigeria no go fit enta any member kontri for European Union .
Na like dis e don be for five years
How e take start
For 2015 , dem reject some beans from Nigeria bikos of di Eu export regulations
One official for NAQS tell awa Agric Editor say as e reach Tin Can Island , di NAQS team go check di consignment and dey discover say some of di containers don dey turn power and dey reject am bikos of di chemical residue
We take awa own analysis from there , kom discover say aside from di pesticide residue wey dey , pest sef dey and na dem kos di powder form of di beans
He tok say di agency don dey carry out serious campaign to explain how and di reason for farmers and middlemen make dem dey preserve dia beans wit acceptable chemical level
Di official , wey no write hin name down , tok say aside from export wahala , to dey chop beans wey dey don too preserve dey dangerous to human and animal health .
Expert tok say Nigeria dey lose billions
One agric economist , Mr Segun Ayeni , tell Daily trust yesterday say Nigeria dey lose billions of naira sake of di ban wey dey kontri beans mata wey EU give dem for 2015 .
He tok say traders and goment no dey see moni from beans value chain bikos of di ban
He tok say all traders wey dey between , di warehouse pipo , di transporters and we , wey dey involve for di inspection and certification , dat aspect don dey broken down bikos e dey no fit generate any revenue for di value chain .
Pipo reaction dem
Di National president of All Farmers Association Nigeria ( AFAN ) , Architect Kabiru Ibrahim , as he react to di ban wey EU give dem , tok say he fit say he no dey connected wit di kontri noncomformity wit di Global Good Agricultural Practice Protocol
For di production , we need deploy good agricultural practice , and for di preservation , make we no use plenti volume of chemicals wey go dey leave residual content wey dem no go accept as wholesome foods for Europe
Dem no think di general ban for EU well bikos some farmers don already dey comply wit di GAP standard dem
He add say dem dey work wit some farmers to ensure say dey comply wit GAP
As di National president of AFAN , I be di Chairman of di National Technical Working Group on Global GAP for Nigeria wey dem inaugurate for 2017 by Di Minister of Agriculture and Rural Development dat time
He tok say various exporters , agribusiness groups , Ministry of Trade and Invesment , SON , NAFDAC , Quarantine Department go need work together , make dem act as one to make wetin we produce acceptable globally
Mr Idowu Amusa , one food scientist , don advice say make farmers dey grow only organic food and if na must make dem use pesticide on top dia farm , make dem use only pesticide brand and di dosage wey dem recommend
He tok say make dem dey allow time between wen dey use di pesticide and wen dey use food produce , and if he possible , make dem label di food product wit information wey dey relevant about di food cultivation for consumers
I love Nigeria , things go change , still remain di same evritime .

He no dey answer pipo wey dey attack or abuse di kind person wey hin be , upon say he get plenti agbero and wobe pikin under hin control .
New tecnology , wetin dem find wey fit reduce yawa wey dey farm labor .
For many farmers for Nigeria , improved technology dem wey go make farming easy and smooth , wey no dey before , especially for di young pipo , na serious challenge
Upon say na 16 agriculral Institutes and four conventional University dey di kontri , research and development don dey veri slow
Recently , Daily trust speak wit Professor Ishiyaku Mohammed , di executive director for di Institute for Agricultural research ( IAR ) , Ahmadu Bello University , Zaria and he
explain some of di new research and technology wey di Institute develop for farmers
Recent variety wey dem release
For di most recent situation , na like 28 different Sorghum dem release
Na like di same number dem release for groundnut sef
Di institute release like 20 variety for cowpea sef and 66 different maize variety , afta , 13 different variety of cotton
Dey get economic attributes wey dey veri important wey go increase di income of farmers and provide different product for utilisation , whether na as food , fiber , or for makin textile products for cotton case , or even if na to provide oil groundnut and cotton case .
Di IAR don wake di concience of farmers generally make dem know say modern technologies dey
awa scientists dem don dey create machine and tool wey we go fit use reduce drudgery for some years now
For example , planter and tractors don dey wey dem fit use hand hold
And we don dey find way wey we go use perfect rollin weeders bikos pipo don dey complain say farmers dey use hoe wey dem dey use hand hold comot weed
Na so we answer dem wit di mechanical weeder wey we dey develop
we get thresher dem for maize , beans , sorghum and groundnut
Dryers dey important wen you produce crop wen rain still dey fall , so you need find place wia you go fit dry dem
hin tok say dryin sef dey important if you wan store product like tomato
somethin new for ginger seed
He kom continue tok say IAR sef enta one area for science wey just dey emerge wey dem call biotechnology
awa scientists don dey develop wetin dem go use propagate crops fast
For example , we get order make we for micro - propagate ginger .
Na how your plantin material plenti reach go determine di ginger production , di plantin material dem dey veri expensive , na hin make awa scientist dem develop way wey be say you fit develop like 1 to 2 inches of ginger piece inside bottle
You fit produce more dan 200 plantlets wey dem fit grow for field
Right now , we dey receive order from some farmer wey dey find am .
We dey do am for sugarcane sef
Dis technique dey help to propagate disease - free crop , sometimes , plantin materials fit don get disease
Na as your plant reach , na hin di disease sef dey propagate for odas
But dis technique dey try purify material make dem dey disease - free
Na Tissue Cultural Technique dey call am , na der dem dey plant for bottle , make e for proliferate
Each plantet fit give rise to plenti plantet now etc .
New technology for bio - fertiliser , Irrigation
Technology as we develop am dey go through two stage
Di first stage dey scientific
For this part , scientist dem go don dey sure say dis technique get di kind technology or tool wey dem go fit use solve di kasala , afta , di farmers go test am diasef .
Den , based on farmers opinion , dem fit still propagate am
So , for di area crop variety wey i don dey count give you for di last few years now , we don release variety of cowpea wey dey insect - resistant .
Na SAMPEA20T dem call maize own ; na di same year wey we release six different maize wey get potential to yield 6 - 8 tonne per hectare and for 2020 den .
Dem release three types for improved sorghum ( sweet sorghum ) , wit anoda six type of maize
For dis recent time , na wetin we release be dat
We wan release one technology for bio - fertiliser , na capsule wey get of some kind material , wey kom still get some kind microorganism wey dey useful as e be say dem fit help fix nitrogen , wey go benefit how plants take dey grow and develop as dem add fertilizer sef
He tok say we don develop develop technique for irrigation wey we improve so e go dey reduce how farmers take dey waste water .
One rule wey Journalists dey use na to use short sentence instead of long one if e go work .
Di Guild at 60 , inspirin di livin , honorin di dead
Wey Lanre Idowu write .
Sixty years ago , on Saturday , May 20 , 1961 , dem born Di Nigerian Guide of Editors , Pikin wey get great hope for di old National Press Club wey dey Abibu Oki for di heart of Lagos den
Dem name am Di Guild of Nigerian Editors
Dey don sideline di editors well from di Nigerian Union of Jornalists wey don dey exist like six years before Guild , bikos dem bi management staff , dey no fit trust dem make dem represent di interest of di rank and file journalists
As answer for di reverse discrimination wey NUJ dey do , dia need to make Professional Guidance , make dey kom stil protect dia interest for di socio - economic development wey dey unfold for the early days of nigeria wey dey independent , di Guild emerge make dem fit occupy middle ground of professional managers wey dey strategic between owner and di general rank of journalist dem
Lateef Jakande ( 1929 - 2021 ) for Nigerian Tribune be di first foundin president
hin Cabinet get pipo like Babatunde Jones ( 1925 - 2008 ) of Di Daily times as Vice president , Abiodun Aloba ( 1921 - 2001 ) of mornin Post as di Secretary and Nelson Ottah of Di Drum as vice Secretary
Dem establish Di Guild make dem use advance di interest of di profession , make e deepen editors dem relationship wit public , from media , goment , association wey dey professional and di one for trade and oda groups wey dey civil society
Na make e for be proactive agent for development , wey go dey expect kasala , dey tackle am and make e clarify issues before e too serious .
Dey test di promise of hin birth soon for di crisis wey start for di early time of di First Republic
some editor kom be di casualty of di cat - and - mouse politics for dat era
Jakande go court wit Chief Obafemi Awolowo for Treasonable Felony and dey jail am for 1963
Dat same year dem appoint Jose as managing Director for Daily times , he no fit be executive again for Di Guild again technically as e be say na only defacto editor dey executive position
Dat time sef , Aloba dey fight for hin job as e be say dem dey probe di Post bikos of dia finance
As di leaders of di Guild don get challenge for different levels , Di guild soon lose dia way , dey no know right or wrong thin again
Di Guild be wan change dia name so dem go fit accomodate electronic media , e kom add for dia identity kasala for years later
Di Guild continue under military rule , 1966 - 1979 , dey continue dey play active role for press freedom stuggle , dey kom enhance di respect wey dey for journalists and journalism
Sake of say dia members dey increase , and dem introduce different job title dem , di Guild don continue to dey struggle on top di question of who dem fit call editor .
Dis issue dey di crisis wey dem table for Minna convention for 1982
As di Guild affairs dey sttuggle wit partisan political interest wey dey kom from Geopolitical and sectional interest wey dey creep , di Guild no work for six years before dey kom start am back for 1988 .
Di membership question kom back for 2008 and 2017
Dey neva stop .
In nine days , Nigeria editors go meet for Kano to elect new team wey go dey lead dia dem , especially for dia member issue and moni mata wey dey neva resolve
Sake of di major development for di industry ,
For now , he dey proper to congratulate di industry say dey try wella to make di Guild still dey relevant till now .
Tomorrow , di Guild na major part for di industry effort to honour di memory of nine media leader wey die last year
Di newspaper proprietors association of Nigeria , di broadcastin association of Nigeria , di Nigerian Guild of editors , di Nigerian union of journalists go celebrate Alhaji Lateef Jakande togeda , foundin president of NPAN , NGE , Prince Tony Momoh , former NGE president , Mr John Egbuna , former director general for FRCN , Mr Eddie Aderinokun , former editor for morningg Post , Mr Sam Nda - Isaiah , Chairman wey depart for Leadership newspaper , Chiel Gbolabo Ogunsanwo , former editor for Sunday times , Mr Bisi Lawrence ,
former general manager for Lagos State broadcasting Corporation , Malam Wada Maida , former president for di Guild and Chairman for News Agency Of Nigeria , and Malam Ismail Isa , former president and life Patron of NPAN for one aftanoon wey dem dey give tribute for Lagos , honour pipo wey don dia , dey kom still inspire di pipo dey alive
Hapi diamond anniversary to di Nigeria Guild of editors
We need more quality interventiom programme wey go maintain di relevance of media as pipo wey dey shape and guide awa public morality
Idowu na editor in chief for media review and di trustee wey dey supervise di Diamond Award for Media Excellence ( DAME )
Aithough he get moni , he no still dey hapi .

To tame Nigeria oil spillage and gas flarin scourge
E kom from Jerome Mario - Utami
Di recent news report say Okordia - Rumekpe 14 - inch crude truck line wey Shell Petroleum Development Company ( SPDC ) dey operate discharge 213 barrel crude oil for Ikarama community for Bayelsa don reach awa side say though Nigeria wey been dey proud say dey be giant of Africa and di black kontri wey get pipo pass for di world stil dey get plenti third world kasala
As dem dey clarify say na like 1 . 34 hectare land dem pollute wit di leakage wey rupture for di pipeline follow , SPDC confirm say dey finish di investigation of di incident , dey tok say out of 213 of SPDC bonny light crude leak , na like 110 barrel dem see recover for di recovery exercise wey dem dey do for di site , e kom remain 109 . 12 barrel of di volume wey spill .
Admittedly , wetin Dutch oil giant claim na fact wey dem fit verify but e fit no be di only explanation
Notwitstandin dia clarification , reasons dey wey qualify dis kind apunin for Nigeria oil and gas industry as reality wey dey suppose analyse generally
Make we start wit reality
Aside from di awareness say spillage dey happen , communal right for environment wey clean and access for clean water supply na hin dey don violate for dat kind case , wit dia admission , dey don abandon thousands of site wey dey don pollute for di region , wey dem nid identify and study for detail as dey compensate di community wey e affect well for dia loss wella , dis lastest spill apun weeks afta one wey resemble am for one pipeline facility wey rupture wey one International Oil company wey dey operate for Niger Delta
dey manage , wey dem report say destroy Benikrukru and commuinty wey dey around am for Warri South - west local goment Area for Delta state .
And anoda one for early momo on Sunday , March 14 , 2021 for Polubobu / Opuama , Warri North local Goment Area for di state , go fit settle .
Dis kind big scale set of spillage also include but e no dey limited to ; di big spillage wey dey history for place like Ogini land , Rivers State and Erovie community for Ozoro , Isoko North Local Goment for Delta state for 1990s , di two for Nigeria south south zone and negative impact still dey der .
Shey na di only explanation / example dem be dis ?
Di answer na ogbonge
no , as oda ones dey
Oda critical reason / concern dem why we suppose see di situation as crisis .
Di first and veri important na di inability of Nigeria and hin pipo to appreciate and treat activity wey relate to crude oil spillage and environment pollution wey dey kom from exploration / crude oil production as national calamity
Di second na di stunnin conciousness wey gas flarin / environment degradation dey apun bikos of activities wey dey related to crude oil prospectin / production for di kontri dey under - reported .
Dis second concern dey kom from one recent comment , wey be say from media report na from di Director - General , National Oil Spill Detection and Response Agency ( NOSDRA ) , Idris Musa , wey tok say wetin hin agency find show say average of five oil spills na hin Nigeria dey record evriday .
Musa , wey follow journalists tok for Abuja , tok say for 2018 , we get 600 oil spill incident and for 2019 , we get about 700 oil spill - impacted site actross di kontri .
Dis comment wey dey open brain dey more important for wetin we dey discourse if pesin remember say Nigeria accordin to report don get about 139 place wey gas don flare across Niger Delta both for di oil fields wey dey water and di one wey no dey , wer gas wey dey flare dey reach 11 % of evrithin wey dem dey produce .
Pass anything , na di question dem wey e bring kom mind be ; wetin dey stop di development of petroleum sector and Niger Delta region
Shey Legislative work no dey ?
Why dis kind legislative framework no dey provide strong source of solution for pipo and community wey oil exploration and production affect badly for coastal comminity dem ?
If dis framework dey , why e no dey work or make dem do am ?
Shey di framework get evrithin like legal solution for di issues of violations wey relate to oil ?
Why di nation neva learn serious lesson from Dutch goment wia all di pipo wey dey operate must restore wia dem dey operate back to how dey meet am ?
Regardless of wetin oda pipo tok , di truth be say if all of us get am for mind to develop policy wey go bring prosperity for oil and gas sector , while we go still save di pipo for di region , we ready to find di strategic triangles wey hold di key to success for hand .
Apart from di fact say success need make dem analyse am wit care , of di different kind of knowledge wey dem need to make innovation possible , e don necessary for di nation make dem hold di middle ground since both di ministry and sector don dey manifest signs for long time now say dem go be institution wey no get potential wey strong .
And as we know , any organization , whether private or public wey no gree search for hin potential , hin survival na by chance .
For dis level , if we luk di operational template of di ministry , and how dey don know say di up , mid and down stream players of di petroleum industry say dem no dey follow rules , e no go dey wrong make pesin conclude say dem fit divide di serious reasons wey dey kos Crude oil spillage / gas flarin to ; regulatory framework wey plenti wey no dey work , oil and gas exploration and production for Nigeria dey ; federal goment failure to make di kontri refineries dey work to dia full capacity back ; petroleum
ministry inability to make International Oil Companies dey follow di international best practices as e relate to di environment wey dem dey work ; Di last one , clear responsibility / work details wey no dey and action plans for agencies and parastatals wey dey function under di ministry .
Di failures dem wey dey up get direct consequence , na bad influence for di sector , di ministry and di region .
To take explain dis points , make we use di first challenge start , e dey important to dey tok about di law dem wey regulate crude oil exploration and oil production issue wey plenti law dey regulate but too dey weak and di Acts wey dey law wey no dey just complicate how e dey work , but e don too old as time don dey change , e dey create corner corner way for pipo wey dey operate for der especially the International Oil Companies ( IOC ) make dem fit use exploit both di goment and
host communities .
some of dis laws / acts wey we dey tok about don dey since 1960 but dey no dey achieve dia purpose wey Di Petroleum Act of 1969 , Di Harmful Waste ( Special Criminal Positions etc ) , Act 1988 , Mineral Oil Safety Regulation 1963 , Petroleum ( Drillin and Production ) Regulation 1969 dey but no be oly dis one dem .
( Subsidiary Legislation to Petroleum Act ) and di off - shore Oil Revenue ( Registration of Grants ) Acts 1971 among odas .
As dey no mind di number , concept , provision and definition dem , dis law dem no dey useful again , dey don old to di extent say dem dey give pipo wey dey work for di sector corner corner to dey chop both di goment and host community dem .
Utomi na di Programme Coordinator ( Media and Policy ) , Social and Econnomic Justice Advocacy ( SEJA ) , Lagos .

SEC ban CMO wey dey no register from operation May 31
Di Securities and Exchange Commission ( SEC ) tok say dem go stop Capital Market Operators ( CMOs ) operation wey neva renew dia registration for May 31
Di commission tok am for one circular wey di management sign on Monday for Abuja
Di commission tok say any CMO wey no renew dia registration before late fillin expire for May 31 no go fit operate for capital market .
Bikos of wetin dey apun , di commission tok say to dey fill di renewal of registration late go dey between May 1 to May 30
E tok say di CMOs need complete renewal process on or before April 30 .
Di commission note say dem go publish di name of di CMOs wey renew dia registration of SEC website and national newspapers dem .
E kom add say dem go declare di name of CMOs wey dey eligible give relevant security exchange and Trade Associations .
Di News Agency of Nigeria ( NAN ) report say SEC for March don share circular give general public and di CMOs for di periodic renewal of registration by di operator wey dey wan introduce again

Pipo wey dey operate for Edo State Police command don arrest one man wey hin name na Igboje Victor , bikos dem think say he get hand for di kilin of hin cousin brother wen two rival cult dey fight .
Igboje dey among di 54 suspect wey Edo state Police Commissioner parade , Phillips Aliyu Ogbadu , say dem dey various crime for di state .
As per wetin di Comissioner tok , dey arrest di suspect for armed robbery , kidnappin , murder , cultism , rape and oda tins .
Dey later know say di incident apun for Sabogida - Ora Opuje community for Owan west local goment for Edo state
I dey innocent
For one interview wit Daily trust , Igboje deny say he get hand for di kilin
I no get hand for my brother death but dem arrest me bikos I be Eiye cult group member while my late brother dey Aiye group .
For awa community , we been dey sell Igbo take make moni , but Aiye group use di drug business use police arrest Eiye members .
He tok say di leader of di two group plan to meet dat night solve di gbege
He kom later add say , For di night of di meeting , Aiye members set trap for dem , dey kom shot Eiye members as dem dey go di meetin venue , dey kil one of dem wey dey later carry go mortuary .
Di pesin wey die brother na soldier , he say make dey go bury am bikos of hin mama .
Afta di burial , I go di neighbourin community go buy food but wen I kom back , I hear say Eiye boys don go attack one Aiye guy and di guy na my cousin , he die bikos of di injury wey hin get
He tok say he no dey for di group wey attack hin brother , he add say na bikos dem dey different group make dem tok say na hin kil am
And police kom arrest me wit di rest
I no even dey der wen dey attack my brother
He tok say : I no kil my brother
Di commissioner of police kom tok say , dem go go court if dey don finish dia investigation
Economy kasala for Nigeria don worse as plenti food item don double dia price for di weekend and pipo wey dey bake sef join dem as dey add 30 % for evritin wey dem dey use flour do .
Economy kasala dey plenti as bakers increase bread and biscuit wit 30 %
Di kontri economy wey hard don show face for anoda mata as di Association of Masters Bakers and Caterers of Nigeria ( AMBCN ) don tell dia members say make dem increase bread , biscuit and any oda tin wey dem dey bake price wit 30 percent bikos of di cost of production wey don high .
Bread and biscuit na food wey common for plenti house for Nigeria , and before di association announce wetin dem tok , plenti pipo for di kontri don dey complain bikos of how tins cost .
For di National Executive Council ( NEC ) meeting wey di association do for Abuja recently , dia members dey complain about how tins cost and dey gree say make dem increase di price of wetin dem dey sell .
AMBCN national president , Mansur Umar , tok say di price wey dem change na bikos of di way wey cost of production take increase suddenly and how sugar , butter , yeast and flour moni sef increase
As dem dey commend federal goment say dey revive di cassava flour programme , di association dey complain bad bad about regular flour price wey just increase anyhow since di last six month , wey be say one flour truck no reach 6 million before kom be 9 million now .
He tok say ; afta we consider di bakin / ingredient and material price wey don too increase , sake of say make dis awa noble work wey dey bleed fit survive , di association conclude say make we just increase awa price wit 30 percent
Di association sef conclude say dem go ask federal goment make dem reverse di tariff regime wey National Agency for Food Administration and Control ( NAFDAC ) force dem dey pay and make only NAFDAC dey steamline bakers regulation .
Dia national secretary , Jude Okafor wey tok sef say he dey hope say feredal goment do wetin dey want so dem go fit avoid di moni wey dey wan increase .

National Drug Law Enforcement Agency Chairman , Buba Marwa , tok say NDLEA dey investigate N30bn slush fund wey dem feel say na moni for drugs .
He tok am for Abuja on Monday mornin wen hin give 45 officers wey dey work well commendation letter and best performing command award for March and April , 2021 .
He tok say di strong action wey di agency dey take no go stop until all di street , community , town and city wey dey di kontri no get drugs wey dey illegal again
He tok say : As we continue to dey fight how dem dey use illegal drugs for outside , awa leaders for di agency go dey find how dem go maintain di situation .
Na di reaseon why we don make awa Directorate of asset and Finanacial Investigations , go make sure say dem collect all di moni and property wey get link wit drug traffickin , wey lead dem go meet di pipo dem and final order to forfeit property and moni wey worth plenti billion naira wey get link wit di pipo wey dey traffick di drugs and dia baron dem .
Marwa tok say di strength wey di agency dey use target drug cartel don make dem fit seize different illegal drug wey reach 2 , 050 , 766 . 33kg , moni wey reach N90bn and dey don arrest 2 , 175 pipo wey dey carry di drug .
He emphasize on top di fact say e dey important make di criminals dem no go fit collect any moni wey dem get from dia drugs dey go still kom go jail .
kidnappin mata for Zaria and whole kontri don dey worse .
Vigilante arrest 2 kidnappers for Zaria
Daily trust tok say vigilante don arrest two pipo wey dem suspect say be kidnapper for one ghetto area for Zaria , Kaduna State .
Di incident apun around 10 on Sunday wen some kidnappers enta di place wit force say dey wan kidnap pipo wey dey stay for der but local vigilante face dem .
One pesin wey dey stay der wey no wan tok hin name , tok say di kidnappers dey shoot anyhow to make pipo fear but di vigilante face dem wit dia gun before police kom later .
Daily trust later find out say some of di kidnappers dem kidnap four pipo wey dey der as some youth injure diasef for wen e apun , di kidnappin last for about two hours .
Kaduna State Police Command Spokeman ASP Muhammad Jalige tok say dem dey interrogate di two pipo wey dem arrest and police dey find di oda ones wey run .
IPOB leader don threaten pipo say hin go dey kil pipo wey no reason wit am
IPOB Emma Powerful don threaten pipo say he go spill blood .
Emma Powerful wey be media and publicity secretary for IPOB threat to dey kil any Igbo pesin wey no follow hin warning don dey too serious , and dey no suppose ignore am except say we no get goment , wer small small fascist like Mr Emma Powerful as he call himsef go dey tok say hin go dey drag pipo kom out , dey send dem go meet Baba God as he tok bikos dey no follow am or hin organization .
Di mouth wey hin dey run no be play ; as e be say di kasala for Nigeria South - east show say na plan dey plan am .
As he no understand how simple Igbo leadership dey be , wey be say dia leader na Onye - oje ozi or servant of hin pipo , wey make di pipo agree wit am afta he don consult plenti pipo , Emma Powerful wey prefer one thug title , Onye - ike , wey be say na to dey force dem , make dem fear am and now he dey threaten to kil di same Ndigbo wey he say he dey fight for .
For man wey be say he no dey tolarate , wey be say to kil pipo take push hin cause no be kasala , di question be say who go wan stay tru tru for Cave Republic wey be say na thug dey run am
Di Biafra wey pipo know for history no be Ndigbo choice ; Na di only choice wey dem force Ndigbo do be dat for dat time , wey dem face bravely wit plenti courage and sacrifice so dem go fit defend and uphold
Biafra no too oppose authority reach how dey try make di pipo right dey valid , no be say make dem just exist , but na to live wit dignity .
Di Biafra wey dey history na like safety precaution for all Igbo pipo wey suppose don too suffer dat time fit kom , place wey dey fit stay safely .
Di declaration and di struggle of di old Biafra no be show or avenue to make moni wey di pipo wey dey lead am dey do pass now .
Before dem declare Biafra for 1967 , Eastern Consultative assembly , one group wey dey represent , still dey advice for all di opinion wey pipo get for east , bikos of wetin dey apun gree say make dem make di declaration wit dia authority .
Na di reason wey make di whole Ndigbo and oda tribe wey no be Igbo , wey sacrifice , wey dem no fit forget gree protect di republic wey still small
As di war dey end sef , wey Biafra don fall , wey evribodi don settle , Ndigbo go back go protect Nigeria , wit clean mind , strong determination and courage , so e go fit work ,
Di context of new Nigeria kasala and disagreement for dia point of view wey dey deep na bikos of one neo - capitalist state wey dey go backward , and di chain of di productive forces , wey dem chain , wey no fit produce di material of hin existence again .
As di new Nigeria kasala dey grow , wey e no dey progress and e slow , di simple tins like tribe , culture and religion dey struggle to preserve , express and recreate diasef .
ova - all , e dey easy to carry retirement flag , wen dey no understand how socio - economic infrastructure dey important if dey wan build kontri wey go survive .
South Sudan wey be Africa last born still dey breastfeed as dia condition now worse pass dia former condition .
Notin show say Biafra current leader wey like to dey make noise know anythin about how dem dey build or create kontri
Even if dem dey independent , to built state no dey di real deal , to dey command pipo witout respect , make di fascist leaders like Emma Powerful wey dey threaten to kil pipo don show already .
Ndigbo too posh to get leaders wey be thug and tout , wey no understand say Igbo political culture and framework na to dey consult elders .
Mr Nnamdi Kanu wey been dey command dem , no know any village for Igboland apart from hin own , dey claim to be dia leader like say na hin own , pipo wey be say he no know how dem dey live except for di moni wey hin dey send give dem from abroad .
Mr Emma """" di Powerful """" wey be dia media and publicity secretary don use hin arrogance and petty fascist inpunity spoil Igbo basic framework wey be say na to dey consult pipo and to dey agree for somethin generally before dey do am .
Na only organisation wey thug full dey threaten to destroy pipo wey no gree wit am .
But dis new threat wey Mr Emma """" de Powerful """" issue say he go send pipo go meet dia forefathers sake of say dem no follow am , don too much .
Sake of dat one reason , dey suppose find way restrict hin and hin pipo to avoid kasala

E for don be like di great dream logic of di marine wey plant di America flag for Okinawa for 1945

I go dey imagine say I be like dem and den if I reach house afta di ceremony , as my mind dey sweet me bikos of freedom and di blank canvass put before my veri own means .
I go go bed , go nirvana , go wait for morning so I go fit wake for mornin , go work .
E don reach sixty years since dat time
Even though say na only 30 years I be , I don live for di bad dream of Nigeria history for all di year one by one for dis sixty year journey , I don feel evri disappointment and evri sorrow wey pesin fit feel bikos say dia kontri fail .
E don reach sixty years now wey all my dream leave , some die , bikos ravishin drought wey follow dis land wey get plenti water .
Odas don fly comot
wetin do us ?
I remember one artwork wey dey tok about sometin like """" Age of Discovery """" for Internet wey I see .
Inside , one man stand ova anoda man wey sidan for hammock wit power .
Dis suppose Amerigo Vespucci representation as he dey wake America continent of dat time make dem join mankind league as di last continent .
Na me and my brodas dey do house work for holiday wen we dey grow up .
Me sef remember wen I dey pretend say I go sleep back afta Subh so I no go do my house work and my brodas go kom vex wake me , make I no cheat dem .
Unlike America , dey don know Africa since beginnin of time , Indeed , na she first wake , she wake di rest sef but na she dem no know pass for di family , maybe bikos she go sleep back wen her siblins go dey work take discover fire and wheel .
Pipo like Joseph been call her Dark Continent
Since den , Africa no get any popular culture wey pipo know kom still accept apart from bloody , rooten and poor mindset wey reach to make one teenage band wey kom from America from di 80s feel say na dia moral duty to kos rain wey go stop di drought wey wan carry dem go by force .
Odawise she go die
E no dey ancient pass dat one , wetin she need na rain , nature , di same tin wey dia ancient forefathers sef need dat time .
Shey na wetin apun be dat ?
Shey we sneak go bed back , afta we wake di oda pipo for we world
And shey we go sleep back afta dey wake us di second time ?
Wu go know say Africa , togeda wit Nigeria go spoil so tey , dem go dey wait make some teenager wey no sure say dem no dia right from left dey give dem charity .
No be me
Shey Conrad correct ?
Shey na my duty to dey tok truth sake of say I dey honest , to wetin hin think say my pipo dey do
Shey make I fly go out like di rest of my dream ?
Maybe make I do am .
How we take reach der ?
We enta one car wey get engine , di sound good and e dey sleek , e kom life like Noah Ark as we dey go for 1960
We suppose dey rocket ship dey go Mars , instead na inside mud we sink put , for one Jalopy wey hin engine no good .
Before awa eye wey don dey gnash , di heart of darkness kom be my home , and my home kom be """" di oda world , """" di opposite of civilisation , place wia be say tin wey no reach man level dey yeye man intelligence wey dem dey use boast and dia grace .
I don resist Conrad for long time now and di sun don dey set , I don tire to dey fight
I dey ready to surrender , my situation wan resemble di of Chief Joseph of Nez Perce native America wen dey subdue am
I don read hin sermon for hin pipo afta he surrender somewia and I no fit stop myself as I dey tok am
Dey kil awa chiefs dem
Lookin glass don die .
Toohoolhoolzote don die
All di old men don die
Na di young men tok say , Yes or No
Di pesin wey lead di young men ( Olikut ) don die
E cold and we no get blanket
Cold dey catch di small pikin dem die
My pipo , some of dem don run go hill , and dey no get food and blanket .
Nobodi know wia dem dey , maybe cold wan catch dem die
I want get time look for my pikin dem and see how many of dem wey I fit find
Maybe I go find dem among pipo wey die
Hear wetin I dey tok , my chiefs !
I don tire
My heart no well , e no hapi join
From wer di sun dey , I no go fight again foreva
I don decide for my mind say I go surrender , follow wetin my enemy tok
I don decide to follow awa dreams dem go di exile wey dem dey
I go join di queue wey dey long reach like one mile for America or Britain or Canada embassy kom fly go

Luka Istifanus : FCT no go hire athletes wey go win National Sports Festive Medals
