Luka Istifanus : FCT no go hire athletes make dem go win National Sports Festival medals
Di acting director in sports for FCT , Luka Istifanus don frown at di reckless poaching of athletes by di big money spenders as e don vow say di FCT no go waka about dey pay athletes to win National Sports Festival medals
For dis interview wey dem get wit Trust sports , di acting director don yarn on top di performance of team FCT for Edo 2020 and sports development for di Federal Capital Territory
How e dey go as you don resume office as di acting Director of Sports in di FCT ?
Di rate wey dem dey take smuggle no be small
Na me take over as di acting director of sports in di FCT on di 8th day of october 2020 and so tey dat time my major concern na how I go take sports for di Territory beyond wia I meet am
E no dey easy unto say FCT dey more or less civil service settlement
Una no fit compare am wit states like Lagos , Kano , Rivers , Edo , Kaduna and odas
Howeva , we dey do Evrithing wey go help improve di achievements wey we record for past
Interestingly , di Federal Capital Territory Administration don stand gidigba for awa back
FCT don placed 16th place on di medals table wey dem just conclude for di 2020 national sports festival
How satisfied you dey wit di performance of athletes
I suppose start my yarn to say na me be di happiest pesin wen di administration of di FCT approve say make we participate for di 2020 national sports festival
Although room still dey for improvement , I go say I dey satisfied wit wetin we achieve
As we dey look back , na we dey always be di 17th , 18th or 19th apart from wen we host sport festival for 2004 and 2018
una know say if una be di host you get advantage wey plenti
una fit patronise as many events as e possible
you fit register as many athletes wey you want
however , wen una dey go out una go cut down di number of events and athletes to minimise cost
I dey happy say dis time around , we no host but e end up for 16th position despite di enormous challenge wey we face
two states , di host Edo and Delta dey battle for supremacy and na dat dey impact negatively for officiating
we suppose perfom better but na officiating wey dey questionable deny us for plenti medals
no be only us be di victims of di supremacy tussle wey dey between Edo and Delta
in all , we dey grateful bikos we do better dan 21 states
wit di support of di goment , we go do better at Delta 2022
di national sports festival don dey open
how una athletes take cope wit dia opponents wey get more experience
the task no dey easy unto say some states don go far as di USA , France and Germany to hire athletes
as e dey for tennis , di player wey win di singles event na from France and dem pay am a sum of N5 million by Delta state
some states don buy so tey 30 proffessional for outside Kontri which be a whole lot money
Remember in adition to goment money , dem get oil companies wey be dem sponsors
For FCT here , na goment funding we depend on solely
one state don give official money wey reach N15m make e go use am monitor proceedings for combat sports
na di money wey some states struggled get to attend the festival
for us , even before we go Benin city , minister don charge us make we dey responsible to ur behaviors and be worthy ambassadors
hin advised say make we no try win by all means
na hin farewell message to us and we abided by it
we no go outside FCT go look for athletes
e don become di policy of di FCT to raise athletes and expose dem for national and international competitions
na dat exact thing we do
Pale una dey hear , abeg give us good pikin afta una don give us good pikin give us money wey we go use take care of dem
se una support calls in some quarters for di National Sports Festival make dem return am wen e suppose dey for amateurs strictly
no throw - way dis golden opportunity
di advantage wey big pass be say e dey make coach lazy
dem dey give coach salary but wen e reach sports festival time dem go give dem money wey dem go use go oda states go poach other athletes
i remember di 2018 edition , dem force some athletes make dem refund as much as N1m on top say dem fail to deliver medal for di states wey give dem contract
true true dis no help in di development of talents
Na so dem eliminate am
Na so dem deny oda players di opportunity wey go exhibit dia talent
Di sports festival don dey for di highest bidder but FCT no go buy medals
We no get money wey we go use take hire athlethes wey go win medals
We go kontinu dey raise local athletes wey be awa own
Pesin wey get God for hin side
True , true we suppose go back to di grassroots
Na 62 wards FCT get
Na evri council area get 10 words except AMAC wey get 12
Sports development suppose start from di ward level
For di past , FCT don organised so many competitions from di ward level but mostly dey team sports like football , handball , volleyball and athletics
Na events wey no dey capital intensive be dis
We dey always start from di wards to di area council headquarters and to di city centre
Na dis be di platform wey dey kontinue to dey generate athletes for di FCT
So i dey call oda states make dem emulate di FCT wen dem wan develop dia own athletes
As we dey tok of developing athletes , you fit tok say enough standard sporting facilities dey FCT ?
We get six sports centres wey dey under construction for each of di six area councils
Already , we don make one strong appeal and di hon
Minister of state , Dr Ramatu Tijani Aliyu don already go some of di facilities
She don go Kuje and AMAC and she dey dey plan to go to Bwari an odas go see di level of development
wit di backing of di honourable minister , Alhaji Musa Bello , she dey do Evrithing wey go make sure say dem complete diz facilities
We don also make request for sporting equipments for sports like Karate , Judo , Boxing , Wrestling and a host of odas
Na dey expect favourable responses
Na wetin be di plan for di next edition for di sports festival
We don already start training bikos di next edition no reach one year
We don start preparations and we make requests and recommendations wey go enable us prepare adequately for Delta 2022
We don invariably place di welfare for awa neighbours as awa own dey important
We need to dey imbibe di lessons of Ramadan
Need dey make dem pay more attention to di plights of di poor
Di Muslim month of self - purification and self - denial wey dem also know as Ramadan just end
As e dey last , di season wey dem dey use fast don offer all Muslims opportunity wey dem go use reflect on dia relationship wit Allah
E don also enable those wey get means to share food wit pipo wey poor , wey dey in need and pipo wey be less priviledged
For all Muslims , e be opportunity wey dem go use rededicate demsef to di teachings of di faith and di kos of mankind as a whole
Although e be period of deep reflection on di inter - relationship wey dey between man and hin neighbour , for di oda hand , as well as man and hin God
Even though di long - fasting don go , di lessons must endure
Ramadan get high spritual significance , na one of si five pillars of Islam be dat
To devotees , e be period of self - emptying witout which no spiritual being go get a truly rewarding relationship wit hin maker
Na dat explain why dem mark di exercise for Nigeria ( as elsewia in di world ) by private and group players , and abstinence from all forms of wordly comforts and pleasures
di aim Na to enhance spiritual growth and foster charity and brodaly love
As di Muslims don mark di end of dis annual spiritual exercise , dem dey hope say make di outkom go be of immense benefit di nation
Naija pipo can hardly make ends meet due to di economic situation wey dey prevail for di Kontri
As we dey pay attention to di plights of di poor , as dem amply demonstate am for di course of Ramadan we dey invariably place di welfare for awa neighbours say e dey important as awa own
As we dey allow odas partake for awa wealth or material possessions , we honour di one wey make us
Na dis be di heart of all religions but a virtue wey dey hard to imbibe by plenti pipo for Naija
E gast change
So tey di Ramadan fast , like di fawa pillars wey dey Islam , dem aim am at promoting both di spiritual and material well - being of man , e stand to reason say man dey invariable beta off s e dey do di will of God
Wen he dey able to rein in di impulse for self - gratification and greedy accumulation of wealth , man dey more liable to make hin society a better place wey pesin go live in , no be only hin but for hin neighbor also
Dat na one of di most enduring lessons of Ramadan wey we hope plenti pipo go imbibe
E dey noteworthy dat fasting as e be spiritual exercise dey advocated by all religions obstenibly wit di notion say di man wey fit make sacrifices for di bid to tame hin desires go be beta person for hinself and di society wey large
As one expert don put am say , besides abstention for food and drinks , fasting dey help di pesin wey dey faithful make e no dey look di provocative , make e no dey hear di mischievous , and make e no dey utter di obscene and make e dey avoid slander and make e no dey think about inflicting injury for odas
Di month of Rahmah ( blessing ) , barakah ( mercy ) and Magfirah dey upon us
Di blessed month na precious gift from Allah to muslims
But do we know why dis moth dey so special to muslims
Na wetin be di main koko for dis month , and all di blessings wey dey wit it
Na wetin be di lessons wey we suppose take away in observing , di sanctity wey dey dis month
Of course , dis month dey to train us , guide us , and to remind us of how we suppose approach di 11 months of di year wey remain
Ramadan dey teach us plenti lessons : how we go develop awa manners and moral fortitude , how we go treat awa fellow beings wit respect , how we go strenghten awa brodahood , how we go maintain unity wey dey di Muslim community , and how we go dey welkom di non - Muslims wey we dey share land togedir
Di month dey also tech us make we dey more pious , disciplined , and how we go maintain self - control , wen we dey shield awa souls from greed and immorality
But di main koko be say di month dey teach us how we fit improve awa connection wit di Almighty
Di month of Ramadan dey also instill sense of empathy wey dey inside us
E dey allow us to understand di situation of di less fortunate , make we feel and experience di pain of hunger and di pangs of thirst wey awa poverty - stricken brodas and sisters wey no get choice but to go witout food and drinks dey feel everi day wen dem wake
Ramadan na month of mercy and bonding Muslims wey dey all over di world dey help one anoda , and those wey dey dia community , make dem dey spread happiness all around
Dis month na shinny example for di unity wey we fit achieve among all classes of pipo wey dey any society as di rich and di poor , di employer as well as di employee ; di parents as well as di subjects , all dey fast
Regardless of di colour wey dem get for skin or dia social stature , na fasting dey unite all
E dey remind us how we suppose conduct awaselves and awa behaviour towards those wey dey around us while e dey also teach us di impotance of respect
No be to dey abstain from foods and drinks we learn , but we also abstain make we no go make statements and actions wey fit kos harm to pipo or violate rights wey dem get
E dey give us opportunity wey we go use rectify awaselves through performing plenti good deeds wey be like providing food or aid to di needy , improving social interaction , giving charity , sadaqah and zakat , and so on
Di Almighty go remember all di deeds wey do for judgement day
But wetin go apun to all di lesson wey we don learn afta Ramadan
Unfortuntely , we no too dey retain any of di lessons wey we learn for dis holy month pass Eid - Il - Fitr itself
But di koko for Ramadan run deep pass mere celebration
Di lessons wey we receive be di lodestar for di rest of di 11 months for any year wey dem give
Di training wey we receive suppose improve us as human beings fo di rest of awa lives , as dat na di main koko of Ramadan
Afta di month don end , and we don observe awa final fast , and dem don deal wit di Eid celebrations , we go go back to awa normal lives
But e dey important make we kip di spirit of Ramadan alive for di rest of di year , and indeed for awa live wey remain
bikos , na only through unity , modesty , and temperance we fit make di world a place wey beta for all of us
As we don tok evri evri , di nation leadres , political and odawise , get plenti wey dem go take from di lessons of Ramadan
If dem fit curtail deir materialistic tendencies and pay more attention to di yearnings fo di pipo , di Kontri go bikom a place much happier for Evribodi
We direfore dey urge awa leaders make dem imbibe lessons for Ramadan
To awa plenti Muslim readers we tok say , Eid Mubarak
Make Allah reward una sacrifice
Ibrahin Adbon dey write from Abeokuta , Ogun state
I neva open one page today
Column no 6 : who dey check checkpoint for Abuja
E dey go as dem dey tok am say Abuja , wey be di capital for awa dear Naija , dey important
So na me go be di last person wey go complain say security too much
In fact , I go even tok am say e need am more
Checkpoints , wey be di incredibly useful security constructs , don help and e still dey kontinue to help make e either thwart criminal , or even proactively tackle crime
Di police , wey dem saddle wit plenti of di internal security , at least for di ideal situation , man most of di checkpoints for Abuja Metropolis , as well as areas wey dey di surrounding
Sure , di army don pick up di slack for some places , but di boys supose be di main custodians
Dem vex for di pikin say dem do dat kain thing
Boy , dem dey mess things up for plenti cases
For starters , take for instance one of di checkpoints wey dey Wuse II , particularly di one wey dey lead from zone 4 treach Wuse II , just before e reach di bridge
di conduct of di officers for dere , for my experience , dey abysmal
anyone wey ply dat road afta 9pm
I no go enta details , but wetin I fit tok be say e dey extremely unprofessional sometimes
still for Wuse II , just beside di AP Plaza , di Tori na di same
I go lyk suggest to di higher - ups make dem monitor all di checkpoints wey dey Wuse II make dem see wetin I dey tok firsthand
but di checkpoints horror Tori no end for there
probably di one wey worst pass na di checkpoint wey dey afta di popular Banex junction wey dem dey man by cops wey dey from di Counter Terrorismm Unit ( CTU ) no less
barking at commuters and intimidating innocent citizens evri night , dem cut a picture of a poorly - trained and badly - behaved set of individuals wey seem to miss di point say dem suppose protect and serve citizens
na di same CTU dey responsible for di presonnel manning for one checkpoint wey dey near di Naija Farms And Ranch ( NAFARLS ) , wia all kain tinz dey unfold
anyone wey dey ply dat road fit see for demselves
I go also request make di higher - ups do di same , wit a view wey dem go use fix things
forget Abuja for one minute
look around Naija , and di plenti checkpoints roadblocks , really for highway across di Kontri by numerous security agencies , dem dey see am a reson for loss of time generally , or even for consumer goods and services
as di case be wit awa security organisations , dem dey always push back swiftly , wit well - oiled PR machines wey deny allegations or issuing veiled threats
no forget di fact say while plenti checkpoints fit be legal , plenti are not
dem make am clear by di way and manner in which di personnel mounting dey carry out dia activities
now , dis no be police - bashing piece
E no suppose disparge VIOs and FRSC personnel
E be general critique for checkpoints and how we dey do am for dis part of di world
which means we go look at odas , lyk di Federal Road Safety Corps ( FRSC ) and dat of VIOs
again , I no go yarn too much , just make I suggest closer monioring of di checkopints and checkpoints , really for some revelation dey shock
dis na bikos dis no be piece wey suppose disparge anyone or any organisation
but generally someone fit do something about di ridiculous lack of quality of awa checkpoints ?
checkpoints no be recent , e far as innovations go
dem be set standards for di various stypes wey exist , wetin we need do na to adhere to dem
dem dey quite helpful for fighting crime , we no fit wish dem away
But we owe to awaself to get dem right
like most things dem get di capacity for great good , but if to say dem handle am badly , e fit be source for plenti bad things
maybe if we focus on di one wey dey Abuja go help us , as best practices don dey spread nationwide
I no get interest in highlighting di bad , but di personnel wey dey di checkpoint dey make am inevitable
as all hope neva lost : I dey hope say somehow , someone , somewia wey fit do something about awa checkpoints go do something dem
dat someone , somewia , somehow , dey check awa checkpoints , and di pipo wey dey man dem
e fit make all di difference in awa safety and public perception about awa security personnel , wey be something we dey lack solely for a while now
time neva reach ?
we dey do things different - different
put am for rotation
Glut don jam Katsina tomato farmers
Farmers and dealers of tomatoes for Katsina state don experince for di past two weeks acute market glut ; some don resort to dey sun - dry di produce
according to di farrmers , dem no dey expect dat kain development , considering di stiff economic condition wey dey di Kontri , high cost and demand for food items , as well as longtime border closure wey halt free importation of food items wey include tomato paste
Shehu Bashiru Danja , wey be tomato farmer yarn say dem dey expect huge revenue for dis period but dem dash deir hope wit di recent development
plenti of us don target christmas and New year period , wit di hope say we go make good sales or di produce , but e shock us say we go end up for market glut
hin tok say e really affect us bikos of di high cost of production wey involve fertiliser , seeds , herbicides / pesticides and labor
Bahiru kom add say since di closure for land borders and di outbreak of COVID - 19 , di market price for tomato no less pass N1 , 000 for one basket until recently
hin kom add for last year say dem sell one big basket of tomatoes between N3 , 000 and N10 , 00 , one reason wey many irrigation farmers dis season go concentrate on tomato production , and dem dey hope say e go yield huge profits pass crops like wheat , irish potato , or cabbage
Hamza Dalhatu , wey be tomato merchant and farmer yarn say dem borne di market glut out of protest against di indiscriminate taxes and levies wey dem put for di produce for Southern market
so tey last year , increase don dey in taxes and levies on awa goods and trucks wey dey di southern part for di Kontri
di security issue wey dey linger be threats to awa merchants ; na so dem suspend business till dem sort out things
we no fit kontinue lyk dat
Dalhatu tok say , all di cost burden go end up on farmers wey no go consider di cost of production .
one check for Danja and Funtua market don reveal say one small basket of tomatoes cost N400 wen one big basket no pass N1 , 200
so tey last week Friday
anoda tomato dealer , Sani Suleiman Hunkuyi , don express hope say things go soon normal as dealers for Lagos and Ibadan don visit some of dia members wey dey Sokoto , Kebbi , and Zamfara make dem fashion out new terms for di business
di market glut for di produce be temporary and farmers go soon kontinue dey reap I maximum benefits for dem sweat
Suleiman tok say / Suleiman yarn say
Also , Umar Isah , wey be an agric based Katsina yarn say market glut no be beta thing to pipo wey dey produce Tomato and Onion , and e go kontinue unless dem produce modern storage and and processing facilities , no be only by di goverment but agricultural companies and entrepreneurs
di only way be say make dem establish local storage and processing facilities wey dem go use produce zone across di Kontri
hin yarn say , make agric companies and entrepreneurs take dis challenge as soon as possible take use solve di long time problem
Nana na di last pesin wey commot di room
supreme price : di Tori wey dem no yarn of policemen wey dem kill for ENDSARS protest
Sergeant Adegoke Ajibola and Corporal Rotimi Oladele run as fast as deir legs fit carry , seek for place wey dem go hide , pleaded for deir lives as di mob close on dem
all dia pleas go fall on deaf ears
dem drag dem , beat dem , hit dem wit sticks , knives and any objects wey dey available for sight
for di time wey dem still dey beg make dem spare dia lives , dem set dem for fire for one heap of tyres
as di fire dey rage , dia voice lost for di flames , wey dem no go eva hear dem for for life
di two men wey dem burn to death for Iwo Road for di ancient town fo Ibadan , wey be di largest city for Naija , no be criminals
no , di only crime be say dem be crime fighters
one video wey go viral by one of di hoodlums show di despicable scene as dem set di policemen ablaze on top a heap of tyres wey dem don use and dem shared dia bodi
di two dey among di policemen wey no less 22 , seven soldiers and 59 civilians wey dem kill for October 2020 during di ENDSARS protest , according to di toll wey President Muhammadu Buhari announce for one emergency meeting wey hin get wit former Nigerian leaders
di ENDSARS be decentralised social movement and a series of mass protests gainst police brutality For Naija
di slogan call for make dem disband di Special Anti - Robbery Squad ( SARS ) , wey be one notorious unit of di Nigerian Police and e get long record for abuse
di EndSARS protest , wey last two weeks , dey peaceful until hoodlums wey loot public and private - owned warehouse burn police station and destroy propety hijack am
according to di official record and findings by awa correspondence , Ajibola and Oladele no be members of di SARS wey dem just disband
in fact dem no be regular policemen wey dem dey see for road as finding don reveal say dem dey attached to di operation department for Oyo state police command
di area wey dem dey engage dey usually be for special duty as different companies and organisations de request , and as e dey approved by di command
dem dey dia way for dat engagement for one fish depot for di Wema Bank area wey dey Gbagi for Ibadan wen dem meet dia untimely death
coincidentally , Ajibola wey be 41 year - old and hin colleague , Oladele , get three pikin each
Oladele's wife , Feranmi , just born dia third pikin 16 days before di unfortunate incident
Feranmi , wey be di orphan , just as her husband wey late , tok say di news of hin death shattered her world
tears well up for her eyes as she dey recount di experience of six months ago wey dey horrifying
sensing danger as di EndSARS protest don dey tun violent for some areas , Feranmi don plead make Oladele stay for house
her husband ignore her plea , wey say hin no fit abdicate hin responsibilities as a law enforcement agent
undettered , Feranmi call Oladele's elder sister make she kom chook mouth for di mata , but di police refuse all treaties wey go make am stay for house
afta plenti persuasion , hin promise day hin go stay for di office
hin sister say make I leave am since hin tok say no be field e dey go say na di office
four hours afta hin don commot , I kom feel say something don apun to me
I no fit chop
I no dey okay unto say I dey expect make hin call me , but I no see dat kind ti
I call am but hin phone no go through
na so I go meet one of awa neighbawas go inform her about it , but she say maybe my husband's phone don off bikos hin no get time wey e go use charge am
shortly , afta dat one , as I dey outside my room
na so I hear as pipo dey tok say dem don kill two policemen for town
e no too far , na so I see pipo wey dey commot dia property out of di barracks and dem no tell me nada
dem dey move wit fear make dem no go attack di barracks
in fact , dem dey watch me bikos plenti of dem don know say dem kill my husband
as e be like 8pm wen pipo don commot di barracks , I still dey wait make my husband kom house
na so I decide say make I visit di Eleyele headquartes wen my sisters enter for awa house
she say make I follow am go her house
I dey hear pipo yarn say my husband get accident
na dat be di last moment wey I remember
di day wey follow , di man wey old pass for my family kom meet me kom explain say my husband don kpeme
she say I no sabi anything for like five days
her words stop intermittently as she dey try kontrol her tears unsuccesfully
dem tell us make we accept awa fate and move on
na three pikin hin get
my last pikin be 16 days wen di tin apun
dem attack hin for Iwo Road
hin dey among di two victims wey dem roast for Abayomi
she kom add , I hear say those hoodlums chop di flesh of my hsuband wit fear all over her
na una be di boss for dis Tarmac
Bolanle - Ajibola wey be di wife of sergeant Ajibola kom describe di gruesome murder of her husband as disheartening and disguisting
reluctantly recalling di inident wey apun for October 22 , Tokede dey wonder how di standard for humanity don depreciate so tey human beings go dey kill and chop each oda
I dey work for October 22 wey one of hin colleagues call me say dem don kill my husband
dem attack am for police headquarters for Eleyele
so tey di news wey I hea , dem roast am afta hoodlums don lynch am
I no hapi wen I hear am
I no get myself , but I don accept my accept
I hear say some hoodlums don carry part of hin flesh away while some dey chop am
she lament say e dey disheartening and disgusting
plenti commentators , wey include di goverment and di police authorities agree say dem get justifiable reasons for di EndSARS protests owing to di excess of officers wey dey di unit , but for di heat dem kill many innocent and officers wey dey dedicated
hin be good and caring man
so tey hin demise , I don miss evri evri about hin
e dey painful bikos hin get parents wey dey here for Ibadan
my husband dey commited to hin job
Mrs Bolanle - Ajibola kom add say dem dey always assign hin for special assignment and hin dey carry hin tasks out dilligently until dem kill am
for her part , Mrs Oladele decribe her husband as a man wey good to motorists and hin dey respect odas for di discharge of hin duties
my husband dey veri good to me
hin dey always give me wetin I need and e no dey stress
hin dey nice to motorists
in fact , plenti of dem dey visit and gimme money
hin dey respect pipo
plenti pipo dey yarn plenti good tinz about am
hin love hin pikin and e no dey use dia well - being play
hin death horrible
those wey witness di incident say dem beat am seriously before hin kpeme and dem set am for fire
she say , as she drop her head for her hand
dem murder three oda officers gruesomely for di protest for Oyo state
dem kill dem wen hoodlums overwhelm di police for Ojoo , Ibadan
dem later know say na only di bodi of 37 - year - old James Akanmu dem find for wia di attackers dump am allegedly
di relatives of Alidu Yusuf Wada and Peter Agunbiade still dey find di remains of dia breadwinners
Beauty James Akanmu tell awa correspondent say she follow her husband tok a few minutes before dem kill am
I call am wen I hear say prosters dey Ojoo
e tell me say e don apun ( dem dey under attack ) and I tell am say make hin commot di station
hin say hin dey find way wey hin go use commot
as I dey follow am tok , hin phone off na dat be di last conversation wey we get
so tey dat day I neva hear from am
we call hin phone number but e no go through
afta three days , dem call me say make I go check di stream wia dem dump am
we see am , but dem don take evri evri for hin bodi
na only hin identity card and uniform we see for hin bodi
dem don destroy almost all di parts of hin bodi
she narrate as tears dey gush from her eyes say , dem no recover di remaining part of hin bodi and deposit am for one morgue
e dey uncontrollable as she go mute for some minutes before eulogising di late crime detector
na hin be di only one wey dey care for di family
I no get anything wey I go do
hin no get any legitimate business wey hin go use care for hin family , especially hin pikin
hin three pikin na boys
hin parents don kpeme
di last statement wey I get wit am na make e find a way out of di station , and hin say hin go try
before dem kill am , nobodi know say na police officer for di neighbourhood
she add say he neva brag
I still dey find my husband
Alidu Esdir still dey search for di bodi of her husband , Alidu Yusuf Wada , 205 days afta dem kill am for di attack on di Ojoo police station
Mrs Alidu no fit hide her pain as she dey recall her di last moment of her late husband , wey she decscribe as di only hope wey dey her life
Mr Wada leave house dat day wey fateful wit hin usual promise to hin fawa pikin say hin go buy gift for hin way back home
sadly , he neva return to dat house
dem tell am about her husband's death afta di sad event
and since , di search for hin remains neva yield positive results
my husband na good man
e rare to find dat kain kind - hearted husband
he be calm pesin and e dey take care of hin family
hin be di only family wey I get
hin be my papa and my mama
hin care for me wit evri evri wey hin get
he kom leave four pikin for me make I dey care for
as we dey tok , we neva recover hin bodi
I hear say hin wan climb di building for di station to escape wen dem kill am
wen goverment official reach di station to evecauate hin bodi , dem no find am
hin parents dey alive , dem dey Kogi State
I hear say dem strip am , hit am wit sharp objects , drag am for road for oda office front before hin kpeme
I hear say hin struggle wit dem
but you know say , so tey na mob attack , e go hard to survive
she tok am wit tearful eyes
Dem also kill one 42 - year - old inspector Peter Agunbiade wey be exhibit keeper for record department for di station
According to hin wife , dem burn di papa of four to death so tey nobodi see hin remains
Mrs Agunbiade tok say na october 20 di incident apun
Hin tell me say hin dey go work go work as DPO don ask make all of dem report for office
so before 6am , hin don commot for house
Me and di pikin pray for am bikos e dey aware of di situation of tinz wey dey occurate for di kontri for dat time
Hin call me around 12pm dey tok say EndSARS protesters don raze di station wey close to di highway for Ojoo
I ask am for hin wellbeing and hin tok say dem don commot go DPO's office for safety
on top di palpable fear wey dey hover for around am , na di thought of hin pikin and dia wellbeing dey di top of di inspector mind
hin call hin wife back dey beg am make she make effort go di protest , wey don take over di major areas for di state go pick di pikin for school
di wfe do am , but na dat be di last conversation as she no fit reach her husband again
as hin don sense danger , Mrs Agunbiade run go di station di day wey follow , but di building na total ruin
protesters don raze am
e dey deserted and pesin wey we go follow tok no dey
she run go di police station wey dey Eleyele , but nobodi fit give am answer wey go satisfy her about wia her husband dey and dem ask make she go ask di DPO for wia her husbnd dey workk
later , I go di headquarter for Eleyele , I meet di DPO and hin explain say di mobs plenti pass dem
hin tell me say dem beat my husband and burn am alive
hin be good man
hin dey in charge of record keeping
hin be recorder
hin no be troublesome man
hin be exhibit keeper
hin be graduate and hin no like violence
hin no dey always dey uniform
pipo no dey see am for outside
hin parents still dey alive
hin be caring husband to me and caring father to hin pikin
if to say na di last moni wey dey hin hand hin go still drop am for us
hin dey calm
plenti pipo for awa neighbourhood no no am until he kpeme
hin paln na to ensure say hin pikin be gradute , but now , hin no dey to fulfill hin dreams
she narrate say , we neva recover hin remains
one 14 - year - old twin of di late inspector tok say dem neva recover from di shock wey make dem lose dia Papa for tender age
dem get two oda siblings wey young
Kehinde Agunbiade , wey tok on top di children behalf say , wen we hear about am we felt broken and shattered
we believe say awa Papa dey innocent , as di Bible don tok am say wen di wicked dey face justice di innocent go be part of am
my Papa dey gentle , kind and e dey alwsy find way wey hin go use take help pipo
hin suppose go for hin graduation for hin Master's degree before di incident apun
na hin good deeds save am
if no be for hin good deeds , a Kogi state - born Yakubu Enemali go don kpeme afta hoodlum attack di Ojoo divion of di police force for Naija , Ibadan for di protest , noted di woman wey save am
dem kill three policemen for di attack , but na good samaritan save Enemali
Daily Trust don gather say na woman wey hin don help for past save di Papa
Di good samaritan wey refuse to mention name , for security purpose , confirm for Daily trust say dem axe Enemali for head , shoot am for leg and she meet am for hin pool of blood
Before Enemali's wife go reach , di woman don carry am go nearby clinic for first aid
seven months afta dem rescue am , Enemali still neva utter one word
Hin dey in pain and hin no fit tok
Hin dey misbehave , get sleepless nights and hin no dey quick comprehend issues
For di moment , even if to say Enemali fit recognise pipo , hin no fit tok , na dis necessitate di need make e undergo Magnetic Resonance Imaging ( MRI ) wey be test for di brain for di Chemical Pathology Department for di University College Hospital ( UCH ) , Ibadan make dem determine which kain surgery dem go carry out
Dem diagnose am wit seizures for di MOP and SOP department of di hospital
According to di medical expert , Dr Mustapha Ajakaiye , seizure na sudden , uncontrolled electric disturbance for di brain
E dey kos changes for behaviour , movements or feelings and level of consciousness
awa correspondent wey visit hin residential apartment for Idi - Omo area , Akinyele local goverment Area for Ibadan , observe say shishi no dey dia sitting room
Enemali's wife Tosin , tok to di Daily Trust Saturday say , dem don sell all dia property use di money take care of hin health and di pikin
na fashion desighner I be
I sell all my sewing machine use take care of am bikos I neva know say e go take dis long make hin regain consciousness
Aside for my machines , I don also sell all di chairs , television , home theater and oda valuables wey dey awa house
As una fit see am , we no get anything again
I don invite person wey go buy di bed frame for front of di house make we use am buy drugs for am
I decide say I go stay wit am unto say my husband na good man
I know say hin dey alive today bikos of hin good deeds
I no sabi di woman wey rescue am wen di hoodlums attack am , but God see hin heart and make an escape route for am
Dem cheat , forget and neglect am
six months afta di # EndSARS protest wey claim di lives of plenti policemen , including di six officers attached to di Lagos State Command , dia widows stilll dey wait on top di promises wey di goverment and di goverment and di Police force make
so tey wen dem lose dia breadwinners , we fit describe di plights of dis widows as a desperate struggle for survival as dem no get choice but to fend for dia pikin , one task wey dem neva expose to for dia husbands lifetime
Di burden wey di cold hands of death place don place for dia hand don weigh plenti of dem down
As dem no fit cope , some of dem don commot go dia village
Dem tok say di lagos state goverment give N10 million each , but dat good gesture don pitch dem against di relatives of dia late husband
awa corespondent don hear from some of di widows say di relatives of dia late husbands don collect di money wey state goment give dem
dem say na only shikili money dem hand over to dem by di head of di respective family
Those wey follow awa correspondent yarn say dem dey expect di schorlarship wey di police force don promise dia children
Di officer wey dem kill for Lagos protest na Assistant Superintendent for police ( ASP )
Edward Yard wey dey attach to Denton station ; inspector Ayodeji Erinfolami wey dey attached to di defunct anti kidnapping unit ; Inspector Aderibigbe Adegbenro wey dey attached to Meiran division ; Sergeat Bejide Abiodun wey dey attched to di DOPS HQ ; Ehibor Samson nd one oda wey dem attach to Orile division
Daily Trust Saturday don report earlier say dem set 16 police stations ablaze for di unrest of di state
Dem include Orile , Amukoko , Layeni , Old Area J command , Ajah , Elemoro , New Area J command , Elemoro , Igando , Ebute - Ero , Ajah and e barracks and Ilasamaja police stations
Odas na Makinde and e barracks , Ikotun , Isokoko , Pen - Cinema , Onipanu , Alade police stations e . t . c
dem vandalise like 13 formations , amongst wey dey na stations like Ojoo and Ojodu
A total of 38 policemen for various formation / location wey dey di state don sustain varying degrees of injury
back to di village
Hannaty Yard tell di correspondent say she and her five pikin don relocate go village

I don carry my pikin relocate go my village for Niger state

na me dey responsible for di things wey hin dey do

For Olamide Erinfolami , life no dey fair for am and her pikin

na Daily Trust Foundation fund di Tori , and na MacArthur Foundation support am
Abiodun Alade and Eugene Agha for Lagos , Jeremiah Oke for Ibadan and Idowu Samotu for Abuja
Explosion dey for around dat ikeja and e kill some pipo
Dem dey develop Naija's gas for di domestic market
di natural gas na one cultured industry wey dey drive innovation and e dey touch nearly Evri field and aspect of life wey we care about
from mobile phones to di makeup wey we dey wear , to medical devices , bank cards , and even di football wey e dey kick around wit friends
Di industry na one of di building blocks of di things wey we need and love evri day
dem dey use natural gas for transportation , cooking , electricity generation and manufacturing
Dem dey use am as raw material wey dem dey use make ferterlizer , antifreeze , plastics , pharmaceuticals and fabrics
Di steel and paper industry dey also us e natural gas to generate process steam wey dem dey use for industrial applications
Data wey dey for ground don show say Africa's largest economy , Naija , get di largest natural gas reserves for di continent
wit oil , di industry go account for about 70 per cent of its revenue , e go make di sector one of Naija's best and most sought - afta employment sectors
plenti of Naija's electricity generation na from natural gas , while dem dey use di crude oil for power backup
one forecast wey di U . S Energy Information Administration do don show say dat natural gas go be di largest elcetricity generation source
Natural - gas dem bring its sevaral quality - of - life environmental benefits bikos e dey relatively clean burning - fuel
Globally , di sector dey dey produce millions of jobs , , wit employment wey dey up to 40 per cent so tey di Great Reccession of 008 for di U . S alone
Thus , given di gas reserves wey dey exist , e shock to see say Naija no dey lead di continent gas industry
President Buhari don launch di kontri's decade of gas , for 29th of March 2021
Di aim na to transform Naija into a gas - powered industrialised economy by 2030
Developing di gas industry go boost oda industries through di provsion of electricity and raw materials
Here , we go shine light on three points : some gas development policies wey dey critical , di potential benefits of developing di gas industry for di domestic market , and di employent opportunities wey dey gas industry
So tey di discovery of gas for Naija , subsequent attempts to develop di industry
For example , di gas commercialisation and utilisation programmes contributed to reduce gas flaring and increase gas utilisation by about 300 per cent between 1995 and 2017
there be gas pipeline projects wey concentrate on di western part of di kontri and di continent
Dem commissioned di first Escravos to Lagos Pipeline System for 1989 to supply lagos and neighboring south - west states
Afta di success of di ELPS , di goverment agree make dem dey supply Ghana , Benin and Togo through di Western African Gas Pipeline wey dem commission for 2016
Howeva , dis project no dey favourable to di kontri's domestic market , given di persistent issues for power wey dey di kontri
Evidently , Naija's power sector dey challenged wit electricity facilities wey poor , shortage for natural gas supply , distribution network wey dey inefficient and transmission system wey dey inadequate
Accordig to di 2018 estimate wey di International Energy Agency do , na only 60 per cent of Naija dey use natural gas
population get access to electricity
power shortage don limit di growth for di Kontri's total population for all sectors
E don kos make plenti business close or move completely to neighboring kontries
E dey challenge new start - ups and attract foreign investment
Di lack of electricity don contribute to di high rate of inflation as business don dey pay for expensive alternative electricity source , dia production cost don increase , and e dey increase di price of goods and services
To mitigate diz issue , di Buhari administration don commision gas infrastructure project make dem promote use of gas for domestic market
Di projects include di second Escravos to Lagos Pipeline System ( ELPS - 2 ) Obiafu Obriko
Oben ( OB3 ) gas line and di Ajaokuta to Kaduna to Kano ( AKK ) gas line
Di AKK gas line project go pass through Abuja from Ajaokuta
Den we go see anoda line from Abuja to Kaduna , , den from Kaduna to Zaria , and from Zaria to Kano
wit hindight , dem suppose do dis projects since di turn of di millenium
Nonetheless , dem be notable projects and dem suppose praise dem wit optimism
Dem expect make di project guarantee net investment return
Di gas line go provide gas to cement firms , and residential customers
Di users of compressed natural gas like buses and trucks go dey able to buy di product cheaper as di supply don increase
Di governmet dey also plan to build three new gas - fired power plants for power generation plants wey dem fit locate for Abuja , Kaduna , and Kano , make dem use di pipelines gas to generate 3 , 600 MW power
Di power plant go provide electricity for households and many industries wey dey di Northern part of di kontri
Di benefit for producing a decent amount of power and raw materials from gas go born one success tori
For example , if dem resuscitate di textile industry e go mean say dem dey revive di largest manufacturing sub - sector , wey account for 22 per cent of employment and 15 per cent of manufacturing value - added for 1984
in di long run , di tax revenue for di performing industries and employees go outweigh di cost of pipeline projects
If to say goverment policies dey successful , all oda things as e dey equal , di natural gas industry go be one major source of job opportunities for Naija's labour force wey dey rise
Di industry get high concentration of contractors and sub - contractors , wit different splits wey dey between specialists
Dem characterise di industry as semi - skiled and skiled crafts trades positions
Demmno restrict jobs wey dey di sector to petrolrum engineers alone
plenti roles no need special education
Di skil na something e fit learn on di job , from attorneys to welders to architects , truck drivers and accountants
Di industry dey also pay minimum wage
E mean say di industry get enormous opprtunity to attract , retain , and developlifelong careers for individuals as di industry dey expand
To dey find job for di industry dey similar to oda sophisticated , high - tech industries
Employees suppose get decent education , some certification as industry specialist go be an advantage , training and experince go go far
therefore , as di goverment dey lay out policies for di Decade of Gas , , di opportunity for capacity development go open
Di education sector fit explore di training curriculum wey dey for di industry and ways wey dem go take use attract industry experts wey go contribute to capacity development
In conclusion , di decade for Gas na desirable policy
E be opportunity for Naija wey dem go use to develop di gas industry , even as e dey look a bit too late for dis administration
Thus , di goment wey next and all di relevant stakeholders suppose consider dis ingenuity wey dem go use transform di kontri to a gas - powered industrialised economy
Dr Nasir Aminu na di programme Director for Economics , Cardiff School for Management wey dey United Kingdom
I want make dem know say God don do me marvelous thing

As di demand for rabbit don dey increase , frmers dey explain say make di youths key in for dis kain of farming
Rabbit farming no common for Naija but di demand for rabbit meat dey grow as e be for kontries like Europe and Asia
Acoording to wetin di Food and Agriculture Organisation of di United Nations ( FAO ) don estimate say dem dey slaughter 1 . 2 billion rabbits annually for meat
Di South African National Agricultural Marketing Council for June 2020 don reveal say 1 . 48 million tons of rabbit meat were produced in 2017 .
China wey be di leading producer dey acount for 62 . 9 % of di production wey dey global , followed by followed by North Korea ( 10 . 4 % ) , Spain ( 3 . 9 % ) and Egypt ( 3 . 8 % ) , among odas
As 2019 dey end , Hungary , China , France and Spain dey among di major contributors to di trade balance for rabbit meat by value globally
According to wetin statistic say . Germany , Belgium and Italy na di leading importers as dem dey command 21 % , 19 . 2 % and 9 . 3 % share of global imports respectively
For Naija here , one far , Wise Trust Intl Ltd dey change di narrative amidst huge and rising demand for rabbit meat and breeding stock for di kontri
Pastor Tayo Ayinla wey white meat dey drive hin passion tok am say hin first motivation for di rabbit business na di health benefit bikos pipo wey dey hin age suppose cut down di consumption of red meat and waka dey chop white meat hin kom add say di motivation further led to di discovery of its economic benefits .
Na di pastor get di biggest rabbit farm for di Federal Capital Territory
Hin get 17 species of rabbit on top di farm wey hin start like say a year ago for Karshi , for Abuja Municipal Area Council .
Hin dey raise dem for cage , hutches wey dem construct locally and in free range
Dis reporter wey dey Karshi , visit di farm wia di pastor kom share hin knowledge of rabbit farming so odas fit tap into am
Hin also get rabbits for anoda farm for Kwara state
Some of di free range rabbit for di farm
How rabbits dey multiply
Hin say if di farmer get about 60 to 70 doe ( na di female rabbit dem dey call doe and di male buck ) wit an average of five births per rabbit , hin go get very good number per year .
For instance , on dis farm , we don see a doe wey born 10 to 11 rabbits
But I wan dey more conservative
So make we say five rabbits as an average : di one rabbit fit give farmer between 25 to 30 rabbits for a year bikos wen good management dey dem fit produce four to six times for one year
So if to say hin get five for one year dat mean say hin get 25
Multiply am by di 60 wey we dey tok about e make 1 , 600 rabbits for one year
Of kos , una fit get pass dat
pipo dey demand for rabbit meat
Di demand for rabbit meat dey grow and according to wetin Pastor Ayinla say , dem neva meet di demand fully
Hin tell di reporter say hin receive order of 10 tons of rabbit meat for di Southwest but e dey very difficult to get even one ton
At some time una go get perosn wey go dey request for 2 , 500 rabbits say hin wan breed am but hin go get up 500
One time dey wey we get request of 2 , 500 rabbits for breeding stock for di whole of di North ( di client organisation get Northern representative for Abuja here ) , but for di whole of di North , we dey only supply a little above 200 out of di order wey dem place for 2 , 500 .
So rabbitry na upkoming ATM moni dispenser
Hin say very soon e go turn moni dispencing business
Di rabbit value chain don boom
Di farmer explain for di rabbit value chain say : most of us no know di benefits wey we get for rabbit rearing
Number one be say , plenti value dey for rabbit farming
As a farmer una fit make moni from selling di rabbits breding stock to anoda farmer ; una fit sell rabbit meat to those wey want am ; una fit get income through di sale of dia poo or from di conversion of dia poo into gas for cooking , or generation of electricity and wetin remain of dat process fit be used as fertiliser .
Most pipo dey use rabbit wastes for fertiliser but e no dey as effective as wen una dey pass di poo for some process
Also , dem fit use di urine as pesticide for di production of vegetables
Cost wey dem dey take use start rabbit farm no dey expensive
wit just N25 , 000 to N30 , 000 farmer fit start rabbit farming
Di good thing be say anybodi fit do am ; an old person fit do am bikos of di management dey very easy
Una no need one particular place to do rabbit farming bikos dem be neat animals , dem no dey smell
Actually una fit do am for una house even for person wey get two - bedroom flat
For instance , una fit convert one of di room
Dem no dey smell
Di farmers dey always kom buy from us ; we dey assist dem set up dia farms
And as I tok am , for awa own little way , we start am about a year ago
Rabbit feed no dey expensive
Di thing wey good about rabbits be say dia feeding no dey demand , dem just dey chop anything
For instance , as we dey handle am here , we dey usually go meet pipo wey dey sell cabbage and collect di outer cover of di cabbage , e dey okay for dem
Also for di person wey dey sell watermelons , pipo dey usually chop di red part throw - way di cover
Di cover dey medicinal to dem
Also , we dey go market wey dem dey sell carrots go pick di leaves
Virtually wetin rabbit dey chop na almost free , and e dey get much easier
wen di rain start den we fit get plenti fresh leaves for dem
One word for di youths be say make dem work hard
My advice for di youths be say make dem understand say di goverment no fit meet all of awa needs
Di reason why we dey get some kain kwanta be say plenti pipo want make goverment jobs
First and foremost , una need look inward : wetin I fit do for myself
Until una fit do something for unaself una no fit do anything for di kontri
Una suppose understand say lots of opportunity dey as dis kontri is concerned
Some pipo go tell you say dem wan do dis and dat
Egun pipo speak beta pass una
But market no dey
So di question na : how una go dey kontri wey get pass 200 million pipo kom dey tok say money no dey
Una dey tok say market no dey
Na either una no understand how dem dey market wetin una dey do
Abi una no know how dem dey do business
Like for rabbit , if una see how awa rabbits be , di business go attract you , dem dey look so robust
So pipo dey say I neva see rabbit wey big like dis
Dis na di way we dey take use manage dem in terms of wetin we feed dem and di environment wey we create for dem
So pipo go begin dey look inwards

Banks assets don declare and corruption war
If u dey plan to buy correct seed , make u find di ones wey get SEEDCODEX tag by di National Agricultural Seed Council ( NASC ) .
Di SEEDCODEX tag na electronic seed verification and authentication system wey dey attached to every seed pack .
Farmers go fit scratch am and send di code to one numba for verification .
Di Director General of di council , Dr Phillips Ojo , tok dis for Abuja wen e dey follow tori - pipo yarn about di readiness of di agency to provide quality and certified seeds for di 2020 / 2021 plantin season .
Awa call to farmers na say only di seeds wey get di NASC SEEDCODEX tag fall for dis category and na im make dem buy from dia seed suppliers .
Di SEEDCODEX tag , as u know , na di result of di NASC electronic seed verification and authentication system wey go enhance di efficiency of awa seed certification and quality assurance program wey we establish to prevent seed adulteration by greedy seed merchants .
Farmers suppose know say all di certified seeds packs for Nigeria must get dis authentication tags wit di code on dem , so farmers go fit send di code to immediately verify if di seed wey dem buy na original and dem go fit report any mago - mago seed dealer for di national seed business to NASC , Dr Ojo yarn .

Traffickers hide drugs for inside statue of Blessed Virgin Mary
Drug traffickers wey dey find easy way to smuggle illegal drugs don follow di religious route as dem load di statue of di Blessed Virgin Mary , Mother of Jesus wit drugs .
NDLEA operatives wey dem plant for two courier companies seize di drugs wey dem hide inside di statue , and som odas for inside motor spare parts wey dem wan ship go Canada and UAE .
About 140 grammes of methamphetamine wey dem wan send go Philippines , inside di statue of Mary na im officers seize for one of di courier company .
Anoda 500 grammes of heroin wey dem dey send go Canada for inside motor spare parts na im dem seize for di second courier company .
Accordin to Mr Femi Babafemi wey be di director of media and advocacy for NDLEA , dem seize anoda two separate package of Indian hemp wey dem wan send go UAE .
3 . 1kg wey dem hide inside spices and anoda one kilogramme wey dey inside local herbs .
For anoda development , di NDLEA for different sting operation arrest 31 suspects for Ondo State , unto say dem catch dem wit 276 kg of assorted illegal drugs .
Som of dose wey dem arrest na seven female .
Dem arrest dem durin a two - week raid wey begin for April 6 .
Babafemi tok say dem do di sting operations to stop di rate of drug abuse wey dey increase among youths and even di elderly for Ondo State .
E add am join say di illegal drugs wey dem seize na 74 . 285kgs of Indian hemp , 267 grammes of oda psychotropic substance ;
201kgs of skuchies ( combination of Indian hemp , tramadol , ethanol , and Zobo ) .
NDLEA scatter or destroy most of di spots wia dem dey sell di drugs .
E yarn .
Inside Akwa Ibom , di NDLEA also seize 62 . 150kg of illegal drugs for Oron and Uyo .
Babafemi yarn wetin di NDLEA commander for di state , Obot Bassey tok , say na four suspect dem arrest inside two sting operations wey dem do for April 22 and April 23 .
E tok am say di NDLEA chairman , retired Brig . - Gen . Buba Marwa , don commend di operatives for di two states and dose wey dey Operations and General Investigations Directorate for Lagos on dia steadfastness .
Pastor Adefarasin ; if Nigeria na scam ; den all of us na scammers
Na di compulsory duty of everi citizen to hold di government to account .
In fact , citizenship na call to duty for di state .
And no compulsory duty wey pass make citizens dey scrutinize and monitor dia employees """" di government """" frequently .
Criticising di government na part of di rights of everi citizen , and active citizenship get to do wit takin di governmentthroughe pace .
No government wey dem no dey criticise , and no government too special for pipo to criticise .
But , we need differentiate between any government and Nigeria as a kontri .
Government go kom and go , but Nigeria go remain .
We need understand say Nigeria na di pipo wey dey inside .
So , wen we belittle di kontri , we just dey shoot awasef for leg .
If we tok say Nigeria na scam , indirectly wetin we mean be say , Nigerians be scammers .
Nigeria no be scam , like som of dose wey dey abuse di nation dey always tok , unknowingly ; Na we turn Nigeria to anytin wey e be .
Nigeria no be just a place somwia .
Nigeria na di pipo .
Di gud , di bad and di ugly """" na we make am be laidat .
Anytin wey dey affect di kontri , na we be di agent wey cause am .
If Nigeria na scam as Pastor Paul Adefarasin tok , den we all be scammers .
Even say I agree , say Adefarasin anger na becos of di love wey e get for di kontri , im comment say Nigeria na scam and fraud no dey reasonable .
If Nigeria na fraud ; den all of us be fraudster , leaders and followers join .
All of us don contribute to di dissapointment of di entity .
We dey live for a kontri wia pastors dey run dia ministry like business .
Dem dey run am like business enterprise but dem no dey pay tax for dere .
CAMA ; Government introduce a law wey go regulate di business undertaking of di religious industry and wey go bring som transparency and accountability inside di spiritual business .
But na pastors dey against dis law pass .
Still , na dis same pipo wey no wan follow di law be di loudest voice wen dem dey pass capital sentence on Nigeria .
Funny tin be say , dis pastors dey follow di law of oda kontri dey run dia church for dose kontri .
Dem dey submit dia finance for regular check by di authorities for UK , US and oda places .
But for Nigeria dem dey live above di law .
Pastor Chris Oyakhilome don dey spread harmful lies about COVID vaccine .
E claim say na di concoction of di anti - Christ .
Dem fine am 125 , 000 pounds for Uk , sake of say e dey tok harmful and unsubstantiated tins about di vaccine .
But for Nigeria wia e dey kontinue to bring different COVID conspiracy , dem neva call am to kom explain im offence , sake of say na man of god e be .
Maybe na why Nigeria be scam .
If Nigeria na scam , den na becos of pastors wey dey siddun for top , kom dey step on di law wey dey govern di land .
If Nigeria na fraud , den na becos of pastors wey dey sign agreement wit politicians everi election period ; dey campaign for dem on di altar , dey command di demons of hell untop dose wey no gree accept dia anointed candidate .
Clergymen dey as corrupt as di politikal class .
Also , civil servant , wey dey collect N150 , 000 per month , but get pikin for UK school , and property for all ova di major cities of di kontri , go abuse Nigeria and carry all im hypocrisy put for lamentation and insult to di state .
E go calm down ignore e own contribution for di corruption wey dey destroy di kontri .
Also , som citizens dey reject laws , rules and regulations .
Wia traffic light dey , dem go ignore am ; wia protocol dey , dem go bypass am , and for places wia dem don get standard for gud service delivery and operations , dem go abandon am .
Still , all of dem go blame Nigeria for di bad status quo as if say di kontri dey exist witout di pipo .
Di problem wey Nigeria get na pipo problem .
But di bad tin be say nobodi wan take responsibility for di terrible way wey tins be .
We dey blame di Nigeria wey no exist .
Na all of us get hand for inside di bad situation of Nigeria .
Instead make we dey follow di tin wey we don conclude about Nigeria , make we forsee goodness and positivity into di system , and make we dey work to make awa kontri di tin wey we want make e be .
Nigeria go be wetin we want make e be .
Di politicians get comma .
But dat na di reason why new generation of leaders must come up and take kontrol .
Nobodi fit free awa mind except us .
Citizenship na call to duty .
NIGERIA NO BE SCAM .
Why separation no be di Silver Bullet to Nigeria challenges
Di principle of self - determination as e dey for di UN charter wey awa pipo wey wan separate hold - on to , take effect for a time wey many pipo for di world dey under colonial yoke or oda form of kontrol by outside power .
Di principle na to give chance to independence and liberation movements so dem go fit gain dia freedom and determine dia path of future development .
For di world wey we dey today , dis principle only apply to few pipo , becos majority of di world don dey free from colonial kontrol and sef - governing .
So dem go need adjust di principle of sef - determination , wey dem establish under di UN charter , so e go fit accommodate di demand of awa pipo wey wan separate , becos if we follow wetin dey dere , dem no qualify .
First of all , dem go need to prove carefully and convincingly say di area wey dem claim to represent dey under som form of kontrol , and say dem dey lack di basic freedom wey everibodi suppose enjoy as e dey di UN charter .
And for wia dem wan prove dat one , dem go need convince di UN on di steps wey dem don take , from di national ( National Assembly ) , sub - regional ( ECOWAS ) and continental level ( AU ) to present dia case .
And di UN no go just take dia word laidat .
Dem go get committee wey go confam di fact to know weda true - true , Nigeria as a kontri dey practise di basic requirement of demokracy or not .
Dem don even complicate di case wit di fact say dose areas no be area wey dem dey fight untop , and no be area wey dey under any trusteeship wey go need UN referendum to give dem direct independence or ask dem who dem wan join inside di pipo wey dey fight untop di place .
If our secessionists cannot provide these basic requirements , the farthest their case could get within the UN system will predictably be the waste paper basket because the UN is not for frivolities .
E no dey give chance make som movement wey no know wetin dem dey about abuse im wide and transparent process .
Di case of marginalisation , wey dem mention as part of di reason for separation , dey too simple to waste awa time untop .
Na everi democratik system dey get winner and loser for election .
And as awa politikal system no perfect reach , di konstitution make am compulsory say as many ethnic group and geo - political zones as possible must get representative for government and im institutions .
E go tough for di pipo wey wan separate to convince di outside world say dia case of marginalisation dey more compelling pass dat of more dan 300 oda ethnic group wey dey Nigeria .
Wetin dis one mean be say , why di international community , wey di pipo wey wan separate dey report and seek support from go single out jus two out of like hundred of dat kind case wey dey ring for di Nigerian media say na im dem go work on ?
What makes their cases so special and urgent above those of others in Nigeria who have conversely chosen not to follow the path of secession ?
Out of all di three tins wey make awa secessionists dey agitate , no one dey convincing or compelling enough to justify dia action .
On di amalgamation argument , Nigeria own no be special case for Afrika or for di world .
If Nigeria go need break up unto say Britain no join am well , den dis go be di case of almost all di kontris for Afrika .
In short , if dem use dis principle , e go start di course to begin a new scramble for Africa by di old and upcoming world powers , and like befor , na Afrikans go be di victim .
Make we no deceive awasef , becos if di break - up of Nigeria happun ( God forbid ) , e go lead to di birth of kontris
wey go dey weak sotey , dem go dey beg from di foreign powers .
We don get som argument wey dey compare di break up of Nigeria wit dat of Eastern European states and di Balkans .
Untop dis one , e go beta make we undastand well say di tin wey work for Europe fit no work for Africa .
In di case of di kontris wey we mention , na part of di great geo - strategic games of di major world powers wey get direct cultural , economik and politikal link and interest for di emerging scenario .
And dis kontris don get clear boundary befor dem agree to kom togeda for mutual defence durin di uncertain situation of di Second World War .
Immediately di Soviet order , wey join dem togeda begin dey scatter , all dis kontris need go back to di status quo ante .
And , more importantly , dis developments get di backing and guarantee of di important powers for Europe and di world .
Se Nigerian secessionists get dat kind recognition and profile in di face of di principal powers of di world wey go make dem answer dem ?
Surely , di answer na zero .
Dis no kom mean say di agitation of pipo to separate for di kontri no get som gud reason .
Anybodi wey dey live for dis kontri wit dis rising case of insecurity , poverty , corruption , nepotism , economic uncertainty and di unbelievable incompetence and near criminal indifference of di government to dis challenges go conclude say truly , we dey for a kontri wey dey fail for im basic konstitutional duties and responsibilities .
And for a fragile kontri like awa own , wey get plenti fault , e dey normal for tendency or preference for separation to arise and grow fast wit di clear dysfunctionality of di government wey dey .
And na everybodi get dis dis feeling .
But as discouragin as di outlook be , and as temptin as di outcome dey appear , separation no fit be di solution to awa current challenge as a nation .
Indeed na prospect wey get som unknown dangers , danger wey no be for di secessionists alone but for di kontri as a whole .
Nigeria no dey perfect .
Even som of di advance kontris don show say despite dia years of existence and dia gud systems , dem no dey free from crises wey dey kom from internal conflict .
Make we no dey deceive awasef say as we dey try break up awa kontri , som kontris go graciously assist us .
Wetin dem go do na to give us di means to destroy and weaken awasef , so dem go fit benefit while we go suffer am .
Na di truth about di international system be dat .
As di popular German beamter tok for di beginnin of my paper ; Na we be awa own problem and solution join togeda .
We need put awa mind , talent and effort togeda to develop Nigeria instead say we wan breaking am .

Investin in young pipo : Ahmed Bobboi example
For July , 2017 , I get di honour to spend one evenin inside one British bank wey dem dey call Coutts , as part of di plenti activity wey dey for us as di 2017 Queen's Young Leaders .
U fit dey wonder say why I go dey write about event wey I go for place wey dry like bank .
Anyway , Coutts no be ordinary bank .
Apart from say na one of di eight oldest bank for di world ( dem start am som 329 years ago for 1692 ) , Coutts na private bank wey dey popular for im big customers like Her Majesty di Queen .
Inside di big hall , na two welcome us under a big dome for di centre of di building .
Na sharp - sharp I recognise one of di two men wey stand wit a familiar wide smile .
Na Sir John Major , befor - befor British Prime Minister and Chairman of di Queen Elizabeth Diamond Jubilee Trust .
We don meet befor , for one dinner wey dem organize for us for di Australian High Commission wey dey London , and na dere e congratulate us for awa recognition by Her Majesty .
Dem introduce di oda man to us as Lord William Waldegrave of North Hill .
Na im be di Chairman of di Board of Coutts Bank and Chairman of di Royal Mint Advisory Committee .
Dat evening dey full of entertainment ; eatin and drinkin .
E sweet well - well
But apart from di display and glamour , we tok and gist wit Lord Waldegarve and Sir Major , two outstandin leaders for di United Kingdom ( UK ) .
Dem show dia happiness to celebrate awa achievement , and dem describe us as special pipo .
Dem encourage us to develop awa skills more and create long legacy for awa kontri and di Commonwealth togeda .
Afta , I follow Sir Major and Lord Wadegrave yarn for private , I ask dem som question about public service , banking and finance , innovation and young pipo generally .
I learn a lot of tins from dem
and I komot for Coutts .
Dat night seriously inspire and motivate me more as a change agent , innovator and young leader for Nigeria .
Weda u dey for government , or u dey business , and especially as innovator or entrepreneur , I no fit tok am finish , how important dis kind inspiration fit be for di work wey u dey do .
Som pipo fit komot face for dis confirmation say e no dey relevant .
Dem don forget how dis kind tok fit be beta way of mentorship and motivation for upcomin leaders , and e fit serve as example for dem to see champions among pipo wey be like dem .
Di feeling of validation and motivation , wit guidance and support na necessary ingredient for everi leader , especially young pipo .
Di earlier awa older generation for Nigeria realise and accept dis culture of support and mentorship wit dia full chest , and truly celebrate awa achievements , di beta e go be for di future of dis kontri and di growin population of young pipo .
Make u forgive my digression .
Di reason why I dey narrate dis experience na say , since wey e don happun , I no experience dat kind tin again , until recently wen I siddun wit anoda public servant for Nigeria , di Executive Secretary of di Petroleum Equalisation Fund
( Management ) Board ( PEF - M - B ) , Alhaji Ahmed A Bobboi .
Even say oil and gas no be my main industry of discipline or practice , I get strong opinion say make pesin no sabi am dey very careless since di contribution of di sector to revenue
pass any oda sector for di kontri .
So I don dey try sabi wetin dey happun for di industry , even say I want make we shift and focus on non - oil sources of income .
I dey happy say I get di opportunity to yarn wit a crucial stakeholder like di executive , especially becos di organisation na pacesetter for di use of advance technology to improve efficiency and performance for di sector .
Howeva , wetin I gain from dis experience even dey more valuable pass my understanding of di industry more .
We discuss difrent topic ; from history to government , and from job creation to innovation and entrepreneurship .
E dey very excitin and refreshin , and e carry me straight go Coutts again .
I meet Mr Bobboi for di first time wen I join one team wey e follow kontrol , we dey work untop one regional entrepreneurship acceleration programme under di supervision of Massachusetts Institute of Technology ( MIT ) wia different community for di world join MIT for evidence - based practical approach to make di entrepreneurial ecosystems strongthroughinnovation .
I dey suprised by di vision and dedication wey dis go bring for PEF - M - B to dey involve for dis project , as e surely dey visionary and more beneficial to help build a formidable entrepreneurial ecosystem wit partner like MIT pass di ordinary Corporate Social Responsibility ( CSR ) programme wey most organization dey do , wey no dey get impact most times .
For dat particular encounter wey I get wit am , we yarn about awa two - years programme wit MIT and di big responsibility of truly acceleratin entrepreneurial development as remedy to lack of jobs and catalyst for prosperity .
The He spoke about various pain points for him as a leader and the approach to solve them .
One of di wonderful takeaway wey I collect na im idea about di National Youth Service Corps ( NYSC ) and how we fit use am serve young graduates and di nation beta .
Becos e don dey notice say som corps members wey dey serve for PEF - M - B dey always dey idle , di executive secretary tok say e don dey find way to ensure say di corp members no just dey engaged , but say dem komot wit skills and knowledge wey go last , and wey go give dem career wey pass government job .
Part of dis go be to do one big programme wey go turn dem to entrepreneurs wey get passion for innovation , througha dedicated and well planned innovation and enterprise trainin durin dia service year for PEF - MB .
Di honesty and sincere disposition of Mr . Bobboi dey visible and penetrating truout awa discussion and me sef kom get di strong will to do my best , no be only to kontinue dey innovate for different sector but to also dey ensure kontinuity for di inspiration and support of younger leaders and innovators , wey go fit make all di difference for awa dear kontri Nigeria .

In preparation of di July local government election for Lagos State , di rulin All Progressives Congress ( APC ) go conduct open primary for aspirants wey dey di 20 local government areas ( LGs ) and 37 local council development areas ( LCDAs ) , Daily Trust report .

We go rememba say 1050 aspirants wey be di combination of 250 chairmanship and 800 councillorship aspirant dey contest for di 434 positions wey dey di 57 LGs .
Di party don dey for confusion untop plenti aspirants , as dem dey set up screening committee wey go dey unda di supervision of di Deputy Governor , Dr Obafemi Hamza .
As at wen we dey write dis report , aspirants dey wait anxiously for di result of di screenin .

Daily Trust make us know say di party don already give di aspirants guideline befor di open primary wey go happun for local government wia consensus no fit happun .
As e dey for di guideline wey Daily Trust see , Accredited members go use open ballot vote for di venue , dem go stand for front of di poster of di candidate wey dem like , and
di candidate wey get di highest numba of votes na im dem go announce as di winner .
Afta di popular report say di APC National Leader and strongman for Lagos politics , Asiwaju Bola Ahmed Tinubu don endorse som candidate , di former governor don deny di claim , say im no get candidate wey im prefer .
For one chat wit Daily Trust , di Publicity Secretary of di state Caretaker Committee , Seye Oladejo tok say , di guidelines dey clear , say na open direct primary make dem do .
Di party dey strongly committed to internal demokracy and dem provide a level playin ground for all aspirants .

Technology don make professional farmers for China strong .
Human resources dey veri important for China rural vitalization .
Currently , na more dan 17 million high - class farmers dey work for villages , so dem go fit improve di rural areas .
Di knowledge of science wey Chinese farmers get don lay solid foundation for dia general development and e dey give stronger support for di kontri rural economy .
Bao Yuan na young man wey get aquatic product company wey e establish 2014 for Qujing , Yunnan province for southwest China afta e graduate from Yunnan Normal University for 2014 .
E tok say """" Artificial breedin no just dey give pipo option of different choice , e also dey protect different kind of fish wey don dey komot for water .
Song Xueqin na Gen Y female wey don get name for North China Lvliang Mountains ,
for Shanxi province sake of say she sabi different flat peach graftin technique .
Afta she graduate from college , Song don do different businness like catering , gypsum processin and rearing of sheep , but she no make am for any of dis business .
For 2009 , she hear say dem fit turn Chinese wild peach to flat peachthroughgraftin , na so she tell one of her friend say make dat one help am bring flat peach scion from di independent Uygur region , Xinjiang province of Northwest China .
Afta , she invite one expert say make e kom teach am di tins wey she need to know .
Afta 1 year , Song and her husband graft flat peach scions on more dan 4 , 000 wild peach for one hillside near Hetaozhang village , Fenxi County , for Shanxi province , but di result no good .
Afta she konsult di relevant materials and experts , she finally realize wetin cross - pollination be .
Di yield go only go up wen di type wey dem join togeda match .
She yarn .
Last year , di woman collect di first certificate for her life , a certificate for new professional farmers .
Rural areas no dey eva lack resources .
Recently , as pipo standard of living dey high , dem dey get larger demand for fresh and high - quality agricultural products .
Zuo Chenming wey be senior researcher for AliResearch , a research branch of Alibaba Group tok say """" Dis trend dey make more and more educated entrepreneurs wey get technical skill and know how to do businesses , to go back to di rural area .
For early morning , Mi Xiaohong from Yuzhong County , Lanzhou , Gansu province for Northwest China start work for cowshed , she dey clean di cowshed , and give di cow new feed and water .
E no easy to make cow feed , becos we need calculate how many grass and oda materials wey we go add for inside .
We go need to know di ratio of bran , glacial flour and salt , wey go dey inside .
She tell People's Daily , say dem go need dey adjust di ingredients wey dey inside di as di cow dey grow .
Mi , dey always go trainin programs wey di County government organise , and she don turn specialist for cattle husbandry .
I divert plenti times wen I still be novice , but now my fellow villagers dey always come meet me for advice .
She add am join say , na onlythroughkontinuous learnin she go fit solve more problems .
Today , local authorities all ova China don dey give new policy and technique to make sure say farmers study new technologies .

For Gansu Province , dem dey organise trainin session for di leaders of professional cooperative and coordinators of animal epidemic prevention .
All dis na effort to bring technology to di farm and find solution to agric problems .

Rice sufficiency : Nigeria get long way to go Expert
Dr Philip Idinoba , wey be rice commodity specialist for AfricaRice , don show im consign untop di increasin population wey dey affect Federal Government effort to boost rice production .
Idinoba yarn dis one for interview wit News Agency of Nigeria ( NAN ) for Gombe on Tuesday .
E tok say government need to invest more on rice , so e go fit boost Nigeria food security .
As e yarn , di government dey do plenti tins to boost rice production , sake of say na staple food , but di growin population of di kontri dey bring down di effort .
E tok say di rate of urbanisation , wey be one of di key factors of rice consumption for Nigeria , dey veri high pass di rate wey we take dey use plant rice .
Nigeria still get long way to go for rice sufficiency .
We dey make effort everi yearthroughdi Anchor Borrowers Programme , special intervention programme and oda donor funded projects .
All dis na to bring som tins wey go help farmers increase dia yield and productivity .
But even wit all dis Federal Government effort , di numba of new mouth wey dey join evri year cancel all dis improvement .
Idinoba yarn .
Plenti tins to do
Di agronomist add am join say we need to do plenti tins by increasin awa investment , especially for dry season farmin .
As Idinoba tok , we fit take advantage of dry season farmin to boost rice productivity .
We go get beta result for rice production if we fit close di gaps wey dry season dey always cancel for rice cultivation .
E yarn say , if u get eight million farmers wey dey plant rice for wet season , and only two million out of dem dey plant rice for dry season , den di effort never reach yet .
Idinoba , wey still be water management specialist , advise farmers wey dey areas wit flood for di kontri say make dem plant di kind seed wey go fit tolerate flood and go fit survive for water between three to four weeks .
He tok am say All dis varieties , wey dem release three years ago , and still dey multiply by di National Seeds Council of Nigeria , wit oda seeds companies , dey available , and farmers go fit get am .
Dis year , wit di kind tori wey we hear from farmers for Kebbi , Jigawa and Adamawa wey use dis kind varieties , u fit no get complete failure laidat .
Derefor , make we combine dis kind technology go help one way .
Di rice specialist add am say for dose kind areas , improvement go need dey di cropping environmentthroughdi construction of water structures to kontrol , retain or evacuate water .
