Wetin Kano need for 2023
Kano need create new path to development for 2023 .
Dis na becos di state don dey enta di pit of poverty .
Awa rich pre - colonial history show say na Kano rich pass for all di Hausa states , becos di state dey involve for di economy .
Even say di colonialists destroy di economic foundation of Kano and oda society wey dem colonise , di policy of di pipo wey lead di Native Authority from 1926 to 1963 contribute to make Kano remain as di leadin economic centre of Northern Nigeria .
For example , dem establish di first modern water treatment plant wey dey di region for 1931 , di first independent power plant for Northern Nigeria , wey get 15MW , and for more dan 80 years , dem neva establish any one wey resemble am for Northern Nigeria .
Dem establish di first industrial estate wey dey di Northern Region , dem inherit only one primary school for 1926 , and for 1963 everi village don get primary school ( more dan hundred ) , dem establish secondary schools , dem no meet any hospital ( except one dispensary ) and for 1963 dem don build two general hospital and more dan hundred dispensaries for everi village .
Na dem lay di foundation of modern Kano .
Politikally , na dem make di NPC becom di rulin party for Nigeria .
From 1966 to 1979 and 1984 to 1999 , Kano still maintain im position as di second to Lagos .
Kano no get kontrol ova macro - economic policy but e leaders fit provide di right environment for economic growth .
For example , di Dawanau Market , wey still be di biggest grain market for West Africa , e dey bring pipo from all part of di kontinent , even from far place like Gabon and Congo .
All dis na result of di foresight wey Alhaji Bashari Garko ( may Allah bless im soul ) , wey establish di market get .
Di three administration wey don rule Kano from 1999 till today , fit claim say all of dem be di best tin wey don happun to Kano , but why Kano don reduce to numba nine for Nigeria ?
One single project no dey wey don bring correct economic change for Kano , even afta plenti effort of consign pipo .
If di elite dey focus and determine , wit state leadership as e dey for di pre - colonial period , Kano no go go down to numba nine for Nigeria wit GDP of $ 13 . 30b afta Lagos ( $ 46 . 03b ) , Rivers ( $ 32 . 14b ) , Delta ( $ 25 . 48b ) , Oyo ( $ 21 . 64b ) , Imo ( $ 20 . 64 ) , Edo ( $ 17 . 50b ) , Akwa Ibom ( $ 15 . 26 ) and Ogun ( $ 13 . 82 ) .
If we no prevent am now , we no go fit imagine di disaster wey go kom in di next 10 years .
Dis na becos of many reasons .
One of dem be say we get more dan four million pupils for public basic schools ( primary and JSS ) and by 2033 dem go don finish secondary education .
Assume say na onli 10 percent of dem ( 400 , 000 ) go go higher - level , di government go fit sponsor dia education ?
Afta dem complete higher education , di economy go fit give dem beta employment ?
As e be so , e no fit .
Dis na becos , more dan 250 medical doctors and more dan 1000 nurses wey di state government dey sponsor , na im dem no fit employ .
We go dey deceive awasef wit di skills acquisition programme wey dey train artisans wey no go get any job afta dem learn di skills , sake of say di local economy no fit employ dem .
Everi day we dey hear billions wey federal government allocate for one economic programme or di oda , and still , we no dey reason pass to train plumbers , carpenters , mechanics etc .
Since , awa idea no dey about how we go use resources employ di large population as Gajimasu ( 1095 - 1135 ) do wen e begin di city walls .
We need tink outside di box .
Kano no need genius wey get di best qualification and experience , or saint as di next governor .
Dis na becos di governors wey dey for di last 20 years get som of di best quality , and dem fit even don do dia best , but as all of us dey see , di result no be di best for di state .
So , we need reason outside di box .
Di two parties , APC and PDP no fit provide di kind leadership wey we want , sake of say na godfathers dey kontrol dem , and dem no get idea on wetin to do , but dia main focus na how to share di state resources .
Di best tin wey dem fit do na to negotiate for governor wey go serve di interest of a godfather or cabal .
So , di two parties no be di best option .
Beta pesin fit kom outside on e own , or wit di help of oda beta patriotic pipo .
E fit use any way win , even if e negotiate wit any of di two parties or anoda party sef .
E dey possible
E don happun befor .
One example wey dey near us na Nasir Elrufai for Kaduna State .
Im be one of di best for im generation , but di security situation for di state don pass im power , sake of say e dey depend on im personal intelligence and capacity .
Pesin wey beta pass am for Kano no go make di place beta unless dem change som important tins .
I no claim say I get all di answer or even say na me get all di idea wey dey down .
Som of dem na part of Aminu Kano idea .
Plenti beta idea dey for di mind of more intelligent pipo .
Di idea wey I dey suggest na base on my small experience as labourer of politicians and som trainin wey I get outside dis kontri .
Right now , Kano dey crossroad , and dis ideas fit dey useful .
Som pipo need kom togeda to organise one political movement wey no dey in kontrol of anybodi but pipo wey wan sacrifice .
Make dem look di suggestion below :
Need dey for us to start political organisation at di lowest level and make sure say na di members dey in kontrol .
Material reward no go dey , but sacrifice .
Dis dey possible wit mobilisation and di right message .
Befor di election , di movement or party need take detail inventory of di state and design comprehensive action plan wit specific targets wey dey measurable .
Operational guidelines go dey for all appointees plus di governor , and dem go need announce am so every citizen go fit know and challenge , if dem no follow am .
Anybodi wey dey find position inside di movement or party , go begin from di lowest level to di highest .
Som pipo go argue say dis strategy go kill ambition .
Wetin we need now no be ambition but sustainable system wey dey in kontrol of di pipo .
Also , make dem no give anybodi any position unless e don fulfil som basic condition of competence and honesty , and e go bring reference and guarantor .
All public officers must declare dia asset publicly , and dia family members own join , immediately dem reach office .
And forensic experts go need verify everytin .
From time to time , di public need dey know dia salary and expenses ( plus travel , entertainment etc ) .
Anybodi wey becom governor or reach any position no go ever do tins on e own .
Di governor no go ever
Make appointment alone .
Criteria , go dey , dem go need set expectation or target for dose kind appointment , and dem go need dey assess and evaluate am from time to time .
All contract wey dem go award go dey fair and transparent , and expert inside and outside di government bureaucracy must evaluate am .
Allocation of plots must dey transparent too .
No governor go get total kontrol of di treasury and na competent staff go dey in charge .
Di governor go be di leader wey go guide all di institution to develop and end one - man rule .
If di governor dey free from dis prison of power , e go lead di state to greatness .
E go lead by example and corruption go reduce becos dem don block all di way wey e fit use abuse power .
Governor suppose dey to supervise public servants and make sure say everybodi do im duty well .
E suppose inspire im pipo wit good lifestyle , commitment to service and transparency .

Niger republic and 6 oda kontries don lose di right to vote for UNGA - Guterres
UN Secretary - General Antonio Guterres don tok say Niger and six oda nations don lose dia right to vote for di United Nations General Assembly ( UNGA ) , sake of say dem neva pay dia dues .
Di oda kontris wey lose dia UNGA votin right na ; Iran , Libya , di Central African Republic , Congo Brazzaville , South Sudan and Zimbabwe , di Jerusalem Post report on Tuesday .
Three more kontris """" Comoros , Sao Tome and Principe and Somalia """" go get di chance to kontinue to vote , even say dem no pay dia dues too , but sake of say dem show say dem no get di capacity to pay .
Guterres write letter give di General Assembly President , Volkan Bozkir of Turkey say dem go suspend di UNGA votin right of kontris wey dey owe di UN , accordin to di UN Charter .
Di Charter tok say make dem suspend di votin right , if one member state no pay im fees for more dan two years .
Inside di article , a member - state wey owe dues wey dey equal or pass di amount of im contribution for two years fit lose im vote for di General Assembly .
Iran dey owe 16 . 2 million dollars , money wey pass any oda kontri own .
Meanwhile , Iran don blame U . S , say na dia sanctions no make di Islamic Republic pay im contribution to di UN .
Iran Foreign Ministry tok - tok pesin , Saeed Khatibzadeh yarn say di money wey dem wan use pay UN dey frozen for two South Korean banks , sake of U . S . sanctions .
E tok say di Islamic Republic get a total of USD 7 billion for dose banks , di report tok .
Khatibzadeh tok say make di UN guarantee dem say dem go transfer di payments successfully witout using U . S . banks .
Sake of say di United States don seize Iran international asset befor , di Islamic Republic of Iran don insist say make di UN no use any American bank receive awa kontri membership fee .
As an alternative , dis organization dey guarantee di financial transfer channel , Iran International News quote Khatibzadeh .
BREAKING : Paris Saint - Germain win French Cup
Paris Saint - Germain don win di French Cup as dem beat Monaco 2 - 0 for Wednesday
final wey dem play for di Stade de France .
Goal wey Mauro Icardi and Kylian Mbappe score won a largely uninspiring final for PSG who now go into the weekends final round of Ligue 1 fixtures with a record - equalling 10th league title still a possibility .
The French champions have now won the French Cup six times in the last seven seasons having reached the final every year since 2015 .
It was also the second trophy of coach Mauricio Pochettinos managerial career after he won the Champions Trophy for PSG in January , although this will for many count as his first major honour .
We work every day to experience this kind of feeling , reward and recognition , said Mbappe .
Its the work of a whole group , staff , all the people who work every day for us , the club and of course the supporters who couldnt be there .
We think a lot about the fans and this title is for them as well .
Monaco meanwhile continue their wait to win the French Cup for the first time since 1991 , in their first final since 2010 when they were also beaten by PSG .
Niko Kovacs side have however had a positive season and can finish it on a happier note at the weekend by qualifying for the Champions League for the first time since 2018 .

Chairman for di economic and financial crimes commission ( EFCC ) Abdulrasheed Bawa don make declaration say dem go resuscitate di Bank Employees Assets Declaration Act of 1986 to block loopholes wey bankers don create to sanitise di kontri's financial system
According to wetin Bawa tok , dem take di decision due to di role wey dem dey expect make bankers play for di fight against corruption , as di EFCC don mandate am to ensure say dem comply wit di Act .
Section 1 for di Bank Employees Declaration of Assets Act 1986 don make am mandatory for Evri employee for di bank to make full disclosure of assets upon employment for annual basis .
Di law wey dey under Section 7 Sub - Section 1 stipulates say na offence e go be for an employee of a bank make e own assets in excess of dia legitimate and probable income
Afta di EFCC chairman don stipulate di deadline , consequences go arise as a result of non - declaration by bank employees
Spelt out penealty of 10 years inprisonment upon conviction as well as forfeiture of assets wey dey beyond and above legitimate income and probable earnings for dat kain bank employees .
Dis piece of legislature don dey so tey 1986 under di military
So tey , dis part of di constitution don dey ineeffective by those wey suppose dey implement am ordinarily
Bankers don aware of dis legislation but di level wey dem dey comply no dey encouraging
For di 80s , dem dey hand form to bankers wey dem go complete and submit
But as e dey go for awa kontri , dem don abandon di implementation of dat provision for di law , and dem no longer consideram as a fundamental part for di banking profession .
Stakeholders dey blame di failure on top di authorities wey include di CBN , Chartered Institute of Bank of Naija ( CIBN ) and Bankers Committee for some kain abnormalities wey dey di industry .
According to wetin dem dey tok , dem say diz regulators dey rely on di bank wey dem suppose supervise , make e supply information
For instance , dem don argue am say di failed banks episode apun some months afta dem give di regulator for diz banks clean bill of health
Dis suggest say dem don doctor di information wey di bank supplied
Naija don dey battle case like corruption and money laundering and dem dey accuse bankers and banking officials say dem be part of it
Some moni don remain redundant for plenti accounts bikos some account owners don kpeme which some bank officials go convert to dia own as dem go leave families of di account owners for penury .
Dis dey in spite of di fact say di banking sector no strange to self - regulation , given its tempting , delicate and di operating system wey dey fragile
Di CIBN Act of 2007 don dey regulate di banking system
E get code of conduct wey bankers don agree pon wit CBN
Disciplinary tribunal wey get power for di high court dey and e dey ensure say dem bring reported infractions , unethical conduct and indiscipline before di tribunal , and sanctions wey dem recommended for formal prosecution .
But one of di challenges be di weak reporting system wey bankers get wey dey lead to di inability of CIBN make dem take appropriate actions .
Di spirit wey stan gidigba for di back of di Act of 1986 na to make clear , di financial standing wey bank employee get for di time of employment , and afta years of service , in a bid wey go make dem ascertain say dem dey commensurate dia legitimate earnings wit dia lifestyles wey dey current
Na dis dey kom on top di heels of allegation say some bankers be direct beneficiaries for fraudulent transactions wey dem dey carry out for di bank
Wetin be common knowledge be say di declaration of assests by public officers wey include di civil servants , pesin wey dey politically exposed and those wey dey for di Ministries , Departments and Agencies ( MDAs ) .
Dem require dem make dem declare dia assets evri four years
On top di election and appointment of political office holders , before dem assume office dem suppose declare di assets wey dey get pon entry kom declare am again for di exit point
Dem do dis declaration by oath
For anoda word , execution and attestation before di high court or some oda superior officer for di law dey
Di Naija customs service ( NCS ) , Naija Immigration Service ( NIS ) , among odas , dem don covered by di Code of Conduct Act wit regard to di declaration of dia assets .
As e dey so finacial experts believe say di impression wey di directive to bankers create make dem comply wit di of legislation wey dey pre - exist dey amount to stigmatisation and e dey also isolates bank employees , wey dey puts dem in di limelight .
In oda words , d belief of revisiting of di Act of 1986 dey encourage di policy of isolation wey dey kos apprehension in di industry .
Dis na di concern say di Act fit kos enrolment into di banking profession to further go down as a result of stigmatisation .
Some stakeholders don caution against di drama about stigmatisation , arguing say plenti bankers , from di highest cadre to di level wey low pass , dey live above dia means .
According to wetin dem tok , an average banker even from dia early point of calling , dey cut corners by conniving wit customers say dem go beat di system .
Dem insist say for evri major corruption , banker wey dey facilitate di transaction dey
E dey laudible say di EFCC dey try use di Act for reason wey good
Di worry be say di banks wey di goment no own per se although di goverment get shares in dem
Dem dey use bank save moni
Di koko be say laws wey dey check illicit enrichment dey
Article 20 for di UN Convention Against Corruption dey explicit on top dis
Section 7 for di EFCC act don empower EFCC make e dey investigate pesin wey hin lifestyle no commensurate wit di means of income wey dem get
Dem believe am for some part say di politically exposed person dey plunder di assests for dis kontri plenti of dem dey untouchable
Dem accuse EFCC say e no fair and even - handed
If dem sanitise di banking sector , we go get ripple effect for oda sectors of di economy
Dem take all diz measure to strengden di fight against corruption , and not to stigmatise di banking profession or portray it as di scapegoat wey dey witin di system .
Besides , di banking career no be one kain rouguish profession
Some bankers be di forefront of exposing some of di mega corruption issues wey wedon see di EFCC making headway .
Part of why dis law dey be say e dey ensure make di kontri dey free from financial crimes , and make e dey also block loopholes wey unscrupulous players dey esploit
While dem dey hope say make di Act of 1986 na sincere attempt at sanitising di system , dem suppose create platform wey go report thresholds of deposits on a daily basis , and di regulator suppose dey able to access it to know di declarations wey dem make .
E dey make am easy reference to wetin dem don declare as legitimate income to check those wey dey live above dia means

Rabbit farming don boom for plateau
Di secretary , Plateau Rabbit Breeders Association , Mr Pam Gyang tok say rabbit farming don bikom popular for di state wit plenti residents engaging in it .
Gyang tok am for an interview wit di News Agency of Naija on Tuesday for Jos , say e don bikom a household business just like poultry farming .
Gyang tok say plenti trainnig outfits wey dey involved for di breeding and selling of live rabbit don spring up across di state .
Di secretary tok say rabbit rearing na lucrative business wey fit increase pesin income and impact positively on di economy .
Hin tok say rabbits dey highly fertile and farmers dey sell according to dia weight as e dey range from N1 , 800 to N5 , 000 or even more
Hin tok say for di lockdown wey COVID - 19 occassioned families dey kom farm kom request for rabbits cages and rabbits to startup farms for dia backyards .
Hin say di high demand for rabbits meat so tey di numerous health benefit over red meat don arouse di interest of plenti farmers .
Gyang say di get low mortality rate and e require minimal handling adding say plenti pipo don invest in rearing dem so e go meet international market standard .
Hin say , awa rabbit meat don go as far as London and we go still export dem weneva dem demand for dem
Hin tok am say farmers dey generate resources from di sale of di hide and skin of rabbit for textile industries and hin faeces na source of fertilizer .

Farmers don raise concern as CBN don suspend anchor Borrowers loans
Farmers and oda stakeholders for di agricultural sector dey express dia concern over di suspension of agricultural loans wey dem dey access through di Naija Incentive - Based Risk Sharing System for Agricultural Lending ( NIRSAL ) by di Central Bank of Naija ( CBN ) recently
I dey think say una dey run / jappa for me
E dey handle most of di agric loans to di farmers by di CBN especially its popular Anchor Borrower Programme ( ABP ) .
Di apex bank say di fraudulent activities for NIRSAL loans under di ABP and dem order for di suspension of such loans until dem don pay all previous beneficiaries back .
E no dey clear yet if di suspension dey only on di Anchor Borrowers Programme alone or e also include those of Micro finance banks through NIRSAL .
Di suspension don ground loan activities fror NIRSAL and farmers dey worried say among odas , di timing dey wrong , as many of dem don go far wit plans say dem go expand dia agricultural production
One farmer wey dey really worried say wetin dey apun now dey threaten di economy and e dey call on top di CBN make dem please step in and save millions of Naija pipo make dem access diS loans for agricultural production .
Plenti farmers wey dey wait for NIRSAL disbursement for di social media handle don express sadness over di suspension of di loan facility as e dey threaten to ground dia dreams for expansion .
As hin dey react to di development for di chat wit awa Agric Editor , di leadership of all di farmers association of Naija , wey Architect Kabiru Ibrahin dey head am , tok say thoughdi CBN dey blames NIRSAL for di non - performance of di ABP , make dem do di needful in fishing out those wey dey responsible .
Make e dey kontinu to provide qualified farmers di support wey dem need
We dey urge di CBN make dem do due dilligence in prequalifying farmers wey dey participate for di programme bikos several cases of briefcase farmers wey dey pose as real farmers abound .
Dem collude wit some NIRSAL officials make dem defraud di programme
Timely repayment no dey forthkoming for di ABP bikos of di fraud
Anyone wey give bribe to take a loan wit an interest component no get desire to repay am
awa initial understanding of di role of di NIRSAL na to primarily incentivize commercial banks make dem embrace lending for agricultural production but certainly no be to prequalify prospective loan seeking companies .
dis na how corruption take take over and di farmers now be di worst for it
Hin say we dey call on top di CBN make e reverse di decision on top di disbursement of di ABP support to farmers
Dr Femi Oke wey be di AFAN chairman for South - west zone say di suspension of di NIRSAL loans go impact food production for di kontri greatly
As Oke dey follow di News Agency of Naija ( NAN ) for Lagos don urge di CBN make dem investigate di allegations wey dey against NIRSAL witout undermining di various efforts wey farmers get toward achieving food security and self - sufficiency .
Hin call on top di CBN make dem resolve di issues wey dey surround di suspension of di NIRSAL loans
Di AFAN official say dem disappointed plenti farmers by di suspension of di Anchor Borrowers Programme ( ABP ) and NIRSAL loans , as dem dey provide a lot of support to smallholder farmers .
NAN also reported say di CBN recently suspend all loans wey di NIRSAL disburse following di allegation of corruption by its officials
Wetin dey una mind

for wetin we hear , dem base di suspension for di ABP

hin say , e no good and we dey implore make goverment chook mouth for di mata and address am

Dem need do something immediately make e no go jeopardise di effort of di farmers say dem ready to go back to di farm
Plenti farmers specifically in di South - West dey wait on top di loan and dem dey expect say by now dem suppose disburse am
Very few of awa members don get access to di loan , plenti neva get access to di interview
me self neva do di interview
I still dey wait make dem select me
hin stressed am say , farmers no dey hapi on top di suspension of loan

Hunger , poverty and di challenge for innovative food storage
Gimme evrithin wey una get
If una visit plenti offices across di kontri for lunchtime during di months of may , june , july and August , chances dey high say una go find a good number of workers wey dey munch am for mouth .
True as corn don dey season one of di delicacies for dis time na di combination of roasted corn ( wey dem popularly code - name as mouth organ ) and di pear for Africa pear .
Coconut na ocassional substitute wey dey close to pear dis writer get good authority ova am say plenti pipo dey find di coconut and a mouth - organ combination say e delicious
Outside dis months wey corn and pear dey season di combination no dey dey available
During di harvest months enough corn and pear wey go sustain di kontri for a substantial period , perhaps na an entire year , dem go don harvest am
But wit inadequate knowledge and how dem go utilize modern and cost - effective storage and preservation methods , tonnes of maize and pear just dey waste Evri year .
Di same dey apply to oda agricultural commodities for Naija
For harvest periods , surplus dey often dey , but in di absence of proper storage , a huge proportion of dis harvest dey waste .
Dis perennial issues don pose one huge threat to di economic well - being of farmers , di major wey dey operate for di subsistence level .
Di challenge wey be di kwanta of poor storge and preservation of food dey pose to awa kontri , don bekom more haunting wen pesin dey consider di difficulties wey confront us for di post - COVID era
E dey imperative say beyond di volume of awa agricultural output wey dey improve make we look critically at how we go empower farmers across di kontri manage dia harvests beta
Na dis go translate to immense economic value not only to di farmers demselves wey go enhance dia livelihoods , but also to di kontri as a whole , as plenti food go dey available for extended periods , for consumption and export
Plenti research organisations and universities don introduce different solutions to di kwanta of post - harvest losses as di years dey pass
Di innovations wey dem don develop , being home - grown dey unique bikos dem dey reflect di reality of awa local goverment
No be say dem dey relatively cheap , as dem dey often dey technically uncomplicated , but farmers fit adopt dem readily
For di area of fish farming , one innovation dey wey dem dey call am iced - fish box wey dem go use harvest fish go store am so e go remain fresh on transportation to di market from di farm or ahead of processing and storage .
Dem don develop special smoking kilns wey go replace di labour - intensive , traditional fish smoking methods wey no dey efficient and e dey unhealthy
Outputs wey dey commot for dis kilns be good enough for export and e dey several multiples of wetin dem dey ordinarily obtain for traditional fish - smoking methods .
Naija researchers don also produce composite packaging material wey dem fit use package dat kain smoked fish or even smoked meat as di case fit be , preserving di end - product and e dey boost di commercial appeal
If to say na beans , corn or rice wey don discoloured , mouldy , smelly or e dey infected wit weevils , grains dey pose gbege of storage for farmers and e dey lead to considerable financial losses
For di past , grains wey dem dey export from Naija don face rejection bikos of di unacceptable level of residual pesticides wey dem contain
Local researchers wey dey active for di area of grain preservation , churning out of a handful of innovative solutions ova di years
For instance , solar dryers wey dem develop for different products dey
If to say di abundance of sunshine wey dey awa kontri and di simplicity of construction of dis dryers , dem dey available for average farmers
Dem fit replicate construction easily for di local setin
Dis solar dryers work dey enhance di efficiency of drying of agricultural produce
Dem dey do dis as dem dey concentrate di rays of di sun on a particular surface , wey go dey enhance drying efficiency over di traditional method wey dem dey take use spread grains , cassava , plantain peeling and odas indiscriminately under di sun
local researchers don develop specially constructed steel drums wey wen dem shut am bikom airtight ( hermit ) and e dey allow make farmers store grains ova several months
Dem be specialised storage silos wey fit help store and preserve grains over plenti months
In fact one twin silo dey , wey fit accommodate 100 tonnes of grains at a time
Local researchers don also develop bio - pesticide as an alternative to chemical pesticides
Chemical pesticides wey dey available though effective against pest dey harmful to man and hin environment , too
Bio - pesticide for di oda hand , dey much safer and dem dey constitute no hazard for environment
Dem make One of such pesticide ( NSPRIDUST ) wey be an innovation by di Naija stored product research institute , from diatomaceous earth , wey be a powdery form wey dey occure for rock naturally for Naija
Bio - pesticides go help make Naija grains potentially dey more acceptable for di export market
We no fit leave fruit and vegetable out of di problem of poor preservation and storage for Naija
As we dey import apple , pears , strawberries and oda fruits round - di - clock plenti no dey wey we go yarn on top Naija's fruit exports
Again , over time Naija researchers don herald different solutions to dis yawa wey dey ground
One shed wey dem construct specially for fruit and vegetable for instance , wey dem make of simple and raw materials wey be local ones , and e dey help farmers preserve fruits and vegegtables for long
Den , di fruit dryer , wey dey dry certain fruits dey help to preserve dem
Local researcher dey work fervently on top fruits and vegetable conservation using di principle of evaporative cooling
Evaporative cooling na di cooling wey dey result make water evaporate from a surface
Incidentally , di use of evaporative cooling for fruit and vegetable preservation no be new thing , as dem don dey practice am for traditional setin for Naija
Researchers don dey find way wey dem go take use enhance di efficiency of traditional evaporative cooling systems wey dem go use preserve di shelf life of fruits and vegetables ova a duration of time
For tubers of yam and potatoes , local researchers don kom up wit products like ventilated yam barns wey go dey store yam tubers , diffused - light store wey go dey for di storage of potatoes , cassava root warehouse wey go dey store cassava roots among odas
Doubt no dey say widespread adoption of dis technologies by farmers across di kontri go help to considerably stem di tide of post - harvest losses for Naija
Na dis , one suppose repeat go transalate to significant economic value wey no go be for only farmers and di agricultural chain rate wey wide but also for di entire kontri as well
To get di agricultural value chain make e increasingly adopt diz innovations go entail patient and sysyematic engagement
Farmers cooperatives and association go be good medium wey go help reach farmers across di kontri wit information and education
na so di media and media institutions
Research institutes and faculties for agriculture for awa various universities , wey be vital hotbeds for innovation , go work collaboratively so tey dem go jointly share and popularise innovations wey dem dey emanate diafrom
Agricultural chambers for commerce be potential source of popularising dis innovations especially as e dey among policymakers and influencers suppose be involved also
Di increasing penetration of smartphones across di kontri also present opportunity wey go reach millions of farmers wit information and education
Pessu na di executive director for Naija stored products research insitute for Ilorin

As di Federal Goment open four land borders last week don slow down keepkeep wey dem dey do for katsina , Daily Trust fit tok .
Before dom shout am , pipo wey dey sell grains go disquise say dem be agent from company kom buy bigbig farm produce keep to store and get profit later .
As one dealer take tok , despite say dem match leg ontop to dey carry rice and other food enter Nigeria , market pipo still get double mind to keep market ontop say goment fit change dia mind anytime depend on wetin dey ground .
Alhaji Aminu Hussain , wey dey sorghum , say to dey keepkeep market no be new tin for di market , but e kom go up wit di new agricultural policy of dis administration and border wey dem close .
Many of us chop beta gain ontop farm produce for last year , na why pipo kom out quick dis harvest time to dey buy keep but border wey dem open don slow am down .
The fear wey we get na say price for food go still kom down .
E add join say farm produces wey no kom out plenti bikos of bad way of dem bandit dis year , don give market pipo mind to keepkeep dia market .
Rice , maize and sorghum n aim dem put eye .
Mallam Muhammadu Tarzana , wey dey sell grain for Bakori market , say as dem shout to open border again last week don get hand ontop price for major food for di market .
E no be like last year we , by dis time , maize dey around N8 , 000 and N9 , 500 , sorghum dey N7 , 000 , nah N14 , 000 and N13 , 000 dem dey sell dem now .
Dis shout of open border again wey dem shout down spoil di price of paddy rice from N14 , 000 go N12 , 000 , sorghum from N14 , 500 go N13 , 000 and maize from N15 , 500 go N14 , 000 .
Tarzana add join say many market pipo comot hand to dey buy market bigbig afta dem shout am , get am for mind say di breeze from importation of food go enta anytime .
Our news pipo see say di land border wey dem open again get many eyes .
Plenti of di farmer and market pipo want make di border dey lock so dat dem go dey chop beta for di market wey we dey do for awa house .
Pipo wey dey chop am and some other pipo hapi wit di development and dey expect say goment go allow make dem dey import rice and other food .
But goment kon fall dia hand as im tok say rice , chicken and turkey , oil for cook and other food still dey under ban to dey import .
Sani Muazu Hunkuyi , wey be one agric expert , beg di goment make dem sumit give di pressure , allow food to dey enter .
Goment don invest plenti agric sector and make we nor allow dat big investment enta water wit breeze of importation inside dis kontri
Na true say fear for food crisis don burst evriwia , but we fit reduce am wit farming wit water .
To dey import food go make dis economic recession wey dey di kontri worst to tackle , na im Muazu tok
E add join say yawa go gas for farmers dem if goment cancel dia policy ontop to make food plenti .
Why rice wey flood nor dey important to farmers dem .
Di threat ontop food for Nigeria bikos of flood go soon be tin of di past as dem release FARO 66 , one type of rice wey flood no fit kari .
FARO 66 , wey National Cereal Research Institute ( NCRI ) release give farming pipo dem be type wey get some tins wey dey different from wetin farmers for here sabi before .
Dis type tall pass other one wey farmers sabi .
Witi how im tall and some betabeta farming mata , e get power to survive palava of flood wella .
To kolet new tins among farmers dem dey always be big problem and as dem introduce FARO66 no dey different .
But if dem farmer kolet am finish , di threat ontop food about rice mata go reduce .
For dis year field trip wey NCRI station for Birnin Kebbi , capital of Kebbi State organise , farmers and dem oga dey introduced to dis new type afta a field trip wey dem do for di institute demonstration farm for di city .
For di demonstration farm , farmers dey expose to FARO66 , wey stand gidigba wit flood inside farm and other rice follow di same flood waka .
Di two farm wey dey near each oda show di power to tanda wit flood wey FARO66 type get , wit all di wahala , e grow and strong .
One di farm of other type of rice , na di remaining of rice wey die remain dem see .
As im follow awa news pipo talk , di oga for di NCRI station for Birnin Kebbi , Andrew Shema , say di FARO 66 go tanda wit flood if dem quick plant am .
E add join say , im stem wey hard and as e tall , if dem part am quick , di type go don grow reach size wey be say if flood com , di plant nor go gree for am .
He tok say FARO66 dey release two years ago but to kolet , as for di case wit any new tin , must be small small , tok say , if farmers dem don accept am wella , flood nor go be threat to rice farming again .
As im take tok , to open di eyes of farmers dem as research ontop dis new type dey go front , dem carry dem join bodi to see how e dey go and to record result .
E add join say science pipo wey dey ontop di research get sense say if dem allow farmers dem to see how dis plant fit take tanda wit flood , no be only to accept am go dey fast , to dey use sef go dey .
Shema wey tok say as dem nor give dem plenti moni be dia major wahala for di research work , e call stakeholders dem to kom invest ontop dia idea for beta tomorrow as di research no go only develop di new type but e go still create job , and still develop economy for di kontri .
E explain say dem still do public lecture wey dey among program wey dem do for di first day of di field day wey dem do , e say why dem introduce public lecture join dis year program na to show stakeholders dem say nah if moni wey reach dey n aim research fit get head .
E beg pipo wey get mouth for Nigeria and organization to kom drop put for research .
Di two days nah ontop to show how technology take enter farming
Wen we tok say he dey tanda wit flood , we no tok say flood no go affect am patapata .
Wetin we dey tok be say wit all di tin wey e get for bodi , e go tanda wit flood wahala reach one side .
FARO 66 go tanda wit flood wahala bikos e tall pass FARO 44 and FARO 52 .
Im stem still hard pass other one .
To manage sky as in to plant quickquick na im be di key to tanda wit flood .
To plant quickquick dey save bigbig if flood come .
If rain don starts , farmers dem no need to dey waste time .
Dis one go make crop dey strong and hold leg for ground wella before flood go com , as im tok .
Dem suppose start to dey plant sharpsharp .

Sasakawa dey do make Corona no get power ontop farmers dem
Sasakawa Global 2000 ( SG ) don tok say im don find way wey farmers dem fit take colabo wit buyers to see say di wahala wey Covid - 19 kos no get power ontop farmers dem
Na dis tin di research and training officer for di organization , Mr Benjamin Shamaki yarn inside one media field tour wey dem do .
As im take talk , Sasakawa don train farmers dem for Kano and Gombe state to dey use di aggregator facilities and to colabo di association of dem farmer join wit buyer wey go give beta value , give dem wey dem dey plant and to see say wetin dem dey sell Corona time beta wella .
We don train women wey bi farmer , no be for only new - school farming , but also to take give dia crop beta value .
We don encourage dem ontop how dem go dey form association , ontop wetin we don successfully colabo dem wit buyers .
E tok say dem dey don still produce along di value chain of one crop
As e be , di chairman for dem Bagwai farmer association , Malam Danladi Yahaya Bagwa tok say dem farmer for dat area dey ready to use di aggregator facilities wey SG 2000 give dem for dia agricultural stability wella , e add join say dem go see say dem use di facilities wella .
As im take tok say Covid - 19 don kos bad - market ontop farming for different different state for di kontri , for Kano too .
E add join say if no be for Sasakawa put hand , dem farmer for di area go don forget dia work tey tey .
E still tok say for di pandemic time , dem give farmer for di area different different beta seed , fertilizer and otapiapia for plant wey im tok say e help dem wella for di time .
Di chairman still tok say as dem carry aggregator facility cum , wey stand gidigba as dia help to comot some marketing palava for di area , don help farmers dem keep dia produce witout gbege and to sell for big price for market .
E tok say di aggregator facility don help farmers dem gather wetin dem dey produce for one place and Sasakawa go help colabo dem wit big big companies wey go buy am for plenty money .
E don dey on record say farmers for dis area as dem no get marketing skil , e dey make dem get small value on top dia produce .
Sasakawa don establish one aggregator centre for us , wey dey give us wisdom wey we go take use dis facilities take make pipo buy awa market wella .
E dey sure say as we no get marketing skil before wey go help us make moni wella for wetin we dey farm don cause plenty kasala for us , na so im tok .
As e be , Sakin Noma of Bagwai , Alhaji Bello Gurdo don tok say for di irrigation site for Kano State , Corona burst kasala for farmers dem .
Im tok say di site we be 1 , 562 hectares of land , get hundred farmers , wey be man and woman wey dey do work on top am .
E tok am say di hand wey SG 2000 put am don help make di work of farmers dem dey berekete for di time .

Governance wey dey poor and illegal weapon for wey dey spread by Adefolarin A . Olamilekan
Governance for Nigeria in dis new time especially since di time wey Civil rule don return in 1999 don dey make pipo dey put eye for am .
Di eye wey dem put na bad tori of di goment wey no gree tackle security mata for di country .
E get one sence wey wetin dey hapun make to take sabi governance wella , especially wit plenti plenti illegal weapon dem evriwia for Nigeria .
Di nation no dey good at all , but dey concern for di safety of im pipo .
Pipo dey cry for help for beta security of life and dere properties
As im be today , di way wey weapon dem wey dey illegal dey plenti evri wia na serious wahala for economic sustenance , unity and to dey togeda .
Na inside all dis kasala wey we take sabi wetin di link wey dey between governance and di illegal weapon wey dey evriwia be , wey be main mata for dis time of awa national life .
As Nigeria dey go up and down for di last two decades don make plenti Nigerians sabi wetin be di poverty governance .
As e take be like dat , e go beta for us make we sabi wetin governance be for simple sense and wetin in be for inside dis context .
Di Oxford Advanced Learners Dictionary , Sixth Edition tok say governance na di way wey dem dey control one kontri or di way wey one kontri or institution deu dey control .
So , governance na di process of control and controlling activity wey dey a kontri join weapon wit im circulation .
Again , governance still fit dey look as di process wey dem goment pipo dey hold power , authority and di way wey dem dey give policy wey pertain to pesin life and economic decision for di beta beta of di pipo .
As e be , to dey run di goment go take make dem use decision wey dey good and wey go get good impact on top di management and di sharing of resources wey include moni , pesin and material .
E go involve di regulation , implementation and enforcement for d policy wey pesin want , wey go be for objective wey get target , goals and aspiration through capacity .
As e be , governance na to dey control di development wey pesin want , wey be say , to protect life and property of kontri pipo tru d regulate of arms and weapon dem be koko .
As e be so , e get plenty reason wey explain di poverty wey never stop since for governance for Nigeria .
For example , poor institutional capacity na im cause goment failure , wey no make everything balance in di wey dem dey do justice and fairness , wey cause oppression and jagajaga for mind .
To add join dis one , na as dem dey do ojoro dey help dere family dem , as dem dey selfish , ethnic partial wey don cut to dey togeda ontop decision making troway , and as di political representative no dey too do dia work .
Di mata wey di Chairman for di National peace Committee ( NPC ) and d former Military Head of State , General Abdulsallami Abubakar tok for Transcorp Hilton for Abuja say e pass 6 million illegal weapon wey dem fit trace to di kontri pipo , many of dem no get work and dem dey hungry and angry .
Di nomba of di small small weapon wey dey Nigeria for di hand of kontri pipo wey no dey military reach 6 , 145 , 000 and armed forces and law enforcement pipo count dia own to be 586 , 000 weapon .
E still tok go front about di sekuriti problem wey dey di kontri .
E tell all di nation say na 80 , 000 Nigeria pipo don die for recent month and like three million pipo be Internally Displaced Persons ( IDPs ) evriwia for di kontri bikos say sekuriti problem dey plenti and illegal weapon dem waka evriwia for di country .
E kon tok say di sekuriti forces no just dey over work but dem no get moni , and e tok say dem fit do beta if dem give dem beta weapon , equipment and make dem give dem moni wey go dey accountable .
As di forma head of state and di chairman for National Peace Committee ( NPC ) take shuk mouth for di mata , e don show say we suppose take governance serious ontop plenty die - die tins for di kontri .
Wela , e don show say pipo wey even dey power and authority dey live for inside fear .
For dis side dem suppose hear cry for help of d pipo make dem try reduce as illegal weapon dem waka evriwia .
For onetime dem tok say na for Africa weapon dey increase pass .
Small arms , Mass Atrocities & Migration for Nigeria , tok say na as weapon too dey increase na im make bring gunpipo , n aim still kos di scatascata of many Nigeria pipo .
Di report tok say na as weapon dey plenti for Southern Nigeria n aim make kasala plenti for area like village wahala , cult , kidnapping , tribe and religion gbege , and militancy for di Niger Delta .
And na d same way di report tok say for Northern Nigeria side , as per say corruption don plenti for dat side , dem get plenti land wey no get pesin wey dey rule am , and dem no too get work and na dis tins don make criminal and wahala mani for dia side .
Di report tok say wetin we tok before hapun bikos say Small Arms and Light Weapons ( SALW ) dey increase .
Di mata dey question di feasibility of di National Task Force on top Small Arms and Light Weapons .
So , we must to find di way to dey go front , even say e no dey clear and we no fit settle am .
We suppose face di mata and tackle as di illegal weapon dey dey evriwia for di kontri wit all di goment structure wey dey tackle di mata for di federal , state and local goment level .
And as e be , di National Task Force for Small Arms and Light weapons and di office of di National Sekuriti Adviser for di President ( ONSA ) must tight moremore to tackle di illegal arm wey don plenty wit to disturb and to stop am .
As e kon be like dis , we need program wey go teach how dem dey carry pipo for mind for governance and di sekuriti policy dey needed no be only community policing but policing for individual and group to dey share intelligence .
Di main tin na transparency , accountability and responsibility for beta governance , if dem dey , we no go fit comot all di illegal weapon wet dey evriwia .
Olamilekan na political economist and development researcher and you fit reach am for Whatsapp
Nigeria don record him highest start up among him mate - Tori .
Nigeria don carry first for di start up among oda kontri for Africa , na one tori from fDi Intelligence , one specialist division for di Financial Times , tok am .
As Tolu Olasoji take analyse di report for inside leadership newspaper , e tok say as Nigeria fit do make mouth for di biggest numba for startup for Africa technology ecosystem , e dey back for oda metrics wet dey important .
The report wey di FDI Intelligence and di Briter Bridges write , tok say di investment for di continent start up space no reach di one for di global North .
For example , US start up don raise $ 156 . 2bn as dem enta venture capital for last year , per Pitch book .
And for Africa start up dem don raise just more than $ 2bn for Nigeria for two years , as data tok am .
Na seventeen kontri don dem pick for di evaluation ontop house for plenti tech hub , if dem get more 50 start up , and if dey get kolet investment wey pass $ 500 , 000 for 2019 and 2029 .
Na South African carry first for di advancement of start up , and Kenya carry second .
But for capacity , na Nigeria get di highest volume of start up - e pass 750 .
South Africa carry second , but him start up don raise $ 241m for 2020 , wey no be like Nigeria .
$ 64 . 1m .
Di kontri dey missing inside di top 10 of pipo wey dey important to dey maintain start - ups beyond im founding , wit cost effectiveness and di level wey di tech talent of kontri dey .
E just carry numba six for business friendliness .
Dis one don show as tins take bad for pipo wey get business for Nigeria , na wetin di analysis tok .

Naija don loss N3 . 7tr for poor cold chain logistic .
Naija n aim dem don calculate say e dey lose N3 . 7 trillion evri year for di waste wey dey com ontop as dem no dey keep food well .
Di Chairmo for di Governing Counsel for Naijan Institute of Transport Technology ( NITT ) , Mr . John ONojeharho , wen im bin dey tok for di 8th Naijan Annual Transport Lecture wey dem do for Lagos for weekend .
E say , Naija get one percent for di way wey dem dey manage cold chain
Di market dey big and if dem fit run am well , we fit save like $ 9 billion for evri year if we stop to dey let food dey waste and we dey keep dem well .
Onojeharho tok say if we dey keep di 15 million metric tonnes of market wey fit spoil wey dey waste evri year wella , tins no go dey cost and our economy go beta .
E add join say Naija be number 110 out of 160 countries for di world inside to perform for logistics .
Di pesin wey sabi transport well tok say why di cold chain logistic no good na bicos of di road wey no good , as di cold chain dey continue , high capital investment , light and like that like that .

Di internet don bring fundamental shift enter economy dem wey no near each oda bikos of brier enter ross - border trade and investment , wey distance far , time zone and language and wey national goment regulation different .
E - commerce dey foster direct access to market wey no near and e dey promote globalisation and commercial activities plus e dey komot distinction between domestic and foreign companies to di extent wey e no go possible to know wia di product from kom .
E - commerce no dey limited to buying of product alone , e include e - mail , plus oda communication platform dem , all di informate or service wey company fit offer customer on top net , from pre - purchase information to aftasale service and support .
Di major significance wey e commerce get dey for di fact say e dey encourage system of tradin wey be single world , wey access through electronic means to take get good and services dem dey facilitate from different parts of di world .
Most of di statue wey dey for ground for inside nigeria dey lag behind toward di development and growth of e - commerce in particular and di whole ICT .
For Nigeria , plenty legal research and study don dey conducted .
Plenty for inside di study dem carry opinion say di legal system for Nigeria ey lag behind for legislation wey involve ICT and say di statutory law dem wey don dey ground no dey adequate to take address some of di legal issue wey dey affect e - commerce .
Dis issue dem include electronic evidence cybercrimes , security and data production , e - payment system and inevitably trans - border issues , plus plenty oda ones .
Therefore , need dey to bring out legal and regulatory measure wey dey proper , to take govern di regime wey just dey kom .
Dem don tok plenty times say for inside Nigeria , significant effort to take regulate e - commerce - related activity demstill dey di stage of Sraft Bill before di National Assembly .
E dey important to know say , even wia dem pass dis bill into law , Nigeria fit still face new legal issue for dis area wey go call for legislative intervention .
Wit di speed wey di internet dey take work on top commercial transaction for Nigeria , especially for inside banking and communication sector of di economy , di best wey dem fit suggest be say di legal issues and problems dem wey dey confront e - commerce presently for di kontri should be addressed directly and espeditiously , for di interest of di teeming population of Nigeria customer dem .
To achieve dis , make dem pressure di National Assembly to take pass bill concerning electronic commerce as top priority so dat dem go enact dem into law as quick as possible .
For small time , make awa court take giant step to interprete di traditional law dem wey dey ground in a liberal way make dem take cut gap in order to make di laws dem get ammend to electronic transaction , particularly for di emerging trend of dis information age wey we dey .
Indeed , dem argue say legislation no be di only means wey electronic transaction and attendant documentation fit dey legal .
Di court fit also adapt to recognise electronic transaction for di absence of legislation or private contract .
As former Justice Bungham don tok am before : di common law dey di hand of judges di same kind facility [ as law merchant dem ] make e fit adapt to di need of di general public , principle no dey alter , but old rules to dey apply di change , and new rules go begin exist .
We dey hope say goment go adopt dis activism wey Nigerian judges de do for inside judiciary , Supreme Court judges sef dey involve , expexially for area wia awa existin legislation dey grossly inadequate , comprehensive or elaborate enough to take address legal challenges for inside new technological advancements .
Dis one go set better precedence to make sure say e - commerce consumer dem get protection , to bring investor dem and bring economic development plus stability inside di kontri .
Di koko issue for contract inside e - commerce na documentation and signature .
Di provision for inside section 4 of di statute of Fraud , 1677 or Lagos State Law Reform ( Contract ) Law and awa various statute on real property and landed instrument dem , all of which require make dem write certain contract dem and execute dem duly .
Di question now be say shey electronic sign - off dey constitute valid sign - off contract by email or by binding ?
Dem still neva settle many of dis issues dem even for inside UK although some decision dey favour toward to interprete electronic signature
So marks for inside email wey ey satisfy di tradional requirement of writing and due execusion .
E - commerce transaction na transaction wey no involve paper wey dem dey do through magnetic material like tapes or disk .
Dis one dem be contradiction to di transaction wey be say na paper dem dey take do am wey dey embodied for permanent form and typically expressed in words and figures wey dem dey use signature authenticate .
Dem no fit alter dat kind transaction without say dem alter di face of di document .
As e concern signature , di provision for inide section 93 ( 2 ) ( 3 ) , evidence act 2011 , electronic signature wey relate to data message go conveniently satisfy any requirement for signature wey dem take hand sign as long as say e dey sufficient to take identify an electronic record to di person .
Di provision for inside article 7 of di United Nations Commission on International Trade Law ( UNCITRAL ) model law for e - commerce 1996 dey equally trite on top dis issue .
Thus , for di purpose of establishing proof of electronic signatures .
To dey use password , identification , user names etc fit suffice .
Hence one fit safely tok say electronic signature for purpose of execution dey admissible for evidence provided say dem certify and incorporate am for electronic communication during any e - transaction .
Also , oda legal challenge dem wey dey affect e - commerce include di formation of contracts .
Di element for better formation of contract include offer , acceptance , consideration , intention to enter inside legal relation .
Di question be say , for which point dem fit make offer wit regard to electronic business transaction or now to differentiate between invitation to treat and offer electronic transaction , at which point we fit tok say dem make intention to enter legal relation ?
E - commerce require confidence and trust di satisfaction wey dey transmit order or invoice neva get any matter and e dey kom from whoever e appear to kom from .
Need dey for guarantee concerning level of privacy / confidenciality for information matter .
Lastly , di alarming rate of cybercrime for inside Nigeria , plus high level of illiterate .
No doubt say electronic transaction na aspect of commercial transaction for Nigeria and e don kom to stay dis time .
Make di goment go pass to dey make law , make dem activate as dem go take dey use di electronic platform for dem commercial interaction and for delivery of goment service .

Chad don pass new chartes as dem call Deby son president
Chad don pass charter wey declare Mahamat Idris Deby as President , even as rumour dey social media say he don die .
Mahamat don take over to take replace im papa , Idriss deby wey dem kill dis week .
Di charter tok say di 37 - year old wey be son to late war veteran , na im dem name transitional leader quick quick on Tuesday as head for military council afta im papa death , e go dey do work of president for di republic and head of di armed forces dem .
Di charter repeal di preceding constitution and dem go implement am as di basic law of di republic , according to di temrs wey dey inside am .
Dem also don name di young Deby as supreme head for armed forces , as e tok .
Deby son don oversee di security of im papa when im be head of di elite presidential guard and he dey appear along wit im papa often .
Di best wey dem take know Mahamat Deby na as top commander of di forces inside Chad wey dey help United Nation peacekeeping mission for inside di restive north of neighbouring Mali .
Im sign one decree for Tuesday as he set out one military council wey get 15 generals dem , including imsef and 14 odas wey dem know say dey loyal to late president .
Di task wey dem give di council na to move enter free and democractic election withing 18 months .
Mahamat Idris Deby na chair for di military transition council , di council of ministers , di counil of superior committees of national defence , as di charter take tok .
Di new head of state go dey declare legislation wey di 69 members of di national transition council adopt , wey Mahamat name directly .
Di Transition Charter wey get 95 articles , e also guarantee freedom of opinion , conscience plus worship .
Dem don set transition goment , wey di new president go name di members .
Di charter tok say dem don free all member of army wey dem call to di transitional goment from all military work .
Law for Chad
Di leader wey dem kill , im rule wit strong hand for lmost 30 years , he give to wound wey im get wen im visit battlefield wia Chad soldier dem dey fight rebel group for di north , as di military announce for Tuesday .

US Africom for Nigeria ?
Heck No !
Overpaid , oversexed and over here .
Dat na di resentful and contemptuous opinion many British pipo get for di thousands of American GIs wey station for inside several military bases for Britain durin di Secon World War .
Di gum - chewing , brash , hard - drinking and womanising soldier dem wey from America comedey frequently get into pub fight and knife fight weu dey dangerous wey dey kos bad feeling for di yanks among di locals .
And dis don be di pattern wey America soldiers dem dey take behave evriwia for di hundred of America military base oversea from Okinawa for inside Japan , Stuttgart inside Germany , Incirlik and Diyarbakir for Turkey and Pampanga inside Philippines .
Na why i dey upset , like plenty Nigeria pipo , say na for virtual meetin last week wit di di Secretary of State of di United States of America , Antony Blinken , na dem report say president Buhari ask United States to consider as dem go take relocate di African Command ( Africom ) of im military wey dey for Stuttgart for inside southern German city of presently kom Africa .
We dey thingk am say wit dis kin call , president Buhari dey make way for Nigeria to host Africom .
For di first place , na breach of protocol for President Buhari to do dat meeting wit di American Secretary of State .
Dem suppose do di meetin wit Blinken's Nigerian opposite number , Geoffrey Onyeama , who o kom carri di detail go meet president later .
Yes , America na superpower and all , but protocol na protocol and dem soppose follow am strictly for evri circumstance .
We understand say Nigeria dey face big internal security wahala wey be like say e pass di best effort wey goment and security establishment for inside di nation dey make to take tackle am .
Terrorist insurgency wey no dey tire for di North East banditry , kidnapping inside di North West , farmers / herders clash dem all over di kontri and as dem dey target and kill security and law enforcement personnel dem and oda Nigeria pipo plus di destruction of institutional building for di South East , na dem join take be di cokctail of insecurity wey don dey ravage di kontri .
But even at that , di call to take host Africom on top Nigeria siol when we consider m against various issues and implications of dis move to Nigeria difficult to justify .
Africom na one amng nine of dat kind command wey di America military establish say make e dey serve America strategic interest around di world .
By dem rule and way of operation , dis commands , particularly di ones wey dey outside America like Africom , dem no set dem up primarily to concern demselves wit security and law enforcement issuefor dem area of coverage .
Dem only do so when such issue dey affect di interest of America directly for di area and for such situation , dem no dey mandated to yield dem modus operandi and share intelligence wit di local security and law enforcement agancy dem
If dem set Africom up for Nigeria for instance , e go be island on im ownas e go restrict access to Nigerians of all category and establishing a jurisdiction withing di teritorial area of di base wey go dey virtually off limit to Nigerian security and law enforcement agancy dem .
As e dey always apun wit America military base wey dey outside America , Africom go be forward operating base for disruptive intelligence operations and e go source for act of sabotage and destabilisation against host kontri .
For dis particular case of Africom , part of im original concept na to kontrol as di strategic influence of Nigeria dey grow for West Africa and Africa as we get successful peace enforecement efforts for Liberia and Sierra Leone and awa beta record of peace keepin around di world .
Di one wey dey before Africom na di Africa Crisis Response Initiative ( ACRI ) wey di Clinton administration set up to take counter di strategic interest of Nigeria for inside Africa .
Di Secretary of State for president Clinton , di dour - faced California attorney , Warren Christopher , be visit a nomba of African countries secretly to sell di idea .
But bikos Nigeria na di target , he pointedly komot am from im itinerary .
Senegal , wey no far from Liberia and Sierra Leone , na im suppose be di coordinating base of di ACRI and though dem see am initiative to facilitate assistance of America to African humanitarian issues , im secret protocol dem mistake for military and dem target Nigeria strategically .
Due mainly to undisguised hostility to di idea from France , which was averse to seeing di Americans trying to butt into an area it considers its exclusive sphere of influence , dem review di concept of di ACRI .
For di review , wey draw di expertise of america Military , intelligence , political and academic personalities and institutions wey di America congress carry kom for dem secret sessions , di Americans dem consider and realise di need to set up one AFrican command to add to di oda command wey don dey already and dey cover oda continent for inside di world .
Thus , to follow on di reccomendation of experts wey gather , wey dem kom form all angle of political and security establishments for inside America , na di Bush Junior administration set Africom up wit mandate wey wide pass to contain Nigeria but also to keep eye on top di strategic penetration wey Chinese pipo dey do for inside Africa .
Na as US Central Command ( USCENTCOM ) take be to Middle East and Asia , na so Africom go be to Africa , as e base for Florida , European Command ( EUCOM ) , as e base for Stuttgart , Germany , is to Europe and Southern Command ( SOUTHCOM ) , also based in Florida , is to Latin America and di Caribbean .
Di presence of French military don surround Nigeria already as dem dey for Niger , Cameroun , Chad and Benin .
Di America pipo also get drone base for inside Niger .
To add Africom to di mix for inside Nigeria go amount to a complete capitulation of awa strategic interest to both France and America .
As we get am for mind say awa strategic interest plus profile for Africa no dey always follow wit di one for France and America , to host Africom for Nigeria go be di same thing like make we allow wolf enter chicken cage .
Notin dey inside di insecurity cahllenge wey dey face di kontri wey awa armed forces no fit cope wit .
Dis one na afta di military force wey eventually secure Liberia and Seirra Leone against army of insurgents wey dey well - entrenched and organised for inside di kontri dem from a long logistical supply line thousands of mile ; di army of Joshua Dogonyaro , Victor Malu and Maxwell Khobe , to mention few of di plenty gallant Nigeria soldier wey distinguish demsef for di operation dem .
E dey regretable say di Nigeria military , don fall from high standard wey dem take know dem , dem dey struggle now to cope wit di activity of non - state actors internally .
But intrinsically and essentially , di military for Nigeria still carry di capacity and capability to defeat dis threat to awa nationl security if dem get di correct leadership , doctrine plus motivation .
We need all di assistance and coopration wey di America pipo fit give us if dem wan give us .
But as dem don hold us for hand to take host Africom with awa circumstance in view of im antecedent and implication to awa strategic interest , for awa soil .
Upon say dem dey face challenge , Plateau target 7m metric tons of Irish potato
For Nigeria , na Plateau state be nomba one wey dey plant Irish potato as dem dey produce am for nine of di 17 local goment area wey dey di state .
Di Potato Value Chain Support Project of di African Development Bank ( AfDB ) initiative don Plateau as state wey get 90 per cent of di potato production for inside di kontri as kontri like Chad , Ghana , Niger , Benin and oda ones dey get large supply of potato from Nigeria .
Di large potato production for inside Plateau State , according to PotatoPRO . com , wey be leading source for informate for global potato industry , don make Nigeria di nomba four big kontri for inside sub - sahara Africa .
However , farmer dem tok say dam wey no good reach and bad road network , plus as di cost of fertilizer and oda farmin input kontinu to dey stand as major setback for di production of potatoes for inside di nation and to export .
Oda challenge wey dey contribute to low yield and loss for harvest to di potato value chain include disease like blight and bacterial wilt , plus poor seedlings .
According to di National Bureau of Statistics , Plateau State dey among di ten poorest state for Nigeria as dem poverty rate pass 70 % .
However , di state get comparative advange to take boost economic activities by improving di competitiveness of di potato commodity value chain .
Di project Coordinator for di Potato value Chain Support Project , Thomas Muopshin , tok say though di visibility of di tuber crop dey evident for nine local goment area inside Plateau , Na Bokkos and Mangu LGAs be di hub for potato .
Na dem dey produce potato pass any LGA fir di kontri .
However , Muopshin tok say adaptability research indicate say di remainin eight LGA for inside di state also fit plant potato , dat one go make all 17 LGA wey dey for Plateau fit produce tuber , especially for inside dry season .
However , di Association of Potato Farmers ( APF ) for inside di state , tok say unless dem address di challenge wey dey face di value chain , increase production and export of potato go continue to pass di national .
Chairman of APF for inside Plateau state , Lazarus Makut , for one interview wey he do wit daily Trust , tok say di inadequate small dam , especially for remote area wia dem dey plant potato , and bad road plus high cost of farm input kontinu to dey affect potato output .
He tok say di cost of mechanised farmin wey fit increase production quick quick don dey expensive as di majority of farmers na small scale producer wey dey unable to afford mechanization .
Anoda farmer , wey be Martha Mamgup , wey dey plant potatoe for inside Ampang town for Mangu LGA .
tok say water wey no reach durin dry season dey affect potato farmer and harvest dey low evri year .
Bekos of dis , she tok say , di majority of farmers dem search for location of borehole to farm to take access irrigation water for dem farm .
Martha also explain say di high cost of fertilizer dey prevent plenty farmers from improvin quantity plus quality of yield , she add say wen fertilizer no reach , e dey affect di crop output .
Di cost dey also prevent many of us from expandin di business .
So , to get fertilizer no be dey easy for us .
She tok say di construction of more dam plus borehole for irrigation go lead to plenty production of potatoes .
If di watre no reach for di crop , e go dry and e go later die and day na why some farmer wey get di resources dey prefer to dig boreholes for Mangu for irrigation bikos , without am , season farmin go bekom difficult , as she tok .

Wit potato production inside Plateau State wey don jump from 1 , 656 , 650 metric tons in 2017 to 2 , 359 , 890 metric tons in 2020 , di establishment of Potato Value Chain Support Project and dem expect make diconstruction of tisue culture lab kos make production triple pass seven million metric tons by di time wey 2021 go end .
Di officer wey Monitor and Evaluate state's Potato Value Chain Support Project for di state , Baleri Yakubu , tell Daily Trust say dem expect make di state start production of six million of potato evri year afta dem complete di tissue culture lab at di end of 2021 but e dey optimistic say production fit pass seven million metric tons evri year .
However , Yakubu tok say mak di state goment tackle oda challenges wey farmers dem dey face , especially di one of fertilizer as well as dam and road network as dem dey expect make farmers dem apply proper potato farming regulation to take achieve expected target .
Our correspondent hear say di tissue culture lab , wey dem intend to take improve potato yield for di state by providing seed wey clean wey dey resist pest and oda disease dem wey relate to potato na im dem expect say go commence full operation in few month dem .
Yakubu tok say e dey certain say di advent of di lab go improve income for farmers and revenue for di state goment and e go also help food security for inside di kontri .
Farmer for inside Plateau State , however , believe say di tissue la , if e dey fully equipped , go reduce di cost of treatment for di crop when disease affect dem .
Dem also hope say better quality seed go dey available for affordable price .

China don give reach 140 million COVID - 19 vaccines
China don administer 139 . 97 million doses of COVID - 19 vaccines as of April 4 , 2021 , as di National Health Commission ( NHC ) of di kontri tok .
China dey work to make sure say dem vaccination effort for major area and key sector industry as e base on di overall plan of di kontri , inoculating di eligible population as wide as dem fit reach and to make progress in stages , as Wu Liangyou , wey be deputy director of di NHCs Disease Prevention and Control Bureau .
Di kontri don dey gather resources to ensure inoculation for city wey get large and medium size , city wey get prot , area wey get border wey get high risk of infection , plus dem give priority to key group wey include employee for inside public sector , student dem and faculty for inside college and universities , plus service staff for inside big supermarket dem , as Wu take tok , and e add say vaccination for oda group sef don dey for progress .
For present , Beijing , Shanghai plus some oda places for inside China don give senior citizenswey wan kolekt di vaccine , wey dey above di age of 60 and patients wey get chronic diseases COVID - 19 vaccines , wey get beta physical condition .
He Qinghua , wey official for di NHC note say di commission go advance di vaccination campaign with order of importance , dem go follow di priciple of informed consent , voluntary participation and free inoculation .
Di kontri dey coordinate regular prevention and kontrol wit im vaccination efforts , to make sure say di regular responsibility of local goment dem and di one wey dem don komot eye dey fulfilled , and to dey advance dem vaccination campaign in manner weu dey more secured and orederly and forceful , as e tok am .
Besides , China don take step to take include more pipo for dem vaccination campaign to ensure dem health , di official add .
So far , China don approve COVID - 19 vaccines wey five enterprises produce for conditional marketing or for emergency use .
Phase III of three vaccines dem wey dem neva activate and one adenovirus vaccine show say dem efficacy meet di requirement of National Medical Products Administration for China and di World Health Organization .
Phase II trial for di recombinant protein subunit vaccine wey dem appove for emergency use don show say di vaccine dey safe and e fit cause strong immune response .
All di COVID - 19 vaccine wey China adopt don go through clinical studies wey follow relevant standard , wey national drug regulatory organization dem approve and dem begin dey use am afta e pass strict examination , as Li Bin wey be deputy head for NHC take tok .
All vaccines suppose dey monitor and make dem temperature get record from time to time to make sure say dem meet requirement on temperature environment and transportation .
Li add say Health regulator for inside China don also enhance effort for di training of health worker dem , require say make dem obey operating instructions , so dem go fit guarantee di efficacy and safety of di vaccine .

Cybercrime na global threat to pipo , organisation and kontri dem .
Nigeria dey loss pass $ 128 billion to cybercrimes evri year .
By di time 2021 go end , di world go don loss total of $ 6 trillion .
Till date , e pass 40 Nigeria pipo wey dem dey or wey FBI still dey investigate for dem complicity inside fraudulent scams .
Di allege unemployemnt benefit fraud wey Rufai do go dey under wetin I don call COVID - 19 fraud for Nigeria .
Dis na scam wey dey use loopholes wey COVID - 19 pandemic don cause to dey scam pipo , goment pr organization dem .
During di COVID - 19 lockdown for inside Nigeria , cybercriminals dey do dem frauds along di interventions from goment and private sectors and scamm plenty and some of di scheme dem still dey till date .
Domino pizza fraud dey , federal goment cash palliative fraud , N20 , 000 Dangote relief fund fraud and promo sales fraud among oda ones .
Wen some dey wey dey cyber - criminality outside Nigeria , some youngster dem dey do am inside Nigeria .
Di Economic and Financial Crimes Commission ( EFCC ) dey arrest dem , also try and convict dem .
To understand di culture wey dey sustain cyber - criminality fit help serious goment to fight di crime .
Di family na di di small worldfor inside di larger society .
Na di place wey dem suppose nuture normal human beign for di society .
Apart from di fact say plenty family for Nigeria dey inside dungeon of poverty and e dey hard to take care of dem children , some of di children don bikom breadwinners , as e be , e no legit .
Ethical behaviour training for plenty house na challenge as dem don dey arrest parent plus dem children wey dem gather do cyber - criminality .
For some oda places , yahoo boys mama dem dey form association to take celebrate dem pikin success nd justify di criminal thing wey dem do .

E get one viral video wia some boys dey spray money while pipo wey be like say dem be shepherd for inside white garment church dey enjoy di captive di moment , as dem member wey di female youth wing of di church dey lead dey record di act of shame .
Pikin wey dem born for 1999 wen Nigeria enter democracy again na 21 years now .
Sadly , dem grow to dey appreciate lie as a way of life from politician dem mouth ( and for plenty cases from home ) wey dey decieve pipo to vote for dem nd dem no dey fulfil di promise wey dem amke for compaign .
Lying sef na di foundation of di sociology of hushpuppism .

Dem dey see how di system dey give farudulent pipo soft landing ( for public or private ) .
Shey dem dey ask how many fraud and corruption allegation wey dem don investigate and discharge wit punishment when di accuse dey guilty ?

Dem dey see how poor politcal aspirant dey bikom millionaire withing months wey dem enter office .

All of those weu mismanage monet dey get soft landing .

If we elect fraud pesin enter legislator , e go make law against di crime wey e dey involve ?

Unfortunately , di greed wey dem allege dis defendant dem dey affect all taxpayer .

Make Nigeria sanitise dem anti - coruption system and make dem put accoutability policy in place to take track lifestyle with material accumulation .
We must give youth for inside Nigeria hope by creating employment opportunity , reduce poverty plus review reward system dem .

Di commission need to finish investigation before dem go arrest suspect as FBI do before dem arrest huspuppi and Abidemi Rufai Sandy Tang .
Unless dem tackle di culture wey dey sustain cybercrimes for inside Nigeria wit social social engineering , cyber - criminality go kontinu to spread .
Dr Tade , wey be sociologist write dis piece pu for dotad2003 @ yahoo . com

official theme for 2021 na Arts , Culture , and Heritage : Levers for Building di Africa We Want .
