How e dey feel to born inside pandemic By Dil Afrose Jahan .
When news of death dey evriwia , one new life bring hapines plus hope
For January 1 , 2020 , one new morning , two red line change my life .
I get belle and I dey hapi
Na mamzing start to new year .
Na di most remarkable year of my life .
All of a sudden , evriting change .
My daughter Roshomon Tara was born at di end of di first lockdown in Dhaka , Bangladesh ; she is now nine months old .
I born my pikin Roshomon Tara at di end of di first lockdown for Dhaka , Bangladesh ; she don enter nine months old now .
She be di reason I bekom mother for di middle of global crisis .
No be only her dem born , but na also new me , mama tara , wey spend di whole pregnancy inside lockdown for house and born di pikin for emergency condition inside di emergency .
Tara don see di world wit mask and isolation .
Her grandma dem dey also fear to touch her or kom near her if dem no wear mask .
If pandemic be no dey , my journey to take enter motherhood go different .
Dis Mother Day dey very special as my pikin don dey for my front , dey look me dey smile .
For di last mother day , she dey grow inside of me .
Di only thing wey no change , meanwhile , na di pandemic .
Na 16 weeks belle dey inside me when di pandemic apun , and di world enter lockdown .
I be dey struggle to survive di pandemic with my hormonal and physical changes .
Di 22 weeks dem be like war .
My husband , Sina Hasan na musician , and all im concert dey cancelled for dat time .
I be freelance journalist since January 1 , 2021 .
So we be dey depend on wetin I don save already , and we spend all my savings .
Our parent and two journalists association dem come forward to help for di main time .
I be dey fear evrithing .
Most of di time , e be like say na die
dey knock for awa door .
I be dey adapt to new life wey say na online we dey click and dem dey deliver awa things or home - delivery .
I get to dey wait for one week make dem for take deliver groceries like day .
I even dey fear to send di only family member wey dey live wit me , my husband to komot go buy food storage .
So , I no too dey eat .
Beside sef , I no fit go for my antenatal check - up as dem take give me time .
And I be no dey sure if my pikin dey grow welwel abi if development dey take place timely .
I be dey sorry for my unborn pikin say I dey bring am inside world wey different from as e ever be .
Na tele - medication help me pass some hard time for inside di last three month dem .
I be forget di face of my gynaecologist .
I no fit imagine s she go take look if she no wear PPE .
I need informate about risks , precautions , and how I fit get emergency medical help .
plenty informate be dey flow around .
For inside dis informate wahala , mother dem wey get experience my mama , and my mother - in - law fit only dey support me and no be say dem meet me for pesin when i be get belle .
Traditionally , experienced mothers and mostly older women for inside di family go help new mother dem wit dem experience plus observation .
I be don get plenty panic attack bikos I no get information and understanding .
So I be dig experience of mother dem wey give birth durin dis time .
I see social media as lifeline .
I read plenty exciting experience for social media when I be dey follow one group wey gey over 100 , 000 woman wey get belle and wey dey give pikin breast as dem dy support each oda to take survive di pandemic .
Different media group for di platfrm don help pass 100 , 000 woman wey belle and di ones wey dey give pikin breast as dem dey share experience plus informate durin di lockdown .
Na one di group help me find heakth care fcility to take do emmergency ultrasound afta heavy bleeding fir inside di lockdown .
Anoda group be help to stop anxiety and di depresion wey dey follow childbirth .
I be dey vex say I no fit meet my parents , relatives , or friends to take share di joy of say I welkom new member inside di family .
My daughter was born on August 25 , 2020 , at di same hospital , Azimpur Maternity , wia I was born decades ago .
I be born my pikin for August 25 , 2020 , for di same hospital , Azimpur Maternity , wia dem born me decades ago .
And she meet anoda child one on one when she be enter four months old for December 31 , 2020 , when Tara and her papa go di rooftop with me to see di fireworks .
Anoda fimily with two baby , wey be my neighbour wey I dey meet for di first time also go dere to go tok byebye for 2020 .
Every day na , and e still be gift , to consider di recent statistics of increased Covid - 19 cases .
When news about death full evriwia , di new life bring hapines and hope .
For mother dem , e no different from say dem win war as dem born pikin inside pandemic and dem dey care for di new pikin alone , to confirm di safety wey high pass for dem pikin .
Socially , emotionally , and physically , dis time fit challenge person .
Thanks to di light wey dey shine inside di eyes of di baby dem .
Thank you my pikin , my daughter , for who I be mama and a successful fighter wey survive dis pandemic .
Dil Afrose Jahan don kolekt di National Geographic Society's Emergency Fund for Journalist dem .
Na National Geographic Society support dis work .
Di national question , insecurity and di declaration for inside Asaba .
By Segun Tomori
Recently , governor dem for inside souther Nigeria be meet inside Asaba and dem make some kind resolution on top di state of di nation , which dem don dey call Asaba declaration .
Di meetin dey kom on top di matter as insecurity for di kontri don dey worse , agitation by some kind ethnic jingoist and as di matter murderous herdsmen menace dey generate nationwide attention .
Indeed , di bi - partisan nature wey di meetin get plus di unanimity wey di 17 governor dem display show say dem mean serious business .
Restructuring inside di context of true federalism and di ban of open grazing form di koko of di declaration .
Major light follow be to bring state police , devolution of power , to review revenue formula to take favour federating unit plus di need for national dialogue to take discuss di nation question .
As dem suppose condemn di way gobernos dem dey take drag leg on top financial autonomy for state legislature and judiciary and e no follow di spirit of true federalism which dem dey call for , planty for inside dem resolution na tenet for di ruling All Progressives Congress ( APC ) wey di committee wey Gov .
El = Rufai lead on top true federalism recommend .
One go expect say di leading light for inside APC go take advantage of di bipartisan nature of di Asaba declaration , and di support of di major opposition parti to take begin di process to address di issue .
Instead , we see attempt to take play to di gallery and for some quarter , subtle censure of di governor dem .
Di El - Rufai committee don recommend devolution of power , resource control , state police , local goment autonomy plus review inside revenue frmula for favour of federatin unit among dem .
President Buhari don give support for local government , state legislature and judiciary autonomy since , as im back amendment for inside di statutes and issue Executive Order 010 .
As di state of di nation take be , wey security and economic don bikom big challenge , na dis two sector dem suppose get di untimate attention togeda .
Despite as dem rate Nigeria as kontri wey get highest GDP for inside Africa , we still neva make better effort wey reach to translate am to take improve standard of living or di majority of awa kontri pipo .
For instance now , awa annual budget wey reach $ 35 billion , e dey very inadequate to take cater for di need of 220 million Nigeria pipo .
South Africa wey get about 58 million pipo get National budget wey reach $ 75bn for 2019 and her Social Protection Programme reach 17m of im populatiom
Di effort wey di Buhari administration dey make , though na new way and e dey commendable , na just drop for inside ocean and e no dey adequate to make required impact .
Na here devolution of power and resource kontrol go enter .
Solid minerals and natural resource dem no get any business to stay pass one day inside Exclusive list .
Almost all di state wey dey di kontri get natural resources wey fit sell market wey dem fit explore to tak create wealth and generate di foreign exchange wey di kontri need .
Di present system wia state dey go Abuja to go kolekt federal allocation for inside di kontri dey breed indolence , e no follow di principle of true federalism .
Just as di El - Rufai committee take propose , say make dem review di revenue formula to take favour states since dem go add more responsibilities to dem .
On top state police , e dey undesratndable say dem dey fear say governors dem go abuse am , but like Richie Nortondon tok , To escape fear , you have to go through it , not around it .
For too long , we don dey waka round fear of abuse of state police , we don turn blind eye to di centralised Nigeria Police Force wey don dey overstretched and wey don bikom inefficient and big problem .
As vice - President Osinbajo tok some years ago , State Police na idea wey im time don kom .
We have to address awa fears and overcome it .
One for di way na to enact legal instrument to take establish di State Police Regulatory Commission ( SPRC ) , along wit constitutional amendments dem wey go permit state police .
E go dey similar function wit Federal Police Service Commission ( PSC ) but e go get wider power to take exercise appointive plus regulatory function dem .
Do ban on top open grazing wey di governors dem restate no be nwe thing , e dey part of di fulcrum of di National Livestock Transformation Plan ( NLTP ) wey National Executive Council ( NEC ) approve .
Di International Crisis Group ( ICG ) don put di NLTP as di most comprehensive effort wey Nigeria don make to date to take overhaul di inefficient and grosly underperforming livestock system .
For di core na strategy to take curb migratory or open grazing and thus lower di risk of conflict between herders and farmersdem , therefore , beggars belief that some myopic , sef - acclaimed ethnic champions choose to lampoon di ban on pre - historic , nomadic open grazing .
Make di federal and stae goment move very fast to fully implement dis new plan so we go fit put dis farmers - herders clash wey dey apun fromtime to time behind us .
Di convocation of National Dialogue , wey be major demand of di Asaba declaration fit no dey necessary since report from di 2014 National Conference plus recommendations of di Gov .
El - Rufai - led APC committee on True Federalism dey .
Di two report be make far reaching recommendation wey di governor dem wey we elect and dem legislator for inside di national assembly fit agree on , instead of make dem waste resource wey no dey on top anoda jamboree .
On to di issue of separatist agitations dem , make dem bring modalities to take do referendum as e be inside di constitution .
E dey almost certain say plenty majority of Nigeria pipo wan live togeda , dem no mind awa differences .
To do dis go take di sail komo for di wind of divisive elemnet dem , wey dey fan fire of hate and discord .
di Southern Governor dem don affirm dem commitment to one United Nigeria on top basis of justice , fairness and equity , so must evri patriotic Nigerian .
Though we get challenge dem like evri oda kontri , we must listen to awasefs as US President Joe Bidden dey often tok .
Tomori dey live for Abuja

Dem parade 22 mummies of Pharaoh dem inside Egypt
Na twenty - two mummies of pharaoh wlk for di street of Cairo on saturday evening for one stunning royal procession from Egyptian Museum on Tahrir Square to di new National Museum of Egyptian Civilization ( NMEC ) in Fustat .
Na di event mark as dem take launch NMEC officially .
Against di backdrop of fireworks , di mummies """" 18 kings and four queens """" travelled in order of age on purpose - built gold - colored pharaonic chariots , equipped wit an air ride suspension system to absorb vibrations , and bearing di name of dia occupants in Arabic , English , and hieroglyphics .
Seqenenre Tao II wey rule Upper Egypt around 1 , 600 BCE , lead di parade , as Ramses ix , wey rule for di 12th century BCE bring up di rear .
As e follow di strict international standard for di transport of artifacts , dem place di royal remain for state - of - the - art sterile display cases to guarantee dem immaculate preservation .
Na 60 motorcycles , 150 horses , and a pharaonic music ensemble wey renowned Egyptian maestro Nader Abbassiconduct follow di mummie .
Di procession start with a 21 - gun salute , circled the obelisk for di Tahrir Square wey dey close , and then proceeded along di Nile to NMEC , wia Egyptian President Abdel Fattah El - Sisi personally welkom di mummies to dia new permanent home in Fustat , di National Museum of Egyptian Civilization .
Di parade wey last for 40 - minutes catch participation of 12 celeb for inside Egypt , as 200 + global TV channels broadcast am .
Di pricelees artifact dem go spend di next two weeks for di NMECs laboratory , wia dem go prepare dem for installation inside di Royal Mummies Hall , wey dey for di valley of di kings .
Dem go open di Royal Mummies Hall to visitors for April 18 , wey don jam with World Heritage Day .
To promote di launch , NMEC dey offer 50 percent discount for entry ticket price to di Central Exhibition Hall for visitor from April 4 go enter 17 .
To add join , representatives of local and international media get di opportunity to take picture and video di artifacts inside di Central Exhibition Hall for free on April 4 and 5 .
Overlooking Ain Al Sirafor di heart of di historical city of ustat wey near Babylon Fortress , NMEC na one of di largets and most important archeology museums wey dey di world .
and di first to last for di whole civilization for inside Egypt .

Farmers go benefit from mechanised farm for inside Jigawa
Di Malam Alu Agro Allied Company , wey be farm wey dey on top 100 - hectare of land inside Faru village , along Maiduguri road , Birnin Kudu Local Government Area of Jigawa State , don dey change di prception inside mechanised farming for Nigeria , di GM for di Mansur Dau Aliyu tok .
As dem take establish di farm almost five years ago , as we gather , na direct response to di call by di administration of President Muhammadu Buhari tok say make Nigeria return to agriculture as di mainstay of di economy for inside di nation , pass as dem dey rely on top iol as di source of revenue for inside di kontri .
Each cattle get nomba tag wey dem attach to am for ear .
Founder for di company , Farouk Adamu Aliyu , wey be former member for inside House of Representative key into am , di GGM add .
We dey do greenhouse farming .
We get 10 , 000 square - metre wey be fully automated soilles greenhouse , wia we dey produce tomato .
We also get two 250 square - metre greenhouses wia we dey produce oda greenhouse vegetable dem , plus anoda 500 square - metre greenhouse , wey we dey use as nursery .
Dis greenhouse dem na all dey foreign - oriented , wey we don install to take produce variety of vegetable .
Na only tomato wey dey produce for di 10 , 000 square automated soilless greenhousedem ; and we produce an average of 10 to 11 ton of tomato evri week .
We be get anoda 10 , 000 square - metre locally fabricated greenhouse .
We also get livestock section , wia we get over 300 herds of cattle , some camel , goat and sheep , as e take tok am .
Daily Trust hear say di farm also get fishery unit , with about 50 , 000 fish inside di pond .
Similarly , one forty - ton per hour fertilizer blending plant wey dem install for early part of di year , as we take hear , don dey produce reach 300 loads of NPK fertilizer under di Presidential Fertilizer Initiative .
We don import equipment wey fit install 120 , 000 capacity for poultry system .
We hope say we go dey produce reach between 3 , 000 - 4 , 000 crates of egg for inside one day , as Mansur take tok .
He tok say di farm , also get plant wia dem dey do diary , wey dey produce 2 , 000 litres of milk inside one day , he add say dem also get about 150 - 200 hectres of land elsewia wey dem leave for open field farming plus cultivation of rice and oda crops dem .
Masur tok say major pipo wey dey buy di tomato na premium customers , notably , big big hotel for inside Abuja and Lagos , plus some oda location .
He confirm , however , say di main market for di product na mainly inside eastern part of di kontri like Enugu , Onitsha , Owerri .
However , he admit say apart from di small customers dem wey dem get for Kano , dem no too dey see dem tomato product for local market fpr some kind reason .
First na di fact say di tomato wey dem produce form dem farm na special specie and di second reason be di fact say Jigawa na major area wey dem for dey produce tomato .
You know say tomato na common product for here , so ouw price high small pass wetin dey open market .
So , essentially , pipo no actually dye look awa side , dem dey fell apprehensive wit wetin we get bikos dem believe say e dey cost .
And when you get product wey dey available for evriwia , e sure say pipo go buy di one wey cheap pass .
Na one farm hand dey feed di fish dem .
As dem ask about di average lifespan of dem tomato product , he tok say , if you give di tomato evritin wey e take , i mean say nutrional supplement wey you take feed am as e dey grow , if you give am all of dis things dem , di tomato fit last reach three weeks afta harvest .
But even without am , e go last for minimum of one week , no be for refrigeration , and no be for inside presure and plenty heat .
You fit put am on top table wia better ventilation dey .
E fit last for average of 10 days , but if dem provide evritin as e take require ( evri nutrient ) e fit last reach one month .
We don experiment am , but then , e no dey apun as you dey always want .
Di farm na source of employment for pipo wey reach 200 inside di village wia dem locate am .
He also tok say di company get some pipo to kom train di youth for di araea on information technology skil dem .
He tok further say most of di equipment wey dem use for di farm na from Turkey , except di fertilizer - blending machine , wey dem import from China .
He tok say even di farming method na like as e be for Turkey , bikos dem get Turkish partner wey dey help dem to maintain di standard , but quickly he add say di company dey conscious to allow Nigeria pipo to dey run di tachnical aspect of im operation .
As e dey reflect on top di effect of COVID - 19 on top di operation of di company , Mansur tok say , Malam Alu , as oda corporate entities for di kontri , suffer from devastating effect of di virus .
For Mansur , youth for Nigeria no get excuse to remain unemployed with di kind opportunity wey agriculture dey provide , e note say di pipo wey dey lokk for white - collar job make dem adjust to di reality and go back to agriculture .
He believe say Nigeria don dey do wetin im suppose to done do long time before , e note say if di kontri don take dis step , dem for don corner di present economic wahala .

No doubt say football fans dem for inside Nigeria dey wait eagerly for di 2020 / 2021 UEFA Champions League finals wey go apun tonight wey two English clubs dem Manchester City and Chelsea go contest for inside di Estadio do Dragao , Porto in Portugal .

Dem be former chsmpion .

do Dragao for Porto and di men dem wey go take charge of di technical area .

duo of George Findi and Nwankwo Kanu lift am with Ajax Amsterdam for 1995 .

Farmers dem dey apprehensive as planting season begin with erratic rain dem
As wet season don begin for most part of di season , farmer don begin palntin with fear as rain dey erratic and e fit threaten production .
Rain dey unsatble for Benue , Nasarawa , Niger , Kaduna and part of di Federal Capital Territory ( FCT ) , and plenty farmer dem don plant dem crop .
For di 2019 / 2020 wet season , erratic rain for di north and mid - season draught for di south - west make farmers dem loss money due to crop failure .
Musa Yohana and Halima Thomas , farmers for inside Doma and Lafia , Nasarawa State , tok say dem don plant maize , groundnut plus oda crops dem like casava and yam but fear say dem fit get anoda horrible experience like last season when dem dey forced to plant maize and groundnut two times .
I loss my yam last year due to heat wey dey too much bikos rain no fall welwel .
Dis year , we don dey second week for May but rain neva dey fall welwel .
And I don already plant 15 measure ( about 20kg ) of groundnut .
If e kontinu like dis for anoda one week , I fit loss all di seed dem , as Mr Yohana take tok .
Like dem , plenty farmer around di FCT don plant too , but dem get big fear for crop failure as experience last year .
For Benue state , For Benue state , awa correspondent reprot say farmer don begin to cultivate land and plant crop on top complain say rain no fall .
Some farmer wey don prepare dem farm earlier in di tear tok say dem no fit begin to dey plant until one week ago , as odas dem just begin to clear land at di wake of di rainfall three times withing two weeks wey pass .
One farmer for Otukpo , Ada hyacinth , tok say di ground still dey too strong to cultivate bikos di rain no dey fall frequent .
Anoda farmer wey be Felix Tor , for Makurdi tok say im just plant melon and maize on di farm wey im just clear despite as rain no dey consistent .
Tor be however express fear say di nature of di rainfall fit affect di well - being of di crop .
He pray make di yield do better in di end .
But Vitalis Tarnongu , we don dey clear im 1 , 000 hectares of farmland for di federal Unversity of Agriculture , inside Makurdi ( FUAM ) , tok say as di rain dey fall dis year go make am begin to plant maize towards di end of May .
Tarnongu tok say one plant breeder for inside University don advise am to wait until May 20 to start to dey plant im maize bikos di nature of di rainfall since di season don suggest say e possible make rain no fall for two weeks .
Di sate chairman of di All Farmers Association of Nigeria ( AFAN ) , Aondongu Saaku , describe farmin as business wey worth make dem take risk on .
Saaku tok say farmers wey dey see am as business don take di risk to plent dia crop already bikos without dat kind risk dem no go reap at di end of di day .
Meanwhile , Dr Teryima Iorlamen , wey be seed system specialist for FUAm , tok say farmers dem fit go ahead to plant dem root and tuber crops as e follow di prediction of rainfall wey NIMET make dis year .
Iorlamen tok say di period wey dem expect say farmers dem go wait don pass , e stress say di prediction of NIMET on top rainfall pattern inside Benue State , which dem ( experts ) dey work wit , don indicate say rain go stabilise for di state between April 18 and April 30 , 2021 .
We fit assure farmers now say rain don stabilise , accordin to prediction wey NIMET make .
Anything wey different for now go be dry spell .
I don advise farmers dem to check water logging capacity for inside dem field so dem go fit plant dem crops as dem suppose plant am .
Rice like plenty water , so time neva reach to plant am .
But farmers dem fit enter root and tuber now , dat one include yam , cassava , maize and melon .
We believe say di rain don stabilise .

How cassava don dey is become gold inside Benue
For inside Benue State , farmers don dey expand dem fields almos evri season to take increase production as cassava farin don bikom better business for inside di three senatorial district dem .
Although na di state dem know as state wey dey produce and chop yam pass for inside di kontri , cassava don dey reign gradually .
As such , dem tok say more farmers dem don dey plant cassava .
One cassava farmer for di Gboko area of di stste , Titus Atondo , tok say he begin to plant di crop for many years now .
Atondo tok say cassava farming no dey too get plenty challenge bikos farmers only need to spray di farm once to repel weed , den dem go wait for harvest .
Cassava chips don dey very expensive now .
I get large cassava farm wia I dey make money and my family sef dey chop some of di produce , as e take tok am .
Faith Ben don dey prepare large land for inside di Ugboju area of Otukpo Local Goment Area to take cultivate cassava as soon as rain start to fall , dis one na as dem dey demand for di product welwel for her vicinity .
Di demand for cassava dey high welwel nowadays .
From di tubers go enter di di one wey dem don process , e don bikom crop wey dey bring money .
Na y I dey enter di farming be dat .
She add say na for business alone she dey do am .
For im own part , di stste chairman of di All Farmers Association of Nigeria ( AFAN ) , Aondongu Saaku , admit say dem don dey chop cassava for di state pass yam sef .
Saaku tok dis one bikos dem dey chop cassava for many variety , unlike yam .
Meanwhile , di Director of Agric Science for di Ministry of Agriculture and Natural Resources , Thomas Unongo , explain say cassava farming don dey do well for di state in recent times bikos no aspekt for di crop dey wasted .
Unongo wey get farm wey be three and half hectres for Apir , Makurdi tok say for di past two years , im don dey cultivate di land with new varieties of cassava wey di International Institute of Tropical Agriculture ( IITA ) dem release .
Apart from say dem dey kontrol weed , na one of di crops wey cheap pass to grow .
To produce rice dey cost between N200 , 000 and N300 , 000 for one hectare , as yam dey cost between N150 , 000 and N200 , 00 per hectare , but input for cassava production with stems for farmer dey only cost N150 , 000 .
And wia dem get light vegetation , e fit low reach N100 , 000 .
He tok say e dey chaep and di output / return on top investment na one of di highest for Benue now .
Unongo further note say di challenge of farming cassava for di state dey on top insecurity as herders attack dey worse .
He allege say herders dem dey komot di stem and tuber for dem cattle .
However , he advise say to get better yield , pesin go need to apply weed kontrol three months afta dem palnt am , e stress say wen dem allow weed to grow for insie di farm , dem dey invite pest like grasshoppers dem .
He tok say inputs like fertlizer , herbicides dem , among oda things dey necessary , he add say need dey to dey do farm sanitation , wey go help against attack of rodents dem .
Unongo maintain say as d old variety of cassava go last reach two years before harvest , with one year maturity , di new improved varieties get maturity period of five and seven months , but na eight month better pass for harvest .
Cassava farming don dey turn to gold for inside Benue bikos di state dey near to north , wia dem no dey produce di crop .
Also , the produce , especially garri , don dey cost more bikos vendors dem don dey evriwia for villages dem mopping up di chips wey dem desire to sell go Northern market , as he take note am .

Prominent indigene for Lagos under di name of Eko Pataki don ask Governor Babajide Sanwo - Olu to begin to revolution for agriculture inside di state .
Di indigene dem make dis call against as di recent decision to take block supply of food to di south by di Amalgamated Union of Food Stuff and Cattle Dealers in Nigeria ( AUFCDN ) .
As dem dey raect on top di development yesterday , di group tok say need dey for goment to redirect dem policy towards to broad agriculture investment in order to help food surficiency for di state .
Dis one dey inside joint statement by di leader of di group Chief Bode George , and its trustees , Gen Tajudeen Olanrewaju and Mr Gbadebo Dallas .
Di group cahrge di governor to engage di plenty youth wey no get employment for di state to take drive di agricultural revolution .
Part of di statement read say : di recent action of di Amalgamated Union of Food Stuff and Cattle Dealers in Nigeria wey no allow trailers dem to bring tomatoes , pepper , onions and all kind o foodstuff enter south suppose wake di leadership of lagos State to redirect dem policies to take widen dem investment for inside agriculture .
Lagos State wey be awa foremost concern as Eko Pataki make dem begin impress into immediate duty for huge workforce of di youth wey no get employement for inside di IBILE traditional enclave , as dem dey turn awa vast and enriched land into agricultural holding .
From Ifako - Ijaiye to Imota , from Epe to di rolling fields to di mangroves of Badagry , Lagos State dey blessed wit agricultural fields wey get nutrient wey fit quickly turn to farmland wia different kind of crop like tomatoes , lettuce , pepper , beans , rice , corn , yam , potatoes , cassava go reach many odas wey dem fit plant to take enhance awa sef - sufficiency for food production .
Na awa candid advise to Governor Sanwo - Olu to quickly re - order di state priority to take make sure say awa state bikom di new food basket for di kontri to thereby trigger new agricultural revolution for inside di state of excellence .
China wan raise di proportion of middle - income earners
Di consumption of China don dey continue to rise for recent years , and dem dey optimise im conumption structure .
Last year , di total retail sales of consumer goods for inside di kontri reach 39 . 2 trillion yuan ( $ 6 trillion ) , and final consumption be contribute 54 . 3 per cent to di GDP of China .
DI result na say China still be di second - largest consumption market for di world .
New business like online shopping and influencer marketing don experience rapid development .
For 2020 , dem show over 24 million levestream on top e - commerce platforms , online sales of national entity becked di trend and grow reach 14 . 8 per cent .
di express delivery industry handle 31 . 2 per cent more parcels dan last year .
China don turn largest market for online retailing for eight years straight .
Di robust recovery of China's consumption , despite di severe impact of COVID - 19 don show di strong resilience and huge development potential of di Chinese market .
As major force for consumption , na pillar di middle - income group be for di economy .
For present , China get 400 million middle - income earner dem wey dey account for around 30 per cent of dem population .
For kontri dem wey don develop , di distribution of household income dey always come for olive shape form wey dey sharp for di two end and e plump for di middle .
For oda words , for kontri wey don develop di middle - income group dey usually accpount for 60 per cent go reach 70 percent of di population .
Dem dey consider dat kind structure as say dem dey healthy and good for economic and social development .
In contrast , China way still far to take expand di size of im middle - income group .
Vice - Minister of Commerce Qian Keming tok say with 1 . 4 billion pipo , China get large market and huge development potential .
For di next fifteen years , dem expect say make di nomba of Chinese middle - income don reach 800 million , wey go generate robust momentum for consumption upgrading plus bright prospects .
According to di 14th Five - Year Plan of China , China go work to increase di income for graduates of universeties dem and vocational schools , skiled workers and migrants workers dem for di next five years .
Experts dem believe say e dey possible and necessary to put dem for di middle - income group .
Graduates of university and vocational school dem plenty and are dey well educated and get skil , wey make am possible for dem to become middle - income earners .
Most pipo for dis group , with dem degree of education and competence no go wan do simple and repetive work , so e dey possible say make dem bikom middle - income earners , Su Hainan , wey be contract research fellow with China Association for Labor Studies , tell People's Daily during one interview .
According to di latest statistics from di Ministry of Human Resources and Social Security ( MOHRSS ) , China get over 200 million skiled workers wey take 26 per cent of dem total job , up from 20 per cent few years ago .
More dan 50 million of dem be skiled worker .
For recent years , skiled workers no reach for China , and dem income don kontinu to det rise .
Di MOHRSS issue one guideline recently , wey dem encourage enterprises to institute annual salary system and offer special award for skiled talents , esecially di ones wey get high skil .
Su tok say migrant workers na major part of workforce for inside China , many of dem sef dey well educated and dem get skil , and dem no dey able to do complicated and innovative works dem .
Last year , di nomba of migrant worker for inside China reach 280 million , plus 180 wey work out of town .
Di average income wey dem dey get per month stay for 4 , 072 yuan .
Plenty among dem don dey get close to di threshold of middle income if dem take terms of household calculate am .
To make part of dem imigrant worker to become middle - income earners dey necessary to take marrow di rural - urban income gap , to take improve di competence of workforce and accelerate rural vitalization , and e lso dey feasible to am , as Su take note
As di income of dis major group go rise for future , dem go expand di size di middle - income group for China , dat one go turn di household income distribution to olive shape .
By dat time , dem go don further actuvate di consumption vitality of China , and di kontri go release more dividends to di world .

( II ) Why secession no be di silver bullet to di problem wey Nigeria get ( II )
Di pipo wey dey do say make Nigeria break up put am on top three main reason dem ; di amalgation of northern and southern protectorate for 1914 wey born Nigeria , di charter of sef determination for inside United Nation plus lack of representation and marginalisation for inside di affairs of di kontri .
The mind say na di amalgamation of 1914 wey secessionist group dey say be di foundamental move wey cause plenty inside di current challenge dem wey dey face Nigeria need make dem challenge welwel and debunk am totally .
For dis regard , e go benefit us to know say amalgation be don apun earlier for 1906 wia dem merge di Lagos colony wey don dey since 1862 wit southern protectorate .
Like di 1914 amalgamation wey follow wey dey enervate di secession pipo dem , di amalgamation wey apun for 1906 too na force dem take do am between entity dem wey no dey willing and dem get little or no cultural similarity .
Wetin di pipo of costal state for inside Niger Delta region get culturally and historically wit Yoruba pipo of southwest ?
Wetin be di historical and cultural link wey di Igbo wey dey for east hinterland get wit Yoruba for dat matter ?
As far as we fit see am , di reason to take reject di amalgamation of 1914 go reach for di one of 1906 on top say na force dem force di two against pipo wey get different history and culture .
Why secession pipo dey only tok about di 1914 amalgamation to take press dem demand and dem dey neglect di one wey apun for 1906 ?
Di reason dem dey simple bikos for dem own narrow political tok wey dey try justify North vs South secessionist agenda na di 1914 amalgamation enter am pass .
E no go form beta strategy if dem dey also tok about di amalgamation wey dey essential , by import and effect , and e dey similar to di one wey apun for 1914 .
How e go take look for instance if Oduduwa secessionist tok say na bikos of si amalgamation for 1906 di Igbo wey get different history and culture don kom dominate di economic and commercial life inside Lagos and as such di Oduduwa dey seek to komot for di marriage with Igbo wey di British pipo be force on top dem .
or di Igbo dey say na di amalgamation of 1906 kos the bad nature of economic infrastructure wey dem concentrate put for Southwest wey dey carry dem ( Igbo ) kom invest for Lagos economic zone rather than di East wey go dey convienient pass ?
Anoda falacy wey dem carry concerning di 1914 amalgamation be wey Nigerian entity dem represent sign be say e supoose expire afta hundred years wey mean say na 2014 .
Say Nigeria still dey exist afta im expiry date na somethingg wey secessionist dem still dey try to instigate oda Nigeria pipo against and make sure say dem end of dis joinjoin wey don expire as dem dey call am .
Again dis one na near tok wey no get leg .
By 1914 di British don get full and total kontrol of di territory wey we dey cal Nigeria now and all di entities as dem be don dey under British rule .
Dem don establish di British colonial rule on top Nigeria and na dat one make di amalgamation pure administrative measure by colonial overload wey im no need permision from im subject to carry am out .
For this regard di amalgamation no fit get time to expire as dem dey claim , and e no get .
If time ever dey for di amalgamation to take expire as dem dey claim , e suppose be for di end di British colonial enterprise wey be say at di same time no be British go determine am .
If any genuine document dey wey carry di terms and condition of di 1914 amalgamation wey include pipo wey represent various pre - existing Nigerian entities plus clause wey dey state di clause for di expiry , na di work od di pipo wey dey pray for Nigeria to break up to present am as proof .
For any case , even if such document dey , as Nigeria take get independence for 1960 e no go dey valid again bikos na evri entity for Nigeria dey take part wit di representative wey dem elect to take discuss and agree on top di new kontri .
If di kind agreement wey dem dey carry about di amalgamation dey anywia and if di parti dem wey follow tok about di independence agree to retain am and dem include am inside di independence constitution , e for don bikom relevant constitution and legal case for di secession entity to take cite dem agitation .
On top di issue of di UN provision on sef - determination as dem take cite am for dem secession action , e dey important make dem get two important point for mind .
Di UN no be world goment wey get executive power to take stamp dem will on top national goment dem .
Kontri fit use di principle of sovereignty to take block any resolution wey UN make if dem see say e no follow dem national interest .
Although Nigeria follow sign to di UN charter wey di provision of sef - determination follow , e fit and dem get right to block attempt from any group withing wey wan break di kontri if dem use dat provision .
Thus even as e dey unlike say any group break away from Nigeria and UN support am , Nigeria fit use dem sovereign right to stand against such move .
But di thing wey dey more significant be say although di UN charter dey providde sef detrmination , di UN don place great onus to take seek dem credential and case comprehensively .
Di process to take ssek and to eventually get di support of UN for sef - determination bid dey very complicated and covoluted one wey fit take year to set and e still fit no get success at di end .
Those seeking to invoke di UN principle of sef - determination for dia secessionist bid must first of all prove say dem get di mandate of di pipo of di area dey seek to represent through popular elections or referendum and not through di media or internet .
Di pipo wey dey try to evoke UN principle of sef - determination for dem secessionst bid must firts prove say dem dey do wetin pipo for di area wey dem dey represent want wit popular election or referendum no be through media or internet .
Dem must to show proof say di area wey want do secession dem don dey deny dem or say dem no get adequate representation for local , state and national level of di goment of di kontri .

Dr Mahmud Tukur : Tribute to distinguished accomplishment
For di end , no be year for pesin life count , but di life wey dey inside pesin years Abraham Lincoln
Di small space wey dey here no reach to describe di late Dr Mahmud Muhammad Tukur , politician for inside Nigeria and former minister on top commerce and industry matter for di administration of General Muhammadu Buhari .
Tukur wey follow among one small clique of policy advocates for Northern Nigeria , die for April 9 , 2021 , for 82 years old .
Dem don bury since for Yola , inside Adamawa State .
Dr Tukur na di 1st indigenous Director of di Institute of Administration , Kongo , Zaria .
He kolekt di mantle from Prof . S . S . Richardson for 1967 go reach 1975 when im bekom first vice - chancellor of di Bayero University for Kano ,
Now recall say na late Sir Ahmadu Bello , di Sardauna of Sokoto , who when im attain independence of nothern Nigeria , declare for front of Sir Garwin Westray Bell wey be di last Governor - General for 1957 , for di Lugard Hall inside Kaduna , say di commitment to train di manpower for di north , which according to dem , we go rely on top di attainment of improving di health , prosperity , hapines of awa pipo wey discrimination no ge dey on ground of tribe or creed of which Dr
. Tukur and small oda nomba wey dey distinguished be di pipo wey dem first recruit .
Some don tok di journet of Presido Muhammadu Buhari into politics no go complete without Tukur .
Yes , doubt no de , di description wey dem give Tukur say im dey among di intellectual powerhouse na true since im na contemporary wit pipo like Mamman Daura , Liman Ciroma , Adamu Ciroma , and Hamza Rafindadi Zayyad .
Mahmud Tukur be firm , tenacious and resolute man wey lead life wey get impact , man wey get deep conviction and inner streght , wey serve North without corruption and e enhance di betterment of democracy for di kontri .
Under am as Director , Institute of Administration , Zaria , im supervise and superintend di building of di intelligentsia fo North and e be dey deeply committed wit strong sense of duty to take build Nigeria wey dey equitable .
E dey safe to deduce then , say entire genre of civil servants dem past and current , executives dem for private sector and political elite for di North be pass through di hand of di late scholar wet affect evri facet of education and see to di upliftment of manpower no be only for im region but for Nigeria in general .
President Muhammadu , for inside tribute to Tukur , tok say geberation dem go remember Dr Mahmud Tukur service to di nation .
E get passion for Nigeria wey go dey prosper , get strong economy and dey unite .
Na proud nationalist e be .
Buhari remeber say as Minister of Trade for im first comin as Head of States , Dr Tukur be introduce plenty scheme wey revive di local industry , e boost export and give real meanin and effect to import substitution to regenerate di indigenous manufacturin secor for di economy .
He pray give Almighty Allah to accept am for Aljannah Firdaus and give im family , friends , di Adamawa Emirate Council and di pipo for inside di state di strenght to bear di great loss .
Indeed , di enviable position and competence of Tukur be increase im public profile for Nigeria .
Indeed e go take to do plenty good things to take build good perutation , therefore di contribution wey Tukur put to take develop di education sector durin im time for Bayero University and im tireless effort on top peacebuilding process and socio - economic development of Norther Nigeria no sometin wey dem fit forget .
Late Tukur , wey dem born for 1939 inside Yola , Adamawa State , get im first degree for International Affairs and Political Science for di University of Wales ( wia im receive Elizabeth Morris Memorial Prize as im graduate first for im class ) .
He also obtain Master's Degree in Public International Affairs for di University of Pittsburgh and PhD .
in Public Management for Ahmadu Bello University , Zaria , Kaduna .
He also study for Northwestern and Oxford university dem .
Di deceased be Fulbright - Hays Fellow , senior I . U . C . Fellow and associate member of St . Anthony's College , Oxford ( 1974 ) .
He enter history as di first Vice - Chancelor for Bayero University , for Kano .
For im career as public servant , di scholar wey dey prominent and get fame worldwide be serve for di Adebo and Udoji National Wage Reviews and committee wey dratf Constitution of 1976 , he also be member of di sub - committee on top citizenship right , fundamental right , Political Parties and Electoral System wey Alhaji Aminu Kano be Chairman for .
E be member of di National Constitutional Conference ( 1994 \ 1995 ) and di Committee for vision 2010 ( 1997 ) .
For 1984 , when Major General Muhammadu Buhari be dey do military regime , Federal goment appoint am as Minister for Commerce and Industries .
A business executive , late Tukur be chair for di activities of Fukarabe Industries Limited , Kaduna , and e fulfill di obligation of plenty corporate dictatorship dem .
Leadership and Governance in Nigeria : He be Coordinator for Policy Analysis Limited and write and join pipo to write plenty book dem , wey di one wey prominent pass na :
Di Relevance of Values , wey dem publish for 1999 .
Na three wives dem survive am , nine children and plenty broda dem wey dey distinguished , wey include di prominent global industrialist and business mogul wey dem worldwide Alhaji Bamanga Tukur , wey be former Governor for inside Gongola State wey no dey again , one time Minister of Industries and past chairman for di People's Democratic Party ( PDP ) and Late Engr Hamman Tukur former Director - General for Federal Ministry of Petroleum Resources and di first Chairman , Revenue Mobilization and Fiscal Commission .
We dey commiserate with Nigeria pipo on top di quench of dis courageous academic , who apart from say na match - maker , be get more distinguished career for service give di nation .
Nigeria go surely miss di statesmanship of Dr Mahmud wey dem born for inside Adamawa , na enigma durin im lifetime , he display genuine magnanimity and moral courage , and e always dey put interest of nation above di one of ethnic or group .
Im reputation na say e dey follow due process , im na indeed bridge builder , e dey always readi to use im wisdon plus knowledge wey im don gain over di years for di good of im kontri .
Dr Tukur be man of peace and im deligence and professionalismno dey questionable wey im death na great loss for Nigeria .
He be live life wey get impact and contribute plenty to Nigeria and e don put im name for platter of gold for inside di history of di kontri .
All of us must to keep im service patriotic duty for peaceful and secure kontri .
Make di federal goment immortalise am as per make dem name anything wey dey follow education or di Institute of Administration ABU Zaria as im remebrance .
Indeed Nigeria don loss rare gem , na patriotic Nigerian par excellence , na academic extraordinaire and na great author , wey don serve dis nation wit merit , man wey get strong character and convistion wey live life wit impact wey any pesin fit wish for , as e follow im well defined role for di growth of humanity and im untiring commitment for inside nation - building .
we no fit forget im contribution for di history of awa nation and continent
For di end , as Abraham Lincoln don assert , no be year inside pesin life count , di life wey dey inside pesin years .
Make Allah SWT uplift im work and grant am Aljannar Firdaus .

How support tool , order fit uplift 41 . 5m MSMEs
Nigeria Micro , small and Medium Enterprises MSMEs industry no dey optimise as e suppose be upon dia critical role for national development
although MSMEs contribution for di Gross Domestic Product GDP neva clear bikos of lack structure and data , di narrative dey change fast
Accordin to data wey di small and Medium scale Enterprises Development Agency of Nigeria SMEDAN and di National Bureau of Statistics NBS , e dey about 41 . 5million MSMEs for Nigeria
Togeda , dia account na about 50 percent for Nigeria GDP
To dey grow consciousness na critical role MSMEs play for economic development
Afta job creation , MSMEs dey critical to dey improve di livin standard of citizen wey local capital formation
Dey kom hep drive innovertion and competition for developin economies
As dey wan boost di growth of MSMEs , plenti MSMEs - supported programmes don dey from di federal goment thru di Development Bank of Nigeria ( DBN ) , Bank of Industry ( BOI ) , Bank of Agriculture ( BOA ) , SMEDAN and di Central Bank of Nigeria ( CBN ) wey don be di biggest enabler of small small business dem .
Di CBN intervene wit di growth of MSMEs ,
Apart from say public sector sponsor initiative , private sector entities dey wey dey strive to support MSMEs sector
One of dis na di MTN Revv programme wey dey hep small business think well , make learn dia operation well join so e go allow dem mitigate di effect of COVID - 19 pandemic .
Dis year , 200 MSMEs na hin dey select make e be part of MTN accelerator programme , yello 200 , from across di kontri
Di participant don get series of 11 master class by season facilitator pass various subsector for di economy
For di graduation ceremony recently , some beneficiaries and coodinator speak for di programme
olubukola Ogunmola wey be di CEO of Wanbuk and Device wey dey produce pap , tok say him get plenti benefit
awa workforce don dey grow to allow us meet di demand of awa growin customers
Anoda beneficiary , Daniel Ikwong , CEO of Future IDEAS tok say : I been dey well equipped wit best practices dem and I enjoy every bit of the Yello 200 onboardin experience wella ; di business no go be di same again .
Also , Raheem Yusuff Olatunji wey be di CEO , Yutex Entertainment tok say for am , di programme na for rewardin experience
now I be beta manager for my business
E fit don apun for beta time bikos di effect of Covid 19 pandemic wey dey on top my company plenti
Di chief Enterprise Business Officer , MTN Nigeria
Lynda Saint Nwafor tok say wit MSMEs wey go dey account for 94 % for all business for Nigeria and 84 % for employment
awa goal na to empower MSMEs wit di tool to make dem thrive for di economy
Modupe Kadri , Chief Financial Officer , MTN Nigeria , tok say : We don always believe SMEs as wheels wey dey drive any economy and if you position dem for growth , e mean say you dey empower and you wan enable dem wit di right digital solutions .
Make we no do ojoro , Coca Cola Nigeria Limited and di Whitefield Foundation , e no tey wey dem empower pass 20 , 000 person wey get business skil for di 36 state of Nigeria through di special intervention programme SIP
Dem tok say through SIP , dey don fi support di livelihood of young Nigeria pipo wey dey follow di economic effect of Covid 19 pandemic wey hit 2020
By di end of di programme for April , di pipo don complete thre different stage of course wey season facilitors dem dey do
As dem dey do graduation recently , di Director , Public Affairs , Communications and Sustainability of di firm , Nwamaka Onyemelukwe tok say : We notice say unemployment rates dey rise wit poverty rates as dem reach one peak , and as a socially - responsible company wey focus on refreshin di world , we also dey committed to makin difference for di lives of pipo and communities dem .
Founder , Whitefield Foundation , Olufunmilola Johnson tok say , We dey excited di success of SIP and dis initiative apun bikos of di nd to hep make more successful people wey go grow our economy for Nigeria .

dem give bag wey dem use hand do to important women wey dey di event
Reason why Katsina farmers dem record poor harvest
Zobo farmer for Katsina State don record decline for product even as small rain fall dey dis year
Di farmers tok say di poor harvest na as bikos of di absence of affordable fertiliser from di beginnin wey rain season and invasion of dia farm by di herdsmen wey kom from Niger Republic
Dey kom dey lament continue say di relocation of some of dia market and lack of goment support dey part of dia major challenge dis year
Dey kom observe say di heavy rain wey fall , wey dem record toward end of season no favour di roselle plant , e no make dem grow to dia usual height , wey go don enable am to produce seed wey good wey fi produce zobo
farmer wey dem sabi wella Malam Abdullahi Kwangwama
Malam Abdullahi Kwangwana , wey be zobo farmer for Mani Local goment Area for di state , for wan interview wey Daily Trust do , tok say from di beginnin of last season na hin manure or fertiliser to apply to plant no dey , situation wey slow down hin growth
Malam Kwangwama tok say , we no get any fertiliser from goment truout di season , and na dat one make am difficult for plant grow early
Di small bag wey we fi buy for market for N12 , 000 per bag kom late and e no fi help grow high reach chest , wey e dey normally high reach so tey e go fit produce plenti seed
No too plant plenti food crop dis year
And I only fit harvest 60 bag of hibiscus dis season , against 85 bag wey I get last year
I get two wife and eight pikin , six of dem dey school , and na di only hope wey I get to feed dem and to dey pay dia school fee
goment wan support us to dey produce zobo for commercial quantity for domestic use for Nigeria and export , wetin dey need do na to make adequate plan to provide plan for di provision of fertiliser for cheap price and support farmer to dey access loan wey no get interest wey fi allow us hire pipo , kom cultivate more farmland
Na bikos say buyers dey always wait for produce , and wey dey to do well
Di roselle seed coat or cover na hin dem dey use produce d popular zobo juice for Nigeria , wey dey consider use for di treatment of stomach pain , high blood pressure , weight loss , among odas
For some kontri , dem dey use am for tea production , colourin , dyein , drug production and bicosmetic
anoda farmer and merchant of zobo , Ali Makeri , complain say one of di challenge wey dem face na di relocation of di market by di authority of Mashi Local goment Area , wey am tok say e dey affect patronage
Accordin to am , di market don relocate plenti time to different place , wey far from Mashi main market
Hin later tok say even if we pay revenue to di local goment kom create job for ova five time dem dey relocate us from one bushy area to anoda
Once wey dem discover say we don settle , kom develop one particular place , dey go don kom ovanight kom take us go anoda place wey neva open
Di last one na for dis year wen dey bring us kom here , close to di Mashi Ultra Modern Market
E dey far from di main market and awa customer dey fear to kom here , for security purpose
Therefore , we dey beg di chairman make he reason wit us and make he give us permanent and convenient place wey go dey close to di main market because most of our customers kom from different parts of di kontri ; and dey go dey comfortable if we dey close to di main market .
On top di mata say whether zobo farmer for Katsina State get di capacity to produce large quantity for export , Makeri tok say ; why dey no fit
Na hundreds of man and woman wey be hibiscus farmer dey for Katsina State bikos say e dey bring moni .
Last year alone , we sell am for N8 , 000 per bag from di beginnin , and for some point , e reach N20 , 000 per bag
wetin we need na support
If goment fit attract investor here and dey kom build factory wey fit supply us wit fertiliser , equipment and loan to hire more pipo , I fit assure you say we go generate more revenue for Nigeria
anoda farmer , Malam Yusuf Gwani Gobirawa for Kaita Local goment Area complain say herdsmen from neighbourin Niger Republic invade dia farm before dey fi finish harvest dis year
Him tok say awa hibiscus no ripe well wen we notice di herdsmen from Niger Republic arrive kom start to dey push dia animal for awa farm
Howeva , di member wey dey represent us for House of Assembly intervene through awa tradition ruler and dey kom tell us say make we quick harvest anythin wey remain for awa farm in order to avoid clash wit dem herdsmen
I get only 45 bag instead of 70 to 80
I dey expect dis year
awa borders no dey secure
goment need check di activity of dis herdsmen from Niger Republic by closin di border , especially if e kom towards di end of season so we go fit peacefully harvest awa farm produce
You no say wetin we dey depend on pass na local manure from awa domestic cattle
But now , we no fit carry awa animal comot from home
Even for house , we dey get sleepless night to protect dem so dem no go steal dem
We dey helpless for di hand of di rustlers
dem dey sell zobo for Dankama , Mashi and Maia adua market for di state
Di current market price dey between 7 , 500 and N8 , 000 per bag
E dey expected ro reach N20 , 000 before di beginnin of next season
Di major producer of di crop for Nigeria na dem Katsina , Kano , Bauchi , Borno , Gombe and Jigawa State
For 2017 di Nigerian Agricultural Quarantine Service NAQS disclose say di county generate $ 35million witin nine month for 2017 from zobo export
Lagos East Court of Appeal uphold Abiru victory
Di court of Appeal don dismiss di appeal wey di candidate of di People's Democratic parti PDP don file for December 5 lagos East Senatorial by election , Babatunde Olalere Gbadamosi
Di judge wey dey preside , Justice Daniel Kallio dismiss di prayers of di pesin wey dey appell wey wan upturn di victory of di All Progressives Congress ( APC ) candidate , Senator Mukhail Adetokunbo Abiru , bikos dey no get merit .
For di rulin wey dey hear virtually , the court said PDP and its candidate dem appeal no get merit .
E later affirm di judgment of di Federal High Court , Lagos .
As dem use dismiss di appeal , di Court of Appeal tok say di residency of candidate to election no bequalifyin or disqualifyin factor .
holocaust wey we no fit forget
derfore , I tok ( Jesus ) to una ( Jew ) , di kingdom of God na hin dem go collect from you , and dem go give am to nation wey dey bring forth di fruit
